class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">x &gt;&gt; n</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6caa42a8eebe44e08c56b89db34b7672"><span data-offset-key="6caa42a8eebe44e08c56b89db34b7672:0"><em>x</em></span><span data-offset-key="6caa42a8eebe44e08c56b89db34b7672:1"> shifted right by </span><span data-offset-key="6caa42a8eebe44e08c56b89db34b7672:2"><em>n</em></span><span data-offset-key="6caa42a8eebe44e08c56b89db34b7672:3"> bits</span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b8bf12724c42405ea3a8c77c9f135f72"><span data-offset-key="b8bf12724c42405ea3a8c77c9f135f72:0">(1)(3)</span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="518e9dfc66334a54b14b42966c989a86"><span data-offset-key="518e9dfc66334a54b14b42966c989a86:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">~x</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="dcd998699066474fb6b5a06086a69ca3"><span data-offset-key="dcd998699066474fb6b5a06086a69ca3:0">the bits of </span><span data-offset-key="dcd998699066474fb6b5a06086a69ca3:1"><em>x</em></span><span data-offset-key="dcd998699066474fb6b5a06086a69ca3:2"> inverted</span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c0b21c66c6424c0883700030414e8c65"><span data-offset-key="c0b21c66c6424c0883700030414e8c65:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span></span></p></td></tr></tbody></table>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4e749856b97a4d64a4f76be7d1b7ceeb"><span data-offset-key="4e749856b97a4d64a4f76be7d1b7ceeb:0">Notes:</span></span></span>

1.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="79786116d00e474cbb0cccd216e31cfb"><span data-offset-key="79786116d00e474cbb0cccd216e31cfb:0">Negative shift counts are illegal and cause a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#ValueError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="53351ccd1dad4a1aba3f7d43cf4248f2"><span data-offset-key="53351ccd1dad4a1aba3f7d43cf4248f2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">ValueError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="bd60c8470f8446748e0744935a390f03"><span data-offset-key="bd60c8470f8446748e0744935a390f03:0"> to be raised.</span></span></span>

2.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fe617ca823b4406c95d6608c966d1d87"><span data-offset-key="fe617ca823b4406c95d6608c966d1d87:0">A left shift by </span><span data-offset-key="fe617ca823b4406c95d6608c966d1d87:1">*n*</span><span data-offset-key="fe617ca823b4406c95d6608c966d1d87:2"> bits is equivalent to multiplication by </span><span data-offset-key="fe617ca823b4406c95d6608c966d1d87:3">`pow(2, n)`</span><span data-offset-key="fe617ca823b4406c95d6608c966d1d87:4">.</span></span></span>

3.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="53c864a6895b4793adfe9a4c1ba3b551"><span data-offset-key="53c864a6895b4793adfe9a4c1ba3b551:0">A right shift by </span><span data-offset-key="53c864a6895b4793adfe9a4c1ba3b551:1">*n*</span><span data-offset-key="53c864a6895b4793adfe9a4c1ba3b551:2"> bits is equivalent to floor division by </span><span data-offset-key="53c864a6895b4793adfe9a4c1ba3b551:3">`pow(2, n)`</span><span data-offset-key="53c864a6895b4793adfe9a4c1ba3b551:4">.</span></span></span>

4.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2bf7dc7d40554b7f8e49c3e8c6237257"><span data-offset-key="2bf7dc7d40554b7f8e49c3e8c6237257:0">Performing these calculations with at least one extra sign extension bit in a finite two’s complement representation (a working bit-width of </span><span data-offset-key="2bf7dc7d40554b7f8e49c3e8c6237257:1">`1 + max(x.bit_length(),                                             y.bit_length())`</span><span data-offset-key="2bf7dc7d40554b7f8e49c3e8c6237257:2"> or more) is sufficient to get the same result as if there were an infinite number of sign bits.</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5f4fbd92ad6c4e39ba6698aaa3110d6f"><span data-offset-key="5f4fbd92ad6c4e39ba6698aaa3110d6f:0">Additional Methods on Integer Types</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6014cd737e6d4c14a95f354cb6ba1bc2"><span data-offset-key="6014cd737e6d4c14a95f354cb6ba1bc2:0">The int type implements the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/numbers.html#numbers.Integral" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7ee36fcb7c21482791645d8235cc07da"><span data-offset-key="7ee36fcb7c21482791645d8235cc07da:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">numbers.Integral</code></span></span></a><span data-key="1c61e45b7805432caf0d34c4d4ad40cf"><span data-offset-key="1c61e45b7805432caf0d34c4d4ad40cf:0"> </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-abstract-base-class" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="abc8088356b54ee5ac9574962216fe9d"><span data-offset-key="abc8088356b54ee5ac9574962216fe9d:0">abstract base class</span></span></a><span data-key="783a8070be9749a283dbec9f728b28f7"><span data-offset-key="783a8070be9749a283dbec9f728b28f7:0">. In addition, it provides a few more methods:</span><span data-offset-key="783a8070be9749a283dbec9f728b28f7:1">`int.bit_length`</span><span data-offset-key="783a8070be9749a283dbec9f728b28f7:2">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="84a2c64ab3dd47e0962978a2643cff52"><span data-offset-key="84a2c64ab3dd47e0962978a2643cff52:0">Return the number of bits necessary to represent an integer in binary, excluding the sign and leading zeros:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> n = -37>>> bin(n)'-0b100101'>>> n.bit_length()6

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f7af800b617b437cbbc1f133d4d01045"><span data-offset-key="f7af800b617b437cbbc1f133d4d01045:0">More precisely, if </span><span data-offset-key="f7af800b617b437cbbc1f133d4d01045:1">`x`</span><span data-offset-key="f7af800b617b437cbbc1f133d4d01045:2"> is nonzero, then </span><span data-offset-key="f7af800b617b437cbbc1f133d4d01045:3">`x.bit_length()`</span><span data-offset-key="f7af800b617b437cbbc1f133d4d01045:4"> is the unique positive integer </span><span data-offset-key="f7af800b617b437cbbc1f133d4d01045:5">`k`</span><span data-offset-key="f7af800b617b437cbbc1f133d4d01045:6"> such that </span><span data-offset-key="f7af800b617b437cbbc1f133d4d01045:7">`2**(k-1) <= abs(x) < 2**k`</span><span data-offset-key="f7af800b617b437cbbc1f133d4d01045:8">. Equivalently, when </span><span data-offset-key="f7af800b617b437cbbc1f133d4d01045:9">`abs(x)`</span><span data-offset-key="f7af800b617b437cbbc1f133d4d01045:10"> is small enough to have a correctly rounded logarithm, then </span><span data-offset-key="f7af800b617b437cbbc1f133d4d01045:11">`k = 1 + int(log(abs(x), 2))`</span><span data-offset-key="f7af800b617b437cbbc1f133d4d01045:12">. If </span><span data-offset-key="f7af800b617b437cbbc1f133d4d01045:13">`x`</span><span data-offset-key="f7af800b617b437cbbc1f133d4d01045:14"> is zero, then </span><span data-offset-key="f7af800b617b437cbbc1f133d4d01045:15">`x.bit_length()`</span><span data-offset-key="f7af800b617b437cbbc1f133d4d01045:16"> returns </span><span data-offset-key="f7af800b617b437cbbc1f133d4d01045:17">`0`</span><span data-offset-key="f7af800b617b437cbbc1f133d4d01045:18">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="86662fb4260f4fabbe83511a657b8e40"><span data-offset-key="86662fb4260f4fabbe83511a657b8e40:0">Equivalent to:</span></span></span>

    def bit_length(self):    s = bin(self)       # binary representation:  bin(-37) --> '-0b100101'    s = s.lstrip('-0b') # remove leading zeros and minus sign    return len(s)       # len('100101') --> 6

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="06f451dc7f09488ca2b717501bcf8046"><span data-offset-key="06f451dc7f09488ca2b717501bcf8046:0">New in version 3.1.</span><span data-offset-key="06f451dc7f09488ca2b717501bcf8046:1">`int.to_bytes`</span><span data-offset-key="06f451dc7f09488ca2b717501bcf8046:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="06f451dc7f09488ca2b717501bcf8046:3">*length*</span><span data-offset-key="06f451dc7f09488ca2b717501bcf8046:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="06f451dc7f09488ca2b717501bcf8046:5">*byteorder*</span><span data-offset-key="06f451dc7f09488ca2b717501bcf8046:6">, </span><span data-offset-key="06f451dc7f09488ca2b717501bcf8046:7">*\**</span><span data-offset-key="06f451dc7f09488ca2b717501bcf8046:8">, </span><span data-offset-key="06f451dc7f09488ca2b717501bcf8046:9">*signed=False*</span><span data-offset-key="06f451dc7f09488ca2b717501bcf8046:10">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1ae1c59d13d14a218eedd9b3cfa085a8"><span data-offset-key="1ae1c59d13d14a218eedd9b3cfa085a8:0">Return an array of bytes representing an integer.&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> (1024).to_bytes(2, byteorder='big')b'\x04\x00'>>> (1024).to_bytes(10, byteorder='big')b'\x00\x00\x00\x00\x00\x00\x00\x00\x04\x00'>>> (-1024).to_bytes(10, byteorder='big', signed=True)b'\xff\xff\xff\xff\xff\xff\xff\xff\xfc\x00'>>> x = 1000>>> x.to_bytes((x.bit_length() + 7) // 8, byteorder='little')b'\xe8\x03'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="42b8adf96eb040a8b5f357da4f07bc40"><span data-offset-key="42b8adf96eb040a8b5f357da4f07bc40:0">The integer is represented using </span><span data-offset-key="42b8adf96eb040a8b5f357da4f07bc40:1">*length*</span><span data-offset-key="42b8adf96eb040a8b5f357da4f07bc40:2"> bytes. An </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#OverflowError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5642a212c55c419682f6eed70c1ca11c"><span data-offset-key="5642a212c55c419682f6eed70c1ca11c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">OverflowError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="71d79d791942486cbe91ef9121c4903e"><span data-offset-key="71d79d791942486cbe91ef9121c4903e:0"> is raised if the integer is not representable with the given number of bytes.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="23ae16e5ef754546b7fb69637acc8186"><span data-offset-key="23ae16e5ef754546b7fb69637acc8186:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="23ae16e5ef754546b7fb69637acc8186:1">*byteorder*</span><span data-offset-key="23ae16e5ef754546b7fb69637acc8186:2"> argument determines the byte order used to represent the integer. If </span><span data-offset-key="23ae16e5ef754546b7fb69637acc8186:3">*byteorder*</span><span data-offset-key="23ae16e5ef754546b7fb69637acc8186:4"> is </span><span data-offset-key="23ae16e5ef754546b7fb69637acc8186:5">`"big"`</span><span data-offset-key="23ae16e5ef754546b7fb69637acc8186:6">, the most significant byte is at the beginning of the byte array. If </span><span data-offset-key="23ae16e5ef754546b7fb69637acc8186:7">*byteorder*</span><span data-offset-key="23ae16e5ef754546b7fb69637acc8186:8"> is </span><span data-offset-key="23ae16e5ef754546b7fb69637acc8186:9">`"little"`</span><span data-offset-key="23ae16e5ef754546b7fb69637acc8186:10">, the most significant byte is at the end of the byte array. To request the native byte order of the host system, use </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.byteorder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3993a26a697642b39c9e3c409a72c0a7"><span data-offset-key="3993a26a697642b39c9e3c409a72c0a7:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.byteorder</code></span></span></a><span data-key="3622759080c740419a3f34c8676b0e22"><span data-offset-key="3622759080c740419a3f34c8676b0e22:0"> as the byte order value.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d3d3dab7611840fe8e664dc6847deede"><span data-offset-key="d3d3dab7611840fe8e664dc6847deede:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="d3d3dab7611840fe8e664dc6847deede:1">*signed*</span><span data-offset-key="d3d3dab7611840fe8e664dc6847deede:2"> argument determines whether two’s complement is used to represent the integer. If </span><span data-offset-key="d3d3dab7611840fe8e664dc6847deede:3">*signed*</span><span data-offset-key="d3d3dab7611840fe8e664dc6847deede:4"> is </span><span data-offset-key="d3d3dab7611840fe8e664dc6847deede:5">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="d3d3dab7611840fe8e664dc6847deede:6"> and a negative integer is given, an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#OverflowError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="fbc3a3236a014d879b56e43e5be364f2"><span data-offset-key="fbc3a3236a014d879b56e43e5be364f2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">OverflowError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="eec564c39b28448bae838c865bc12e80"><span data-offset-key="eec564c39b28448bae838c865bc12e80:0"> is raised. The default value for </span><span data-offset-key="eec564c39b28448bae838c865bc12e80:1">*signed*</span><span data-offset-key="eec564c39b28448bae838c865bc12e80:2"> is </span><span data-offset-key="eec564c39b28448bae838c865bc12e80:3">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="eec564c39b28448bae838c865bc12e80:4">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e197cfb04c224c459b0dfa428fe8257a"><span data-offset-key="e197cfb04c224c459b0dfa428fe8257a:0">New in version 3.2.</span><span data-offset-key="e197cfb04c224c459b0dfa428fe8257a:1">*classmethod* </span><span data-offset-key="e197cfb04c224c459b0dfa428fe8257a:2">`int.from_bytes`</span><span data-offset-key="e197cfb04c224c459b0dfa428fe8257a:3">(</span><span data-offset-key="e197cfb04c224c459b0dfa428fe8257a:4">*bytes*</span><span data-offset-key="e197cfb04c224c459b0dfa428fe8257a:5">, </span><span data-offset-key="e197cfb04c224c459b0dfa428fe8257a:6">*byteorder*</span><span data-offset-key="e197cfb04c224c459b0dfa428fe8257a:7">, </span><span data-offset-key="e197cfb04c224c459b0dfa428fe8257a:8">*\**</span><span data-offset-key="e197cfb04c224c459b0dfa428fe8257a:9">, </span><span data-offset-key="e197cfb04c224c459b0dfa428fe8257a:10">*signed=False*</span><span data-offset-key="e197cfb04c224c459b0dfa428fe8257a:11">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="07780dfcaec04c8fa05ee3ceb82c364a"><span data-offset-key="07780dfcaec04c8fa05ee3ceb82c364a:0">Return the integer represented by the given array of bytes.&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> int.from_bytes(b'\x00\x10', byteorder='big')16>>> int.from_bytes(b'\x00\x10', byteorder='little')4096>>> int.from_bytes(b'\xfc\x00', byteorder='big', signed=True)-1024>>> int.from_bytes(b'\xfc\x00', byteorder='big', signed=False)64512>>> int.from_bytes([255, 0, 0], byteorder='big')16711680

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2d3fe46123a44623a0a1ba62fd2eb98d"><span data-offset-key="2d3fe46123a44623a0a1ba62fd2eb98d:0">The argument </span><span data-offset-key="2d3fe46123a44623a0a1ba62fd2eb98d:1">*bytes*</span><span data-offset-key="2d3fe46123a44623a0a1ba62fd2eb98d:2"> must either be a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-bytes-like-object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="38a7bc30ef284cd0b6419d1945bb8c63"><span data-offset-key="38a7bc30ef284cd0b6419d1945bb8c63:0">bytes-like object</span></span></a><span data-key="685d14804f1f4d28831063e6cd176fed"><span data-offset-key="685d14804f1f4d28831063e6cd176fed:0"> or an iterable producing bytes.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9c6d490ff8984112b4be3f05173e4f05"><span data-offset-key="9c6d490ff8984112b4be3f05173e4f05:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="9c6d490ff8984112b4be3f05173e4f05:1">*byteorder*</span><span data-offset-key="9c6d490ff8984112b4be3f05173e4f05:2"> argument determines the byte order used to represent the integer. If </span><span data-offset-key="9c6d490ff8984112b4be3f05173e4f05:3">*byteorder*</span><span data-offset-key="9c6d490ff8984112b4be3f05173e4f05:4"> is </span><span data-offset-key="9c6d490ff8984112b4be3f05173e4f05:5">`"big"`</span><span data-offset-key="9c6d490ff8984112b4be3f05173e4f05:6">, the most significant byte is at the beginning of the byte array. If </span><span data-offset-key="9c6d490ff8984112b4be3f05173e4f05:7">*byteorder*</span><span data-offset-key="9c6d490ff8984112b4be3f05173e4f05:8"> is </span><span data-offset-key="9c6d490ff8984112b4be3f05173e4f05:9">`"little"`</span><span data-offset-key="9c6d490ff8984112b4be3f05173e4f05:10">, the most significant byte is at the end of the byte array. To request the native byte order of the host system, use </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.byteorder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f6483604b0fa45858c2b1cb65692795a"><span data-offset-key="f6483604b0fa45858c2b1cb65692795a:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.byteorder</code></span></span></a><span data-key="7a986a6500304a8cbfa38ca37fd96f1d"><span data-offset-key="7a986a6500304a8cbfa38ca37fd96f1d:0"> as the byte order value.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="cd8844b44e114f98ac93ecf4825627c6"><span data-offset-key="cd8844b44e114f98ac93ecf4825627c6:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="cd8844b44e114f98ac93ecf4825627c6:1">*signed*</span><span data-offset-key="cd8844b44e114f98ac93ecf4825627c6:2"> argument indicates whether two’s complement is used to represent the integer.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6387048cac764f04b3b2382c66c965a9"><span data-offset-key="6387048cac764f04b3b2382c66c965a9:0">New in version 3.2.</span><span data-offset-key="6387048cac764f04b3b2382c66c965a9:1">`int.as_integer_ratio`</span><span data-offset-key="6387048cac764f04b3b2382c66c965a9:2">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0600983b7d104a4faccac0195b34a2fa"><span data-offset-key="0600983b7d104a4faccac0195b34a2fa:0">Return a pair of integers whose ratio is exactly equal to the original integer and with a positive denominator. The integer ratio of integers (whole numbers) is always the integer as the numerator and </span><span data-offset-key="0600983b7d104a4faccac0195b34a2fa:1">`1`</span><span data-offset-key="0600983b7d104a4faccac0195b34a2fa:2"> as the denominator.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6805cc2ab0224c7eb8142d45f83b8fba"><span data-offset-key="6805cc2ab0224c7eb8142d45f83b8fba:0">New in version 3.8.</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f2e0d466372547e5b610d5d679f8efb5"><span data-offset-key="f2e0d466372547e5b610d5d679f8efb5:0">Additional Methods on Float</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="db19c65b0e7843b4a0ddcdc97a389c43"><span data-offset-key="db19c65b0e7843b4a0ddcdc97a389c43:0">The float type implements the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/numbers.html#numbers.Real" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4de443a2e69a485ebd24cd672f8d9a92"><span data-offset-key="4de443a2e69a485ebd24cd672f8d9a92:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">numbers.Real</code></span></span></a><span data-key="76741f4a1b8b48e2aa2688c4d1e78677"><span data-offset-key="76741f4a1b8b48e2aa2688c4d1e78677:0"> </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-abstract-base-class" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7db3cd7d1b284dc5871168044c79954a"><span data-offset-key="7db3cd7d1b284dc5871168044c79954a:0">abstract base class</span></span></a><span data-key="11dc8f97bb33482a8d2e8bd96ae6f325"><span data-offset-key="11dc8f97bb33482a8d2e8bd96ae6f325:0">. float also has the following additional methods.</span><span data-offset-key="11dc8f97bb33482a8d2e8bd96ae6f325:1">`float.as_integer_ratio`</span><span data-offset-key="11dc8f97bb33482a8d2e8bd96ae6f325:2">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b0e48fcb8a8e4160a420c43ccb671f98"><span data-offset-key="b0e48fcb8a8e4160a420c43ccb671f98:0">Return a pair of integers whose ratio is exactly equal to the original float and with a positive denominator. Raises </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#OverflowError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3133d255a4324f838861dcb2c6e5ca59"><span data-offset-key="3133d255a4324f838861dcb2c6e5ca59:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">OverflowError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f69eb8183e4e4482b5fe18f135bed323"><span data-offset-key="f69eb8183e4e4482b5fe18f135bed323:0"> on infinities and a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#ValueError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4f913b5835d34472a6224e4fab3859e2"><span data-offset-key="4f913b5835d34472a6224e4fab3859e2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">ValueError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="273c33a7247f4e3285069dff470d7cfa"><span data-offset-key="273c33a7247f4e3285069dff470d7cfa:0"> on NaNs.</span><span data-offset-key="273c33a7247f4e3285069dff470d7cfa:1">`float.is_integer`</span><span data-offset-key="273c33a7247f4e3285069dff470d7cfa:2">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f72f7f82af4b4f659524fbebc1b5374a"><span data-offset-key="f72f7f82af4b4f659524fbebc1b5374a:0">Return </span><span data-offset-key="f72f7f82af4b4f659524fbebc1b5374a:1">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="f72f7f82af4b4f659524fbebc1b5374a:2"> if the float instance is finite with integral value, and </span><span data-offset-key="f72f7f82af4b4f659524fbebc1b5374a:3">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="f72f7f82af4b4f659524fbebc1b5374a:4"> otherwise:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> (-2.0).is_integer()True>>> (3.2).is_integer()False

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c74a9732485649a39874379cc1d9e110"><span data-offset-key="c74a9732485649a39874379cc1d9e110:0">Two methods support conversion to and from hexadecimal strings. Since Python’s floats are stored internally as binary numbers, converting a float to or from a </span><span data-offset-key="c74a9732485649a39874379cc1d9e110:1">*decimal*</span><span data-offset-key="c74a9732485649a39874379cc1d9e110:2"> string usually involves a small rounding error. In contrast, hexadecimal strings allow exact representation and specification of floating-point numbers. This can be useful when debugging, and in numerical work.</span><span data-offset-key="c74a9732485649a39874379cc1d9e110:3">`float.hex`</span><span data-offset-key="c74a9732485649a39874379cc1d9e110:4">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="590092dedf1a40a3be4f8ee1b56efc5a"><span data-offset-key="590092dedf1a40a3be4f8ee1b56efc5a:0">Return a representation of a floating-point number as a hexadecimal string. For finite floating-point numbers, this representation will always include a leading </span><span data-offset-key="590092dedf1a40a3be4f8ee1b56efc5a:1">`0x`</span><span data-offset-key="590092dedf1a40a3be4f8ee1b56efc5a:2"> and a trailing </span><span data-offset-key="590092dedf1a40a3be4f8ee1b56efc5a:3">`p`</span><span data-offset-key="590092dedf1a40a3be4f8ee1b56efc5a:4"> and exponent.</span><span data-offset-key="590092dedf1a40a3be4f8ee1b56efc5a:5">*classmethod* </span><span data-offset-key="590092dedf1a40a3be4f8ee1b56efc5a:6">`float.fromhex`</span><span data-offset-key="590092dedf1a40a3be4f8ee1b56efc5a:7">(</span><span data-offset-key="590092dedf1a40a3be4f8ee1b56efc5a:8">*s*</span><span data-offset-key="590092dedf1a40a3be4f8ee1b56efc5a:9">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="800a34c09c0444c9ac5665c02f36ab08"><span data-offset-key="800a34c09c0444c9ac5665c02f36ab08:0">Class method to return the float represented by a hexadecimal string </span><span data-offset-key="800a34c09c0444c9ac5665c02f36ab08:1">*s*</span><span data-offset-key="800a34c09c0444c9ac5665c02f36ab08:2">. The string </span><span data-offset-key="800a34c09c0444c9ac5665c02f36ab08:3">*s*</span><span data-offset-key="800a34c09c0444c9ac5665c02f36ab08:4"> may have leading and trailing whitespace.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3de67e99b74a47c7a075c120cc72e4de"><span data-offset-key="3de67e99b74a47c7a075c120cc72e4de:0">Note that </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#float.hex" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="cd30d447565d4ae6a43cd2f7c9b3d44a"><span data-offset-key="cd30d447565d4ae6a43cd2f7c9b3d44a:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">float.hex()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f8ac07c549ea40fdaa330f4c20cea9b0"><span data-offset-key="f8ac07c549ea40fdaa330f4c20cea9b0:0"> is an instance method, while </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#float.fromhex" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5a31c5b07b8c409cb27c90aa568bba2c"><span data-offset-key="5a31c5b07b8c409cb27c90aa568bba2c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">float.fromhex()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="2d7c1821028946138a12a37d2fb327c4"><span data-offset-key="2d7c1821028946138a12a37d2fb327c4:0"> is a class method.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2325b528fe364108bc3c60603cf88576"><span data-offset-key="2325b528fe364108bc3c60603cf88576:0">A hexadecimal string takes the form:</span></span></span>

    [sign] ['0x'] integer ['.' fraction] ['p' exponent]

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5234870c88d94893b659f626af086196"><span data-offset-key="5234870c88d94893b659f626af086196:0">where the optional </span><span data-offset-key="5234870c88d94893b659f626af086196:1">`sign`</span><span data-offset-key="5234870c88d94893b659f626af086196:2"> may by either </span><span data-offset-key="5234870c88d94893b659f626af086196:3">`+`</span><span data-offset-key="5234870c88d94893b659f626af086196:4"> or </span><span data-offset-key="5234870c88d94893b659f626af086196:5">`-`</span><span data-offset-key="5234870c88d94893b659f626af086196:6">, </span><span data-offset-key="5234870c88d94893b659f626af086196:7">`integer`</span><span data-offset-key="5234870c88d94893b659f626af086196:8"> and </span><span data-offset-key="5234870c88d94893b659f626af086196:9">`fraction`</span><span data-offset-key="5234870c88d94893b659f626af086196:10"> are strings of hexadecimal digits, and </span><span data-offset-key="5234870c88d94893b659f626af086196:11">`exponent`</span><span data-offset-key="5234870c88d94893b659f626af086196:12"> is a decimal integer with an optional leading sign. Case is not significant, and there must be at least one hexadecimal digit in either the integer or the fraction. This syntax is similar to the syntax specified in section 6.4.4.2 of the C99 standard, and also to the syntax used in Java 1.5 onwards. In particular, the output of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#float.hex" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9244480777cc4a93a5609e2f04e06593"><span data-offset-key="9244480777cc4a93a5609e2f04e06593:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">float.hex()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f95da5f3807a4fa787e9a0592d84882e"><span data-offset-key="f95da5f3807a4fa787e9a0592d84882e:0"> is usable as a hexadecimal floating-point literal in C or Java code, and hexadecimal strings produced by C’s </span><span data-offset-key="f95da5f3807a4fa787e9a0592d84882e:1">`%a`</span><span data-offset-key="f95da5f3807a4fa787e9a0592d84882e:2"> format character or Java’s </span><span data-offset-key="f95da5f3807a4fa787e9a0592d84882e:3">`Double.toHexString`</span><span data-offset-key="f95da5f3807a4fa787e9a0592d84882e:4"> are accepted by </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#float.fromhex" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6a4beb2b060842fba0ce94d31357bf78"><span data-offset-key="6a4beb2b060842fba0ce94d31357bf78:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">float.fromhex()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="8f98e7570c014150a0abbc091b9ea628"><span data-offset-key="8f98e7570c014150a0abbc091b9ea628:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="92fd85e18d8a45918749f90d567b92be"><span data-offset-key="92fd85e18d8a45918749f90d567b92be:0">Note that the exponent is written in decimal rather than hexadecimal, and that it gives the power of 2 by which to multiply the coefficient. For example, the hexadecimal string </span><span data-offset-key="92fd85e18d8a45918749f90d567b92be:1">`0x3.a7p10`</span><span data-offset-key="92fd85e18d8a45918749f90d567b92be:2"> represents the floating-point number </span><span data-offset-key="92fd85e18d8a45918749f90d567b92be:3">`(3 + 10./16 + 7./16**2) * 2.0**10`</span><span data-offset-key="92fd85e18d8a45918749f90d567b92be:4">, or </span><span data-offset-key="92fd85e18d8a45918749f90d567b92be:5">`3740.0`</span><span data-offset-key="92fd85e18d8a45918749f90d567b92be:6">:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> float.fromhex('0x3.a7p10')3740.0

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="46df49198bfa4a6a982b84cb4d8e01c0"><span data-offset-key="46df49198bfa4a6a982b84cb4d8e01c0:0">Applying the reverse conversion to </span><span data-offset-key="46df49198bfa4a6a982b84cb4d8e01c0:1">`3740.0`</span><span data-offset-key="46df49198bfa4a6a982b84cb4d8e01c0:2"> gives a different hexadecimal string representing the same number:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> float.hex(3740.0)'0x1.d380000000000p+11'

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a7a05812a63b4a06995833d2fd38939b"><span data-offset-key="a7a05812a63b4a06995833d2fd38939b:0">Hashing of numeric types</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8dc963d93a7349c6bbad40eefd67fdaa"><span data-offset-key="8dc963d93a7349c6bbad40eefd67fdaa:0">For numbers </span><span data-offset-key="8dc963d93a7349c6bbad40eefd67fdaa:1">`x`</span><span data-offset-key="8dc963d93a7349c6bbad40eefd67fdaa:2"> and </span><span data-offset-key="8dc963d93a7349c6bbad40eefd67fdaa:3">`y`</span><span data-offset-key="8dc963d93a7349c6bbad40eefd67fdaa:4">, possibly of different types, it’s a requirement that </span><span data-offset-key="8dc963d93a7349c6bbad40eefd67fdaa:5">`hash(x) == hash(y)`</span><span data-offset-key="8dc963d93a7349c6bbad40eefd67fdaa:6"> whenever </span><span data-offset-key="8dc963d93a7349c6bbad40eefd67fdaa:7">`x == y`</span><span data-offset-key="8dc963d93a7349c6bbad40eefd67fdaa:8"> (see the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__hash__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="523bb45c2e874868870e58747ca75149"><span data-offset-key="523bb45c2e874868870e58747ca75149:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__hash__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="4eca347ccd984c85b53b6f48eb3d3c61"><span data-offset-key="4eca347ccd984c85b53b6f48eb3d3c61:0"> method documentation for more details). For ease of implementation and efficiency across a variety of numeric types (including </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9efca8c0076340e2ab5de97ca4a9bb06"><span data-offset-key="9efca8c0076340e2ab5de97ca4a9bb06:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">int</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f8c8cab7075b40f3829c59fa616d8f30"><span data-offset-key="f8c8cab7075b40f3829c59fa616d8f30:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#float" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="55d9d877ec8a44959143a19d2616ba06"><span data-offset-key="55d9d877ec8a44959143a19d2616ba06:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">float</code></span></span></a><span data-key="af30295a63c94695a7e3918c7ad8ffb2"><span data-offset-key="af30295a63c94695a7e3918c7ad8ffb2:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/decimal.html#decimal.Decimal" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0f9574ecdef14da3906ce3be405fb499"><span data-offset-key="0f9574ecdef14da3906ce3be405fb499:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">decimal.Decimal</code></span></span></a><span data-key="3440bdb8b27b46ac91695078175be0e0"><span data-offset-key="3440bdb8b27b46ac91695078175be0e0:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/fractions.html#fractions.Fraction" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d81fc75a472043ca986114971dad89f5"><span data-offset-key="d81fc75a472043ca986114971dad89f5:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">fractions.Fraction</code></span></span></a><span data-key="8596f5d501af4cd5baaf4662149bcac8"><span data-offset-key="8596f5d501af4cd5baaf4662149bcac8:0">) Python’s hash for numeric types is based on a single mathematical function that’s defined for any rational number, and hence applies to all instances of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4a46e92e2cdd4068b8ff76c03461b79a"><span data-offset-key="4a46e92e2cdd4068b8ff76c03461b79a:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">int</code></span></span></a><span data-key="6ca03773cb7e400f8de4610f790a1d0c"><span data-offset-key="6ca03773cb7e400f8de4610f790a1d0c:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/fractions.html#fractions.Fraction" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f71429267add43a78c3e2f84a8bb3596"><span data-offset-key="f71429267add43a78c3e2f84a8bb3596:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">fractions.Fraction</code></span></span></a><span data-key="36301b39458f41ddbfb9444203ed406c"><span data-offset-key="36301b39458f41ddbfb9444203ed406c:0">, and all finite instances of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#float" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="930f99b6810b4dcab921310da3560f7f"><span data-offset-key="930f99b6810b4dcab921310da3560f7f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">float</code></span></span></a><span data-key="62662edca052475a99c3ccb85b8f56ff"><span data-offset-key="62662edca052475a99c3ccb85b8f56ff:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/decimal.html#decimal.Decimal" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7c9131a6624f42baa097e32dd3642952"><span data-offset-key="7c9131a6624f42baa097e32dd3642952:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">decimal.Decimal</code></span></span></a><span data-key="bbf138378f9048ed8be339159f624968"><span data-offset-key="bbf138378f9048ed8be339159f624968:0">. Essentially, this function is given by reduction modulo </span><span data-offset-key="bbf138378f9048ed8be339159f624968:1">`P`</span><span data-offset-key="bbf138378f9048ed8be339159f624968:2"> for a fixed prime </span><span data-offset-key="bbf138378f9048ed8be339159f624968:3">`P`</span><span data-offset-key="bbf138378f9048ed8be339159f624968:4">. The value of </span><span data-offset-key="bbf138378f9048ed8be339159f624968:5">`P`</span><span data-offset-key="bbf138378f9048ed8be339159f624968:6"> is made available to Python as the </span><span data-offset-key="bbf138378f9048ed8be339159f624968:7">`modulus`</span><span data-offset-key="bbf138378f9048ed8be339159f624968:8"> attribute of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.hash_info" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b6345de9ebba47cb8ac796c68b6d2bf8"><span data-offset-key="b6345de9ebba47cb8ac796c68b6d2bf8:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.hash_info</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a4b74314639149c6b820277231fe6b0c"><span data-offset-key="a4b74314639149c6b820277231fe6b0c:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0737776c2bec475096b1a8f38c6ef53a"><span data-offset-key="0737776c2bec475096b1a8f38c6ef53a:0">**CPython implementation detail:**</span><span data-offset-key="0737776c2bec475096b1a8f38c6ef53a:1"> Currently, the prime used is </span><span data-offset-key="0737776c2bec475096b1a8f38c6ef53a:2">`P = 2**31 - 1`</span><span data-offset-key="0737776c2bec475096b1a8f38c6ef53a:3"> on machines with 32-bit C longs and </span><span data-offset-key="0737776c2bec475096b1a8f38c6ef53a:4">`P = 2**61 - 1`</span><span data-offset-key="0737776c2bec475096b1a8f38c6ef53a:5"> on machines with 64-bit C longs.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fa3d052fa0fa42d8991ca18f351afeb9"><span data-offset-key="fa3d052fa0fa42d8991ca18f351afeb9:0">Here are the rules in detail:</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="882a2dca7e674d89ab27ae676b9ce51f"><span data-offset-key="882a2dca7e674d89ab27ae676b9ce51f:0">If </span><span data-offset-key="882a2dca7e674d89ab27ae676b9ce51f:1">`x = m / n`</span><span data-offset-key="882a2dca7e674d89ab27ae676b9ce51f:2"> is a nonnegative rational number and </span><span data-offset-key="882a2dca7e674d89ab27ae676b9ce51f:3">`n`</span><span data-offset-key="882a2dca7e674d89ab27ae676b9ce51f:4"> is not divisible by </span><span data-offset-key="882a2dca7e674d89ab27ae676b9ce51f:5">`P`</span><span data-offset-key="882a2dca7e674d89ab27ae676b9ce51f:6">, define </span><span data-offset-key="882a2dca7e674d89ab27ae676b9ce51f:7">`hash(x)`</span><span data-offset-key="882a2dca7e674d89ab27ae676b9ce51f:8"> as </span><span data-offset-key="882a2dca7e674d89ab27ae676b9ce51f:9">`m * invmod(n, P) % P`</span><span data-offset-key="882a2dca7e674d89ab27ae676b9ce51f:10">, where </span><span data-offset-key="882a2dca7e674d89ab27ae676b9ce51f:11">`invmod(n, P)`</span><span data-offset-key="882a2dca7e674d89ab27ae676b9ce51f:12"> gives the inverse of </span><span data-offset-key="882a2dca7e674d89ab27ae676b9ce51f:13">`n`</span><span data-offset-key="882a2dca7e674d89ab27ae676b9ce51f:14"> modulo </span><span data-offset-key="882a2dca7e674d89ab27ae676b9ce51f:15">`P`</span><span data-offset-key="882a2dca7e674d89ab27ae676b9ce51f:16">.</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fbb115d5f2f54a249c130a0153f47591"><span data-offset-key="fbb115d5f2f54a249c130a0153f47591:0">If </span><span data-offset-key="fbb115d5f2f54a249c130a0153f47591:1">`x = m / n`</span><span data-offset-key="fbb115d5f2f54a249c130a0153f47591:2"> is a nonnegative rational number and </span><span data-offset-key="fbb115d5f2f54a249c130a0153f47591:3">`n`</span><span data-offset-key="fbb115d5f2f54a249c130a0153f47591:4"> is divisible by </span><span data-offset-key="fbb115d5f2f54a249c130a0153f47591:5">`P`</span><span data-offset-key="fbb115d5f2f54a249c130a0153f47591:6"> (but </span><span data-offset-key="fbb115d5f2f54a249c130a0153f47591:7">`m`</span><span data-offset-key="fbb115d5f2f54a249c130a0153f47591:8"> is not) then </span><span data-offset-key="fbb115d5f2f54a249c130a0153f47591:9">`n`</span><span data-offset-key="fbb115d5f2f54a249c130a0153f47591:10"> has no inverse modulo </span><span data-offset-key="fbb115d5f2f54a249c130a0153f47591:11">`P`</span><span data-offset-key="fbb115d5f2f54a249c130a0153f47591:12"> and the rule above doesn’t apply; in this case define </span><span data-offset-key="fbb115d5f2f54a249c130a0153f47591:13">`hash(x)`</span><span data-offset-key="fbb115d5f2f54a249c130a0153f47591:14"> to be the constant value </span><span data-offset-key="fbb115d5f2f54a249c130a0153f47591:15">`sys.hash_info.inf`</span><span data-offset-key="fbb115d5f2f54a249c130a0153f47591:16">.</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8786fd3acc214236b4ffbd947c391b47"><span data-offset-key="8786fd3acc214236b4ffbd947c391b47:0">If </span><span data-offset-key="8786fd3acc214236b4ffbd947c391b47:1">`x = m / n`</span><span data-offset-key="8786fd3acc214236b4ffbd947c391b47:2"> is a negative rational number define </span><span data-offset-key="8786fd3acc214236b4ffbd947c391b47:3">`hash(x)`</span><span data-offset-key="8786fd3acc214236b4ffbd947c391b47:4"> as </span><span data-offset-key="8786fd3acc214236b4ffbd947c391b47:5">`-hash(-x)`</span><span data-offset-key="8786fd3acc214236b4ffbd947c391b47:6">. If the resulting hash is </span><span data-offset-key="8786fd3acc214236b4ffbd947c391b47:7">`-1`</span><span data-offset-key="8786fd3acc214236b4ffbd947c391b47:8">, replace it with </span><span data-offset-key="8786fd3acc214236b4ffbd947c391b47:9">`-2`</span><span data-offset-key="8786fd3acc214236b4ffbd947c391b47:10">.</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1f20d6348a0d4a0f8cf6b55734ab6133"><span data-offset-key="1f20d6348a0d4a0f8cf6b55734ab6133:0">The particular values </span><span data-offset-key="1f20d6348a0d4a0f8cf6b55734ab6133:1">`sys.hash_info.inf`</span><span data-offset-key="1f20d6348a0d4a0f8cf6b55734ab6133:2">, </span><span data-offset-key="1f20d6348a0d4a0f8cf6b55734ab6133:3">`-sys.hash_info.inf`</span><span data-offset-key="1f20d6348a0d4a0f8cf6b55734ab6133:4"> and </span><span data-offset-key="1f20d6348a0d4a0f8cf6b55734ab6133:5">`sys.hash_info.nan`</span><span data-offset-key="1f20d6348a0d4a0f8cf6b55734ab6133:6"> are used as hash values for positive infinity, negative infinity, or nans (respectively). (All hashable nans have the same hash value.)</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5f4236e03f774ab5a8eb102897359311"><span data-offset-key="5f4236e03f774ab5a8eb102897359311:0">For a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#complex" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="aabd8e90056b4dacb91a52b057b6adfa"><span data-offset-key="aabd8e90056b4dacb91a52b057b6adfa:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">complex</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d44cd82860294277b3364c9efc7c0290"><span data-offset-key="d44cd82860294277b3364c9efc7c0290:0"> number </span><span data-offset-key="d44cd82860294277b3364c9efc7c0290:1">`z`</span><span data-offset-key="d44cd82860294277b3364c9efc7c0290:2">, the hash values of the real and imaginary parts are combined by computing </span><span data-offset-key="d44cd82860294277b3364c9efc7c0290:3">`hash(z.real) + sys.hash_info.imag *                                             hash(z.imag)`</span><span data-offset-key="d44cd82860294277b3364c9efc7c0290:4">, reduced modulo </span><span data-offset-key="d44cd82860294277b3364c9efc7c0290:5">`2**sys.hash_info.width`</span><span data-offset-key="d44cd82860294277b3364c9efc7c0290:6"> so that it lies in </span><span data-offset-key="d44cd82860294277b3364c9efc7c0290:7">`range(-2**(sys.hash_info.width -                                             1), 2**(sys.hash_info.width -                                             1))`</span><span data-offset-key="d44cd82860294277b3364c9efc7c0290:8">. Again, if the result is </span><span data-offset-key="d44cd82860294277b3364c9efc7c0290:9">`-1`</span><span data-offset-key="d44cd82860294277b3364c9efc7c0290:10">, it’s replaced with </span><span data-offset-key="d44cd82860294277b3364c9efc7c0290:11">`-2`</span><span data-offset-key="d44cd82860294277b3364c9efc7c0290:12">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="62c8a555c03241ae9c2b0b2174c1e0b6"><span data-offset-key="62c8a555c03241ae9c2b0b2174c1e0b6:0">To clarify the above rules, here’s some example Python code, equivalent to the built-in hash, for computing the hash of a rational number, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#float" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2320b58cd27a4fdc9542ec4a02ea30d5"><span data-offset-key="2320b58cd27a4fdc9542ec4a02ea30d5:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">float</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d8bbb9c07f0c4abe9f52701d52aec5a8"><span data-offset-key="d8bbb9c07f0c4abe9f52701d52aec5a8:0">, or </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#complex" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4bd9761d0983457fb72d7952275f59c1"><span data-offset-key="4bd9761d0983457fb72d7952275f59c1:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">complex</code></span></span></a><span data-key="9d34312cf41a40abaea369887b414414"><span data-offset-key="9d34312cf41a40abaea369887b414414:0">:</span></span></span>

    import sys, math​def hash_fraction(m, n):    """Compute the hash of a rational number m / n.​    Assumes m and n are integers, with n positive.    Equivalent to hash(fractions.Fraction(m, n)).​    """    P = sys.hash_info.modulus    # Remove common factors of P.  (Unnecessary if m and n already coprime.)    while m % P == n % P == 0:        m, n = m // P, n // P​    if n % P == 0:        hash_value = sys.hash_info.inf    else:        # Fermat's Little Theorem: pow(n, P-1, P) is 1, so        # pow(n, P-2, P) gives the inverse of n modulo P.        hash_value = (abs(m) % P) * pow(n, P - 2, P) % P    if m < 0:        hash_value = -hash_value    if hash_value == -1:        hash_value = -2    return hash_value​def hash_float(x):    """Compute the hash of a float x."""​    if math.isnan(x):        return sys.hash_info.nan    elif math.isinf(x):        return sys.hash_info.inf if x > 0 else -sys.hash_info.inf    else:        return hash_fraction(*x.as_integer_ratio())​def hash_complex(z):    """Compute the hash of a complex number z."""​    hash_value = hash_float(z.real) + sys.hash_info.imag * hash_float(z.imag)    # do a signed reduction modulo 2**sys.hash_info.width    M = 2**(sys.hash_info.width - 1)    hash_value = (hash_value & (M - 1)) - (hash_value & M)    if hash_value == -1:        hash_value = -2    return hash_value

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH600-23f228db--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7214d95e2a244b88878dfd6f3e7ce8b4"><span data-offset-key="7214d95e2a244b88878dfd6f3e7ce8b4:0">Iterator Types</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0702f0d3391a4215aea34b8b52113cf3"><span data-offset-key="0702f0d3391a4215aea34b8b52113cf3:0">Python supports a concept of iteration over containers. This is implemented using two distinct methods; these are used to allow user-defined classes to support iteration. Sequences, described below in more detail, always support the iteration methods.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="24107a8a49e545fc9e7b2336722fb808"><span data-offset-key="24107a8a49e545fc9e7b2336722fb808:0">One method needs to be defined for container objects to provide iteration support:</span><span data-offset-key="24107a8a49e545fc9e7b2336722fb808:1">`container.__iter__`</span><span data-offset-key="24107a8a49e545fc9e7b2336722fb808:2">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e642d3c6a999415db4a9205e72ad62b0"><span data-offset-key="e642d3c6a999415db4a9205e72ad62b0:0">Return an iterator object. The object is required to support the iterator protocol described below. If a container supports different types of iteration, additional methods can be provided to specifically request iterators for those iteration types. (An example of an object supporting multiple forms of iteration would be a tree structure which supports both breadth-first and depth-first traversal.) This method corresponds to the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/c-api/typeobj.html#c.PyTypeObject.tp_iter" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1d0ee578d961433ab7e939e5ba426690"><span data-offset-key="1d0ee578d961433ab7e939e5ba426690:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">tp_iter</code></span></span></a><span data-key="5a4f6f5c9c8d445b9f04a327515a39bf"><span data-offset-key="5a4f6f5c9c8d445b9f04a327515a39bf:0"> slot of the type structure for Python objects in the Python/C API.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="79fb7447e6c94d508a48a1ec3046e427"><span data-offset-key="79fb7447e6c94d508a48a1ec3046e427:0">The iterator objects themselves are required to support the following two methods, which together form the </span><span data-offset-key="79fb7447e6c94d508a48a1ec3046e427:1">*iterator protocol*</span><span data-offset-key="79fb7447e6c94d508a48a1ec3046e427:2">:</span><span data-offset-key="79fb7447e6c94d508a48a1ec3046e427:3">`iterator.__iter__`</span><span data-offset-key="79fb7447e6c94d508a48a1ec3046e427:4">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2485ffe567cb4598a53def98b8d8ad49"><span data-offset-key="2485ffe567cb4598a53def98b8d8ad49:0">Return the iterator object itself. This is required to allow both containers and iterators to be used with the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/compound_stmts.html#for" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="311e9a9ddf874d389fce911d27a63400"><span data-offset-key="311e9a9ddf874d389fce911d27a63400:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">for</code></span></span></a><span data-key="8d70aa0317bf410d9207ea020946d938"><span data-offset-key="8d70aa0317bf410d9207ea020946d938:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/expressions.html#in" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="03bbd162e077421ebd15a3c186f58326"><span data-offset-key="03bbd162e077421ebd15a3c186f58326:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">in</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ea9bfe1d108c4da194f68015fbc575ba"><span data-offset-key="ea9bfe1d108c4da194f68015fbc575ba:0"> statements. This method corresponds to the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/c-api/typeobj.html#c.PyTypeObject.tp_iter" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8cc0255b1f814efe90ff76e387e00c97"><span data-offset-key="8cc0255b1f814efe90ff76e387e00c97:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">tp_iter</code></span></span></a><span data-key="3c178c7c7dcb4692ae07c87c137d164e"><span data-offset-key="3c178c7c7dcb4692ae07c87c137d164e:0"> slot of the type structure for Python objects in the Python/C API.</span><span data-offset-key="3c178c7c7dcb4692ae07c87c137d164e:1">`iterator.__next__`</span><span data-offset-key="3c178c7c7dcb4692ae07c87c137d164e:2">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9ef8b876968f416abff3c51d7a302d7a"><span data-offset-key="9ef8b876968f416abff3c51d7a302d7a:0">Return the next item from the container. If there are no further items, raise the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#StopIteration" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1c69b7409ba3435ba25b4a42c50f1cb5"><span data-offset-key="1c69b7409ba3435ba25b4a42c50f1cb5:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">StopIteration</code></span></span></a><span data-key="39d2cbf937b84e57808d0ac12d14a2f5"><span data-offset-key="39d2cbf937b84e57808d0ac12d14a2f5:0"> exception. This method corresponds to the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/c-api/typeobj.html#c.PyTypeObject.tp_iternext" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5dbb6e3c50aa4a488582dea8764cda0f"><span data-offset-key="5dbb6e3c50aa4a488582dea8764cda0f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">tp_iternext</code></span></span></a><span data-key="8ca9a50060b74825aa5e658012bee542"><span data-offset-key="8ca9a50060b74825aa5e658012bee542:0"> slot of the type structure for Python objects in the Python/C API.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c821c3a92ff14af2b0fbce31acf55ba8"><span data-offset-key="c821c3a92ff14af2b0fbce31acf55ba8:0">Python defines several iterator objects to support iteration over general and specific sequence types, dictionaries, and other more specialized forms. The specific types are not important beyond their implementation of the iterator protocol.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3841e050da2d4ad69e808086e4b13867"><span data-offset-key="3841e050da2d4ad69e808086e4b13867:0">Once an iterator’s </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#iterator.__next__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="eaa89f4783004b968f0e760ec2b7cc62"><span data-offset-key="eaa89f4783004b968f0e760ec2b7cc62:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__next__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a77bc0b625634b7a80cd812b48400710"><span data-offset-key="a77bc0b625634b7a80cd812b48400710:0"> method raises </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#StopIteration" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="33864915159f40d8bd395a7ebb68dea7"><span data-offset-key="33864915159f40d8bd395a7ebb68dea7:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">StopIteration</code></span></span></a><span data-key="53570082d9ab42d6b2ef8b5577e37f67"><span data-offset-key="53570082d9ab42d6b2ef8b5577e37f67:0">, it must continue to do so on subsequent calls. Implementations that do not obey this property are deemed broken.</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7a012379ad494fd79a4a9cccb202e433"><span data-offset-key="7a012379ad494fd79a4a9cccb202e433:0">Generator Types</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c4ebc330a3f74abcb1a25fc7779a0875"><span data-offset-key="c4ebc330a3f74abcb1a25fc7779a0875:0">Python’s </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-generator" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b449aac4fcd742c29cf2cf7763bc3825"><span data-offset-key="b449aac4fcd742c29cf2cf7763bc3825:0">generator</span></span></a><span data-key="9732aa768d0e4d9db5752f032822c3a9"><span data-offset-key="9732aa768d0e4d9db5752f032822c3a9:0">s provide a convenient way to implement the iterator protocol. If a container object’s </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__iter__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c5c6a2d75b7246bc909f651d0f5012c7"><span data-offset-key="c5c6a2d75b7246bc909f651d0f5012c7:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__iter__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="5cd17f7181884a59a2df39c5aad9b95c"><span data-offset-key="5cd17f7181884a59a2df39c5aad9b95c:0"> method is implemented as a generator, it will automatically return an iterator object (technically, a generator object) supplying the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__iter__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e604ded7e14e4069a8495f046ff17137"><span data-offset-key="e604ded7e14e4069a8495f046ff17137:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__iter__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="46187d0448e04a5a8b880db0615e19ee"><span data-offset-key="46187d0448e04a5a8b880db0615e19ee:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/expressions.html#generator.__next__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1686c5a6bf0f4c87bb5da08d70955c12"><span data-offset-key="1686c5a6bf0f4c87bb5da08d70955c12:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__next__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="2ddb5687ac42441e90512b9f731e2c8a"><span data-offset-key="2ddb5687ac42441e90512b9f731e2c8a:0"> methods. More information about generators can be found in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/expressions.html#yieldexpr" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="34a0d85e541b4769ad7914fed0fafd19"><span data-offset-key="34a0d85e541b4769ad7914fed0fafd19:0">the documentation for the yield expression</span></span></a><span data-key="e1d7aa4ab36945adb7292a706bf56c2c"><span data-offset-key="e1d7aa4ab36945adb7292a706bf56c2c:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH600-23f228db--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1f83e8bcce3345c4a2db28694aa3017b"><span data-offset-key="1f83e8bcce3345c4a2db28694aa3017b:0">Sequence Types — </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#list" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4a586233591040c9bc6e7e0781770f29"><span data-offset-key="4a586233591040c9bc6e7e0781770f29:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">list</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d88e51e187b0467f8501cf525c621ce7"><span data-offset-key="d88e51e187b0467f8501cf525c621ce7:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#tuple" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e4872c1fa3654d539eb35cc59b7a37fe"><span data-offset-key="e4872c1fa3654d539eb35cc59b7a37fe:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">tuple</code></span></span></a><span data-key="654f3de394db4c0fac6237e3de9c5447"><span data-offset-key="654f3de394db4c0fac6237e3de9c5447:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#range" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2d4f7777fc2e4f178104518c5259840a"><span data-offset-key="2d4f7777fc2e4f178104518c5259840a:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">range</code></span></span></a><span data-key="fa8145ad4af745aca2c40c06f720cbca"><span data-offset-key="fa8145ad4af745aca2c40c06f720cbca:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="079d94bc9d894202a36a90390290d425"><span data-offset-key="079d94bc9d894202a36a90390290d425:0">There are three basic sequence types: lists, tuples, and range objects. Additional sequence types tailored for processing of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#binaryseq" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="acb267d610284f1ca0ff0c275a455b88"><span data-offset-key="acb267d610284f1ca0ff0c275a455b88:0">binary data</span></span></a><span data-key="4303c38a05dc4f7382d8aa46494c6a55"><span data-offset-key="4303c38a05dc4f7382d8aa46494c6a55:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#textseq" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3f91a2a642b94ba2a590345ff3abec03"><span data-offset-key="3f91a2a642b94ba2a590345ff3abec03:0">text strings</span></span></a><span data-key="9ad9324a8104481d99f00b00a4572eab"><span data-offset-key="9ad9324a8104481d99f00b00a4572eab:0"> are described in dedicated sections.</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="265e591b72054312865d2841115f5c8e"><span data-offset-key="265e591b72054312865d2841115f5c8e:0">Common Sequence Operations</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2f990cee43494dabac5d414efa60633f"><span data-offset-key="2f990cee43494dabac5d414efa60633f:0">The operations in the following table are supported by most sequence types, both mutable and immutable. The </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/collections.abc.html#collections.abc.Sequence" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ef709aa1427e418fa0a30901c454079b"><span data-offset-key="ef709aa1427e418fa0a30901c454079b:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">collections.abc.Sequence</code></span></span></a><span data-key="048744ddc6db46e4bb2e5caf3d6988ab"><span data-offset-key="048744ddc6db46e4bb2e5caf3d6988ab:0"> ABC is provided to make it easier to correctly implement these operations on custom sequence types.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="51db3a5b1e0d41efa177ea6fcd1cd151"><span data-offset-key="51db3a5b1e0d41efa177ea6fcd1cd151:0">This table lists the sequence operations sorted in ascending priority. In the table, </span><span data-offset-key="51db3a5b1e0d41efa177ea6fcd1cd151:1">*s*</span><span data-offset-key="51db3a5b1e0d41efa177ea6fcd1cd151:2"> and </span><span data-offset-key="51db3a5b1e0d41efa177ea6fcd1cd151:3">*t*</span><span data-offset-key="51db3a5b1e0d41efa177ea6fcd1cd151:4"> are sequences of the same type, </span><span data-offset-key="51db3a5b1e0d41efa177ea6fcd1cd151:5">*n*</span><span data-offset-key="51db3a5b1e0d41efa177ea6fcd1cd151:6">, </span><span data-offset-key="51db3a5b1e0d41efa177ea6fcd1cd151:7">*i*</span><span data-offset-key="51db3a5b1e0d41efa177ea6fcd1cd151:8">, </span><span data-offset-key="51db3a5b1e0d41efa177ea6fcd1cd151:9">*j*</span><span data-offset-key="51db3a5b1e0d41efa177ea6fcd1cd151:10"> and </span><span data-offset-key="51db3a5b1e0d41efa177ea6fcd1cd151:11">*k*</span><span data-offset-key="51db3a5b1e0d41efa177ea6fcd1cd151:12"> are integers and </span><span data-offset-key="51db3a5b1e0d41efa177ea6fcd1cd151:13">*x*</span><span data-offset-key="51db3a5b1e0d41efa177ea6fcd1cd151:14"> is an arbitrary object that meets any type and value restrictions imposed by </span><span data-offset-key="51db3a5b1e0d41efa177ea6fcd1cd151:15">*s*</span><span data-offset-key="51db3a5b1e0d41efa177ea6fcd1cd151:16">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0b7299525e5b48a78126293740abdc74"><span data-offset-key="0b7299525e5b48a78126293740abdc74:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="0b7299525e5b48a78126293740abdc74:1">`in`</span><span data-offset-key="0b7299525e5b48a78126293740abdc74:2"> and </span><span data-offset-key="0b7299525e5b48a78126293740abdc74:3">`not in`</span><span data-offset-key="0b7299525e5b48a78126293740abdc74:4"> operations have the same priorities as the comparison operations. The </span><span data-offset-key="0b7299525e5b48a78126293740abdc74:5">`+`</span><span data-offset-key="0b7299525e5b48a78126293740abdc74:6"> (concatenation) and </span><span data-offset-key="0b7299525e5b48a78126293740abdc74:7">`*`</span><span data-offset-key="0b7299525e5b48a78126293740abdc74:8"> (repetition) operations have the same priority as the corresponding numeric operations. </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#id14" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5e14a3e1727f4ade89bdb5857e55af55"><span data-offset-key="5e14a3e1727f4ade89bdb5857e55af55:0">3</span></span></a><span data-key="fb5665edcd574ad0a72690c1b90f21b7"><span data-offset-key="fb5665edcd574ad0a72690c1b90f21b7:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ee37c680d92048b5bd9d9ce13b1221bf"><span data-offset-key="ee37c680d92048b5bd9d9ce13b1221bf:0"><code class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f5db74cd341f4c33baae9b722303137b"><span data-offset-key="f5db74cd341f4c33baae9b722303137b:0">slice of </span><span data-offset-key="f5db74cd341f4c33baae9b722303137b:1"><em>s</em></span><span data-offset-key="f5db74cd341f4c33baae9b722303137b:2"> from </span><span data-offset-key="f5db74cd341f4c33baae9b722303137b:3"><em>i</em></span><span data-offset-key="f5db74cd341f4c33baae9b722303137b:4"> to </span><span data-offset-key="f5db74cd341f4c33baae9b722303137b:5"><em>j</em></span><span data-offset-key="f5db74cd341f4c33baae9b722303137b:6"> with step </span><span data-offset-key="f5db74cd341f4c33baae9b722303137b:7"><em>k</em></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="51784e404cd24285a63a8c61c52a297f"><span data-offset-key="51784e404cd24285a63a8c61c52a297f:0">(3)(5)</span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="28ec06bb0e85496e87c218884960b6ef"><span data-offset-key="28ec06bb0e85496e87c218884960b6ef:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">len(s)</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span data-offset-key="8ead0c5718a846bebb71c0c60516cbd9:1"><em>s</em></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="35b8c0a514104dc895d9fb261f3c270d"><span data-offset-key="35b8c0a514104dc895d9fb261f3c270d:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="even"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9481f3da2ebf4accbbf6393ccda099a2"><span data-offset-key="9481f3da2ebf4accbbf6393ccda099a2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">min(s)</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e71622c0ff7a41f5a56c824e63239cca"><span data-offset-key="e71622c0ff7a41f5a56c824e63239cca:0">smallest item of </span><span data-offset-key="e71622c0ff7a41f5a56c824e63239cca:1"><em>s</em></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b1fd9e9f20904c318cc0d5ba15e5f38d"><span data-offset-key="b1fd9e9f20904c318cc0d5ba15e5f38d:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-slate-leaf="true">max(s)</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-offset-key="25d8cdb6d1f54babac5ab2d0d2e3ec85:1"><em>s</em></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span
