data-key="95af8fe20efe475b9c3f77992d8fe8eb"><span data-offset-key="95af8fe20efe475b9c3f77992d8fe8eb:0"> is that a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#range" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="af402bbf413d403f9935f512f2b36200"><span data-offset-key="af402bbf413d403f9935f512f2b36200:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">range</code></span></span></a><span data-key="4d6abf6a31cc4b9fbb6d9e6f0d199170"><span data-offset-key="4d6abf6a31cc4b9fbb6d9e6f0d199170:0"> object will always take the same (small) amount of memory, no matter the size of the range it represents (as it only stores the </span><span data-offset-key="4d6abf6a31cc4b9fbb6d9e6f0d199170:1">`start`</span><span data-offset-key="4d6abf6a31cc4b9fbb6d9e6f0d199170:2">, </span><span data-offset-key="4d6abf6a31cc4b9fbb6d9e6f0d199170:3">`stop`</span><span data-offset-key="4d6abf6a31cc4b9fbb6d9e6f0d199170:4"> and </span><span data-offset-key="4d6abf6a31cc4b9fbb6d9e6f0d199170:5">`step`</span><span data-offset-key="4d6abf6a31cc4b9fbb6d9e6f0d199170:6"> values, calculating individual items and subranges as needed).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d72f0e35c8194a1ab50de08d3c54c651"><span data-offset-key="d72f0e35c8194a1ab50de08d3c54c651:0">Range objects implement the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/collections.abc.html#collections.abc.Sequence" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f90f6947e7f84077b78ce6cf1147446f"><span data-offset-key="f90f6947e7f84077b78ce6cf1147446f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">collections.abc.Sequence</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a75412fd0605401298acefcfa4deb1dd"><span data-offset-key="a75412fd0605401298acefcfa4deb1dd:0"> ABC, and provide features such as containment tests, element index lookup, slicing and support for negative indices (see </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#typesseq" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="733010514a174fc895c4b46fc9c94460"><span data-offset-key="733010514a174fc895c4b46fc9c94460:0">Sequence Types — list, tuple, range</span></span></a><span data-key="f289d90b66a04d8f9d4273f2223b3185"><span data-offset-key="f289d90b66a04d8f9d4273f2223b3185:0">):&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> r = range(0, 20, 2)>>> rrange(0, 20, 2)>>> 11 in rFalse>>> 10 in rTrue>>> r.index(10)5>>> r[5]10>>> r[:5]range(0, 10, 2)>>> r[-1]18

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fb7f0faa29204ca586a7666fba98e3ee"><span data-offset-key="fb7f0faa29204ca586a7666fba98e3ee:0">Testing range objects for equality with </span><span data-offset-key="fb7f0faa29204ca586a7666fba98e3ee:1">`==`</span><span data-offset-key="fb7f0faa29204ca586a7666fba98e3ee:2"> and </span><span data-offset-key="fb7f0faa29204ca586a7666fba98e3ee:3">`!=`</span><span data-offset-key="fb7f0faa29204ca586a7666fba98e3ee:4"> compares them as sequences. That is, two range objects are considered equal if they represent the same sequence of values. (Note that two range objects that compare equal might have different </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#range.start" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5f00d85fd1d94fc2bd27e549c2a3a320"><span data-offset-key="5f00d85fd1d94fc2bd27e549c2a3a320:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">start</code></span></span></a><span data-key="67c82deadd8a45ff894da97fda08f5d2"><span data-offset-key="67c82deadd8a45ff894da97fda08f5d2:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#range.stop" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5cfa67e85cb141b6bfbbe471cb595967"><span data-offset-key="5cfa67e85cb141b6bfbbe471cb595967:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">stop</code></span></span></a><span data-key="117a4b93e6f646e29a1b1a77f65c38da"><span data-offset-key="117a4b93e6f646e29a1b1a77f65c38da:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#range.step" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="49526b0f52104f36924507fcb911a582"><span data-offset-key="49526b0f52104f36924507fcb911a582:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">step</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a2e44918ff8b4e96a2cc54716693ae15"><span data-offset-key="a2e44918ff8b4e96a2cc54716693ae15:0"> attributes, for example </span><span data-offset-key="a2e44918ff8b4e96a2cc54716693ae15:1">`range(0) == range(2, 1, 3)`</span><span data-offset-key="a2e44918ff8b4e96a2cc54716693ae15:2"> or </span><span data-offset-key="a2e44918ff8b4e96a2cc54716693ae15:3">`range(0, 3, 2) == range(0, 4, 2)`</span><span data-offset-key="a2e44918ff8b4e96a2cc54716693ae15:4">.)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e3b4e38b56094e64a713ad5a84dcd72a"><span data-offset-key="e3b4e38b56094e64a713ad5a84dcd72a:0">Changed in version 3.2: Implement the Sequence ABC. Support slicing and negative indices. Test </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="60b5e20cf3764fb99da26562ff34e3e2"><span data-offset-key="60b5e20cf3764fb99da26562ff34e3e2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">int</code></span></span></a><span data-key="415efeac9c934cb39702ad742a820f7f"><span data-offset-key="415efeac9c934cb39702ad742a820f7f:0"> objects for membership in constant time instead of iterating through all items.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ea7f9f10bb5041ff8da83197c33d975e"><span data-offset-key="ea7f9f10bb5041ff8da83197c33d975e:0">Changed in version 3.3: Define ‘==’ and ‘!=’ to compare range objects based on the sequence of values they define (instead of comparing based on object identity).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0b06c46dec21464a99a60f80393ac851"><span data-offset-key="0b06c46dec21464a99a60f80393ac851:0">New in version 3.3: The </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#range.start" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="980d440d536a4df9930b29422aa8b217"><span data-offset-key="980d440d536a4df9930b29422aa8b217:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">start</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d138a2bfbbe943e39a6d6567163c71e2"><span data-offset-key="d138a2bfbbe943e39a6d6567163c71e2:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#range.stop" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="99decc5aa75f4a769920f53ef55f2ebf"><span data-offset-key="99decc5aa75f4a769920f53ef55f2ebf:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">stop</code></span></span></a><span data-key="5cf78e1d46d8485ba981efba101d35b1"><span data-offset-key="5cf78e1d46d8485ba981efba101d35b1:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#range.step" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bc248a86955c44ffac1fbe8d13d2ed6f"><span data-offset-key="bc248a86955c44ffac1fbe8d13d2ed6f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">step</code></span></span></a><span data-key="7e4c97b9d8664f499472c5a47cdb0c0e"><span data-offset-key="7e4c97b9d8664f499472c5a47cdb0c0e:0"> attributes.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8de82de719cb471d96054c2dea06e6bb"><span data-offset-key="8de82de719cb471d96054c2dea06e6bb:0">See also</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5904541ec5b84c209a496b87e5907d2f"><span data-offset-key="5904541ec5b84c209a496b87e5907d2f:0">The </span></span><a href="http://code.activestate.com/recipes/579000/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b11db65037134082b4f9d4c3818cd2ac"><span data-offset-key="b11db65037134082b4f9d4c3818cd2ac:0">linspace recipe</span></span></a><span data-key="ffb436a9f4b64f41ad440d307a50acfe"><span data-offset-key="ffb436a9f4b64f41ad440d307a50acfe:0"> shows how to implement a lazy version of range suitable for floating point applications.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH600-23f228db--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="18a235ee9c6842f1a7a086d96127370f"><span data-offset-key="18a235ee9c6842f1a7a086d96127370f:0">Text Sequence Type — </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="cfb8b78407804121a00906ce9023d584"><span data-offset-key="cfb8b78407804121a00906ce9023d584:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str</code></span></span></a><span data-key="19e94e5c6e7342a0a9bd2061f6ac099d"><span data-offset-key="19e94e5c6e7342a0a9bd2061f6ac099d:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ad64766fad124cbbb9b13b6baefd6361"><span data-offset-key="ad64766fad124cbbb9b13b6baefd6361:0">Textual data in Python is handled with </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4bab9f1b489d41dd837ed8b5c45e4059"><span data-offset-key="4bab9f1b489d41dd837ed8b5c45e4059:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str</code></span></span></a><span data-key="dd8740ab653749b78d051518fc56bde5"><span data-offset-key="dd8740ab653749b78d051518fc56bde5:0"> objects, or </span><span data-offset-key="dd8740ab653749b78d051518fc56bde5:1">*strings*</span><span data-offset-key="dd8740ab653749b78d051518fc56bde5:2">. Strings are immutable </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#typesseq" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3590dbd7dd724ee893023bbbd2d94b85"><span data-offset-key="3590dbd7dd724ee893023bbbd2d94b85:0">sequences</span></span></a><span data-key="7e554a2857de4f90883092036b21bee0"><span data-offset-key="7e554a2857de4f90883092036b21bee0:0"> of Unicode code points. String literals are written in a variety of ways:</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2dd1c4876e5a4f4d8273a8768574f03e"><span data-offset-key="2dd1c4876e5a4f4d8273a8768574f03e:0">Single quotes: </span><span data-offset-key="2dd1c4876e5a4f4d8273a8768574f03e:1">`'allows embedded                                             "double"                                             quotes'`</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e23d0bbf975d4692843cb6dc3e055903"><span data-offset-key="e23d0bbf975d4692843cb6dc3e055903:0">Double quotes: </span><span data-offset-key="e23d0bbf975d4692843cb6dc3e055903:1">`"allows embedded                                             'single'                                             quotes"`</span><span data-offset-key="e23d0bbf975d4692843cb6dc3e055903:2">.</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a9b6530c31d7404a92a30b44a32efe0a"><span data-offset-key="a9b6530c31d7404a92a30b44a32efe0a:0">Triple quoted: </span><span data-offset-key="a9b6530c31d7404a92a30b44a32efe0a:1">`'''Three single                                             quotes'''`</span><span data-offset-key="a9b6530c31d7404a92a30b44a32efe0a:2">, </span><span data-offset-key="a9b6530c31d7404a92a30b44a32efe0a:3">`"""Three double                                             quotes"""`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e1343eacfd3f495ab4f1277b44976ecf"><span data-offset-key="e1343eacfd3f495ab4f1277b44976ecf:0">Triple quoted strings may span multiple lines - all associated whitespace will be included in the string literal.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7cb15d0650514c719b5896b54c5fa7b9"><span data-offset-key="7cb15d0650514c719b5896b54c5fa7b9:0">String literals that are part of a single expression and have only whitespace between them will be implicitly converted to a single string literal. That is, </span><span data-offset-key="7cb15d0650514c719b5896b54c5fa7b9:1">`("spam " "eggs") ==                                       "spam eggs"`</span><span data-offset-key="7cb15d0650514c719b5896b54c5fa7b9:2">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="17ba3eaff81e4a0597372f7a1a524374"><span data-offset-key="17ba3eaff81e4a0597372f7a1a524374:0">See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/lexical_analysis.html#strings" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="de16e8ba43ca4951ac2a95641907f9ff"><span data-offset-key="de16e8ba43ca4951ac2a95641907f9ff:0">String and Bytes literals</span></span></a><span data-key="3f2ce44920164e54b9167fd7eadc8ea5"><span data-offset-key="3f2ce44920164e54b9167fd7eadc8ea5:0"> for more about the various forms of string literal, including supported escape sequences, and the </span><span data-offset-key="3f2ce44920164e54b9167fd7eadc8ea5:1">`r`</span><span data-offset-key="3f2ce44920164e54b9167fd7eadc8ea5:2"> (“raw”) prefix that disables most escape sequence processing.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0aeba9e1316a417e998e0ee392daa9c7"><span data-offset-key="0aeba9e1316a417e998e0ee392daa9c7:0">Strings may also be created from other objects using the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="72f2b965511f4b9aa8647ca6172e4ec0"><span data-offset-key="72f2b965511f4b9aa8647ca6172e4ec0:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str</code></span></span></a><span data-key="948594ce24304504bf77354e18d608a8"><span data-offset-key="948594ce24304504bf77354e18d608a8:0"> constructor.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e5e3103c3b9941d0bca9255f0142fc06"><span data-offset-key="e5e3103c3b9941d0bca9255f0142fc06:0">Since there is no separate “character” type, indexing a string produces strings of length 1. That is, for a non-empty string </span><span data-offset-key="e5e3103c3b9941d0bca9255f0142fc06:1">*s*</span><span data-offset-key="e5e3103c3b9941d0bca9255f0142fc06:2">, </span><span data-offset-key="e5e3103c3b9941d0bca9255f0142fc06:3">`s[0] == s[0:1]`</span><span data-offset-key="e5e3103c3b9941d0bca9255f0142fc06:4">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7036113f3a0b4c07a5481c1f6837e72e"><span data-offset-key="7036113f3a0b4c07a5481c1f6837e72e:0">There is also no mutable string type, but </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str.join" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1a14b2d5481c40239ce2a216bdfd8d66"><span data-offset-key="1a14b2d5481c40239ce2a216bdfd8d66:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str.join()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="00f0f0db7bfb499cb7be1230ffaeda6e"><span data-offset-key="00f0f0db7bfb499cb7be1230ffaeda6e:0"> or </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io.StringIO" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9af09e6c08284904a3883048335ad2ec"><span data-offset-key="9af09e6c08284904a3883048335ad2ec:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">io.StringIO</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f0ed74b250a6481e85425940d980d9ed"><span data-offset-key="f0ed74b250a6481e85425940d980d9ed:0"> can be used to efficiently construct strings from multiple fragments.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="cb18ec78f1734b918faa565cda8fbd2d"><span data-offset-key="cb18ec78f1734b918faa565cda8fbd2d:0">Changed in version 3.3: For backwards compatibility with the Python 2 series, the </span><span data-offset-key="cb18ec78f1734b918faa565cda8fbd2d:1">`u`</span><span data-offset-key="cb18ec78f1734b918faa565cda8fbd2d:2"> prefix is once again permitted on string literals. It has no effect on the meaning of string literals and cannot be combined with the </span><span data-offset-key="cb18ec78f1734b918faa565cda8fbd2d:3">`r`</span><span data-offset-key="cb18ec78f1734b918faa565cda8fbd2d:4"> prefix.</span><span data-offset-key="cb18ec78f1734b918faa565cda8fbd2d:5">*class* </span><span data-offset-key="cb18ec78f1734b918faa565cda8fbd2d:6">`str`</span><span data-offset-key="cb18ec78f1734b918faa565cda8fbd2d:7">(</span><span data-offset-key="cb18ec78f1734b918faa565cda8fbd2d:8">*object=''*</span><span data-offset-key="cb18ec78f1734b918faa565cda8fbd2d:9">)</span><span data-offset-key="cb18ec78f1734b918faa565cda8fbd2d:10">*class* </span><span data-offset-key="cb18ec78f1734b918faa565cda8fbd2d:11">`str`</span><span data-offset-key="cb18ec78f1734b918faa565cda8fbd2d:12">(</span><span data-offset-key="cb18ec78f1734b918faa565cda8fbd2d:13">*object=b''*</span><span data-offset-key="cb18ec78f1734b918faa565cda8fbd2d:14">, </span><span data-offset-key="cb18ec78f1734b918faa565cda8fbd2d:15">*encoding='utf-8'*</span><span data-offset-key="cb18ec78f1734b918faa565cda8fbd2d:16">, </span><span data-offset-key="cb18ec78f1734b918faa565cda8fbd2d:17">*errors='strict'*</span><span data-offset-key="cb18ec78f1734b918faa565cda8fbd2d:18">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8a147471b01c4dccb30e93094267686e"><span data-offset-key="8a147471b01c4dccb30e93094267686e:0">Return a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#textseq" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9499bdaeb92140b79668056e857c64ac"><span data-offset-key="9499bdaeb92140b79668056e857c64ac:0">string</span></span></a><span data-key="e00f7e75986f4e2894c4d5c40d579f93"><span data-offset-key="e00f7e75986f4e2894c4d5c40d579f93:0"> version of </span><span data-offset-key="e00f7e75986f4e2894c4d5c40d579f93:1">*object*</span><span data-offset-key="e00f7e75986f4e2894c4d5c40d579f93:2">. If </span><span data-offset-key="e00f7e75986f4e2894c4d5c40d579f93:3">*object*</span><span data-offset-key="e00f7e75986f4e2894c4d5c40d579f93:4"> is not provided, returns the empty string. Otherwise, the behavior of </span><span data-offset-key="e00f7e75986f4e2894c4d5c40d579f93:5">`str()`</span><span data-offset-key="e00f7e75986f4e2894c4d5c40d579f93:6"> depends on whether </span><span data-offset-key="e00f7e75986f4e2894c4d5c40d579f93:7">*encoding*</span><span data-offset-key="e00f7e75986f4e2894c4d5c40d579f93:8"> or </span><span data-offset-key="e00f7e75986f4e2894c4d5c40d579f93:9">*errors*</span><span data-offset-key="e00f7e75986f4e2894c4d5c40d579f93:10"> is given, as follows.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="55cf7d4187ec40dca16fb5a37c7b0181"><span data-offset-key="55cf7d4187ec40dca16fb5a37c7b0181:0">If neither </span><span data-offset-key="55cf7d4187ec40dca16fb5a37c7b0181:1">*encoding*</span><span data-offset-key="55cf7d4187ec40dca16fb5a37c7b0181:2"> nor </span><span data-offset-key="55cf7d4187ec40dca16fb5a37c7b0181:3">*errors*</span><span data-offset-key="55cf7d4187ec40dca16fb5a37c7b0181:4"> is given, </span><span data-offset-key="55cf7d4187ec40dca16fb5a37c7b0181:5">`str(object)`</span><span data-offset-key="55cf7d4187ec40dca16fb5a37c7b0181:6"> returns </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__str__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f49e936c9c6143d8a1cf177b615dff6d"><span data-offset-key="f49e936c9c6143d8a1cf177b615dff6d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">object.__str__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="cc97f0cc5328406aad4a6d69599c391d"><span data-offset-key="cc97f0cc5328406aad4a6d69599c391d:0">, which is the “informal” or nicely printable string representation of </span><span data-offset-key="cc97f0cc5328406aad4a6d69599c391d:1">*object*</span><span data-offset-key="cc97f0cc5328406aad4a6d69599c391d:2">. For string objects, this is the string itself. If </span><span data-offset-key="cc97f0cc5328406aad4a6d69599c391d:3">*object*</span><span data-offset-key="cc97f0cc5328406aad4a6d69599c391d:4"> does not have a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__str__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3bb8f45b0ac44fe9b7811360bf5d6948"><span data-offset-key="3bb8f45b0ac44fe9b7811360bf5d6948:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__str__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="5cb4fdd0d8cb4c4a911de5a1ead4bd5f"><span data-offset-key="5cb4fdd0d8cb4c4a911de5a1ead4bd5f:0"> method, then </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7caa793f131847e08563aef1d9a578b9"><span data-offset-key="7caa793f131847e08563aef1d9a578b9:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="45a45ad093b340ae98b09379bcc4659a"><span data-offset-key="45a45ad093b340ae98b09379bcc4659a:0"> falls back to returning </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#repr" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e388fa0f84564b14b2c562328fd2e487"><span data-offset-key="e388fa0f84564b14b2c562328fd2e487:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">repr(object)</code></span></span></a><span data-key="4102bb38e2e6443088f34497799d2f6d"><span data-offset-key="4102bb38e2e6443088f34497799d2f6d:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3f56a441ee9c4ab298b92605789577b7"><span data-offset-key="3f56a441ee9c4ab298b92605789577b7:0">If at least one of </span><span data-offset-key="3f56a441ee9c4ab298b92605789577b7:1">*encoding*</span><span data-offset-key="3f56a441ee9c4ab298b92605789577b7:2"> or </span><span data-offset-key="3f56a441ee9c4ab298b92605789577b7:3">*errors*</span><span data-offset-key="3f56a441ee9c4ab298b92605789577b7:4"> is given, </span><span data-offset-key="3f56a441ee9c4ab298b92605789577b7:5">*object*</span><span data-offset-key="3f56a441ee9c4ab298b92605789577b7:6"> should be a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-bytes-like-object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b8feb859e76447e1b50ad3fa7844fe30"><span data-offset-key="b8feb859e76447e1b50ad3fa7844fe30:0">bytes-like object</span></span></a><span data-key="6e0f2f93a29b4cdb96dca5ca43c9cd44"><span data-offset-key="6e0f2f93a29b4cdb96dca5ca43c9cd44:0"> (e.g. </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8dee399f72ba452b8c2142c52bd242a2"><span data-offset-key="8dee399f72ba452b8c2142c52bd242a2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytes</code></span></span></a><span data-key="429c03989eb04a06a123b55c072f1086"><span data-offset-key="429c03989eb04a06a123b55c072f1086:0"> or </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytearray" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7e278b8aaf0f486abd6f8ba0226c6a1d"><span data-offset-key="7e278b8aaf0f486abd6f8ba0226c6a1d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytearray</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f4715052a7eb4380b6e21bf0bf4bc963"><span data-offset-key="f4715052a7eb4380b6e21bf0bf4bc963:0">). In this case, if </span><span data-offset-key="f4715052a7eb4380b6e21bf0bf4bc963:1">*object*</span><span data-offset-key="f4715052a7eb4380b6e21bf0bf4bc963:2"> is a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bb6856f3869e4180bb83f1e6c95a8b00"><span data-offset-key="bb6856f3869e4180bb83f1e6c95a8b00:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytes</code></span></span></a><span data-key="bd7597f6793844baaf3d81e2277933a7"><span data-offset-key="bd7597f6793844baaf3d81e2277933a7:0"> (or </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytearray" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0085d20bec934dfdb38830e62ff62d4f"><span data-offset-key="0085d20bec934dfdb38830e62ff62d4f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytearray</code></span></span></a><span data-key="4f819397d2064a699d949c95576cd0e3"><span data-offset-key="4f819397d2064a699d949c95576cd0e3:0">) object, then </span><span data-offset-key="4f819397d2064a699d949c95576cd0e3:1">`str(bytes, encoding, errors)`</span><span data-offset-key="4f819397d2064a699d949c95576cd0e3:2"> is equivalent to </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes.decode" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="19ccc61190a64c0b8f8a263895cd41eb"><span data-offset-key="19ccc61190a64c0b8f8a263895cd41eb:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytes.decode(encoding, errors)</code></span></span></a><span data-key="678f4a84006946f7b4b0bb54ff4aeb6d"><span data-offset-key="678f4a84006946f7b4b0bb54ff4aeb6d:0">. Otherwise, the bytes object underlying the buffer object is obtained before calling </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes.decode" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2fedfc08030a4f6cadc325b3689d41d4"><span data-offset-key="2fedfc08030a4f6cadc325b3689d41d4:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytes.decode()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="c6c0afc902b44b73b3114e960500a3fb"><span data-offset-key="c6c0afc902b44b73b3114e960500a3fb:0">. See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#binaryseq" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="85a06329593b4279a2ecf7b93c55217d"><span data-offset-key="85a06329593b4279a2ecf7b93c55217d:0">Binary Sequence Types — bytes, bytearray, memoryview</span></span></a><span data-key="05f51901f7074b199bca8b7ea9ef8129"><span data-offset-key="05f51901f7074b199bca8b7ea9ef8129:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/c-api/buffer.html#bufferobjects" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c7a8c50367794f9aa0f15d1aa743637d"><span data-offset-key="c7a8c50367794f9aa0f15d1aa743637d:0">Buffer Protocol</span></span></a><span data-key="2b48bb384d704eb5844dde6c55d8f251"><span data-offset-key="2b48bb384d704eb5844dde6c55d8f251:0"> for information on buffer objects.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ce877d944e9f4a9086b22458b4fa478e"><span data-offset-key="ce877d944e9f4a9086b22458b4fa478e:0">Passing a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="193b8d0f9fac47d784e3f7a12d27762f"><span data-offset-key="193b8d0f9fac47d784e3f7a12d27762f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytes</code></span></span></a><span data-key="e185adb89f3549c790b607297e1c3c78"><span data-offset-key="e185adb89f3549c790b607297e1c3c78:0"> object to </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0510659b6b434bc0bc866bf91f97779e"><span data-offset-key="0510659b6b434bc0bc866bf91f97779e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="db0029bf0da442e3b7ed38daeadef30b"><span data-offset-key="db0029bf0da442e3b7ed38daeadef30b:0"> without the </span><span data-offset-key="db0029bf0da442e3b7ed38daeadef30b:1">*encoding*</span><span data-offset-key="db0029bf0da442e3b7ed38daeadef30b:2"> or </span><span data-offset-key="db0029bf0da442e3b7ed38daeadef30b:3">*errors*</span><span data-offset-key="db0029bf0da442e3b7ed38daeadef30b:4"> arguments falls under the first case of returning the informal string representation (see also the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/using/cmdline.html#cmdoption-b" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a871943ff8c344c9afecb4556bf53a3d"><span data-offset-key="a871943ff8c344c9afecb4556bf53a3d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">-b</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a841fd252986449ebd90edd1da388520"><span data-offset-key="a841fd252986449ebd90edd1da388520:0"> command-line option to Python). For example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> str(b'Zoot!')"b'Zoot!'"

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8f1d82c768a44dd9ac1d33f043309148"><span data-offset-key="8f1d82c768a44dd9ac1d33f043309148:0">For more information on the </span><span data-offset-key="8f1d82c768a44dd9ac1d33f043309148:1">`str`</span><span data-offset-key="8f1d82c768a44dd9ac1d33f043309148:2"> class and its methods, see </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#textseq" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="494b70ebbf0247ba99c5149f4de99351"><span data-offset-key="494b70ebbf0247ba99c5149f4de99351:0">Text Sequence Type — str</span></span></a><span data-key="5698fafa93e242d0bda10e420fa8c397"><span data-offset-key="5698fafa93e242d0bda10e420fa8c397:0"> and the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#string-methods" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="96730a857e5447c4b9bd35c7f1e9f1c1"><span data-offset-key="96730a857e5447c4b9bd35c7f1e9f1c1:0">String Methods</span></span></a><span data-key="cff708614c5f43f8bcd025fe58187ece"><span data-offset-key="cff708614c5f43f8bcd025fe58187ece:0"> section below. To output formatted strings, see the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/lexical_analysis.html#f-strings" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="79bbf65885244763ab74f6c959dc2b1a"><span data-offset-key="79bbf65885244763ab74f6c959dc2b1a:0">Formatted string literals</span></span></a><span data-key="1443c4afba7d4c309f22611f8e4a6f8d"><span data-offset-key="1443c4afba7d4c309f22611f8e4a6f8d:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/string.html#formatstrings" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="45b51f91f76e485895bc55fe1207f829"><span data-offset-key="45b51f91f76e485895bc55fe1207f829:0">Format String Syntax</span></span></a><span data-key="9c7919db4d684a8695d5ab4dc08c2d5f"><span data-offset-key="9c7919db4d684a8695d5ab4dc08c2d5f:0"> sections. In addition, see the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/text.html#stringservices" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9a156e1293d04e788be3bc7442a23564"><span data-offset-key="9a156e1293d04e788be3bc7442a23564:0">Text Processing Services</span></span></a><span data-key="2271e3cfb64a49869ffeeeddf07e88bc"><span data-offset-key="2271e3cfb64a49869ffeeeddf07e88bc:0"> section.</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3a8a6a78d6ab4786bedd242028b9e219"><span data-offset-key="3a8a6a78d6ab4786bedd242028b9e219:0">String Methods</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="88580a35fd7a4f26ad17e1d0f676b4e5"><span data-offset-key="88580a35fd7a4f26ad17e1d0f676b4e5:0">Strings implement all of the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#typesseq-common" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e973a10b5158420582ed89ba34bb7bc2"><span data-offset-key="e973a10b5158420582ed89ba34bb7bc2:0">common</span></span></a><span data-key="5340dfa029664d4fb12aea7d2d6a98ec"><span data-offset-key="5340dfa029664d4fb12aea7d2d6a98ec:0"> sequence operations, along with the additional methods described below.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="566238da68794219bc3e636c50c44353"><span data-offset-key="566238da68794219bc3e636c50c44353:0">Strings also support two styles of string formatting, one providing a large degree of flexibility and customization (see </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str.format" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="16f7df6a745a40269c977b01fe977e1d"><span data-offset-key="16f7df6a745a40269c977b01fe977e1d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str.format()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="67df71b3122742ed91b5b74a6d5e6f00"><span data-offset-key="67df71b3122742ed91b5b74a6d5e6f00:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/string.html#formatstrings" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a8920bcaa2bf4c76afee4784d1d62878"><span data-offset-key="a8920bcaa2bf4c76afee4784d1d62878:0">Format String Syntax</span></span></a><span data-key="59dc1185bf6b40e3bf5b5b502cfd54eb"><span data-offset-key="59dc1185bf6b40e3bf5b5b502cfd54eb:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/string.html#string-formatting" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="108a33c1270a49c5bd0a8af9041b25ae"><span data-offset-key="108a33c1270a49c5bd0a8af9041b25ae:0">Custom String Formatting</span></span></a><span data-key="a372924ba9944277ae554765d62416a6"><span data-offset-key="a372924ba9944277ae554765d62416a6:0">) and the other based on C </span><span data-offset-key="a372924ba9944277ae554765d62416a6:1">`printf`</span><span data-offset-key="a372924ba9944277ae554765d62416a6:2"> style formatting that handles a narrower range of types and is slightly harder to use correctly, but is often faster for the cases it can handle (</span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#old-string-formatting" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3bbb87f817a748ed817b170f13a77353"><span data-offset-key="3bbb87f817a748ed817b170f13a77353:0">printf-style String Formatting</span></span></a><span data-key="dd2ce1f583764725831ad8d8d0659f34"><span data-offset-key="dd2ce1f583764725831ad8d8d0659f34:0">).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="dd5da76289d04dd9b3c412535ebf7b41"><span data-offset-key="dd5da76289d04dd9b3c412535ebf7b41:0">The </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/text.html#textservices" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6d51090f37664c15a0bd5ddfcb115972"><span data-offset-key="6d51090f37664c15a0bd5ddfcb115972:0">Text Processing Services</span></span></a><span data-key="2037dbda1a0b45c4a81e2db67e08bf38"><span data-offset-key="2037dbda1a0b45c4a81e2db67e08bf38:0"> section of the standard library covers a number of other modules that provide various text related utilities (including regular expression support in the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/re.html#module-re" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="65726886ba97466e9e6db05bd25f4172"><span data-offset-key="65726886ba97466e9e6db05bd25f4172:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">re</code></span></span></a><span data-key="3c2d67b85e1b4cb7899c57352e07551c"><span data-offset-key="3c2d67b85e1b4cb7899c57352e07551c:0"> module).</span><span data-offset-key="3c2d67b85e1b4cb7899c57352e07551c:1">`str.capitalize`</span><span data-offset-key="3c2d67b85e1b4cb7899c57352e07551c:2">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="53bf6771c7ae4d5591f24f644989f37b"><span data-offset-key="53bf6771c7ae4d5591f24f644989f37b:0">Return a copy of the string with its first character capitalized and the rest lowercased.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="47989b61c8964949850a4133b782e669"><span data-offset-key="47989b61c8964949850a4133b782e669:0">Changed in version 3.8: The first character is now put into titlecase rather than uppercase. This means that characters like digraphs will only have their first letter capitalized, instead of the full character.</span><span data-offset-key="47989b61c8964949850a4133b782e669:1">`str.casefold`</span><span data-offset-key="47989b61c8964949850a4133b782e669:2">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6cd306777cec466599399dde728e59f5"><span data-offset-key="6cd306777cec466599399dde728e59f5:0">Return a casefolded copy of the string. Casefolded strings may be used for caseless matching.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="09a6dd3c4e36455cbfaac6730d0fca73"><span data-offset-key="09a6dd3c4e36455cbfaac6730d0fca73:0">Casefolding is similar to lowercasing but more aggressive because it is intended to remove all case distinctions in a string. For example, the German lowercase letter </span><span data-offset-key="09a6dd3c4e36455cbfaac6730d0fca73:1">`'ß'`</span><span data-offset-key="09a6dd3c4e36455cbfaac6730d0fca73:2"> is equivalent to </span><span data-offset-key="09a6dd3c4e36455cbfaac6730d0fca73:3">`"ss"`</span><span data-offset-key="09a6dd3c4e36455cbfaac6730d0fca73:4">. Since it is already lowercase, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str.lower" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b24bfbcda7e74a9a855d5ed917f2c370"><span data-offset-key="b24bfbcda7e74a9a855d5ed917f2c370:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">lower()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="48bc671efa0640c28a44f7b5276eb5dc"><span data-offset-key="48bc671efa0640c28a44f7b5276eb5dc:0"> would do nothing to </span><span data-offset-key="48bc671efa0640c28a44f7b5276eb5dc:1">`'ß'`</span><span data-offset-key="48bc671efa0640c28a44f7b5276eb5dc:2">; </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str.casefold" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f09d219b0b4b4c1bb21aa3415abb5917"><span data-offset-key="f09d219b0b4b4c1bb21aa3415abb5917:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">casefold()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="99cd5c0f30aa40578cb78e26aa559bc8"><span data-offset-key="99cd5c0f30aa40578cb78e26aa559bc8:0"> converts it to </span><span data-offset-key="99cd5c0f30aa40578cb78e26aa559bc8:1">`"ss"`</span><span data-offset-key="99cd5c0f30aa40578cb78e26aa559bc8:2">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="060c2e002ae54df4b39644174d909c9e"><span data-offset-key="060c2e002ae54df4b39644174d909c9e:0">The casefolding algorithm is described in section 3.13 of the Unicode Standard.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4ede3e3f5f3a4cbabe5ebd1d4794ad32"><span data-offset-key="4ede3e3f5f3a4cbabe5ebd1d4794ad32:0">New in version 3.3.</span><span data-offset-key="4ede3e3f5f3a4cbabe5ebd1d4794ad32:1">`str.center`</span><span data-offset-key="4ede3e3f5f3a4cbabe5ebd1d4794ad32:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="4ede3e3f5f3a4cbabe5ebd1d4794ad32:3">*width*</span><span data-offset-key="4ede3e3f5f3a4cbabe5ebd1d4794ad32:4">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="4ede3e3f5f3a4cbabe5ebd1d4794ad32:5">*fillchar*</span><span data-offset-key="4ede3e3f5f3a4cbabe5ebd1d4794ad32:6">\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="bbdaee1d44d14beabf126eae09f58734"><span data-offset-key="bbdaee1d44d14beabf126eae09f58734:0">Return centered in a string of length </span><span data-offset-key="bbdaee1d44d14beabf126eae09f58734:1">*width*</span><span data-offset-key="bbdaee1d44d14beabf126eae09f58734:2">. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="68ad842836584bfeb8f0c220d2ea2450"><span data-offset-key="68ad842836584bfeb8f0c220d2ea2450:0">Return the number of non-overlapping occurrences of substring </span><span data-offset-key="68ad842836584bfeb8f0c220d2ea2450:1">*sub*</span><span data-offset-key="68ad842836584bfeb8f0c220d2ea2450:2"> in the range \[</span><span data-offset-key="68ad842836584bfeb8f0c220d2ea2450:3">*start*</span><span data-offset-key="68ad842836584bfeb8f0c220d2ea2450:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="68ad842836584bfeb8f0c220d2ea2450:5">*end*</span><span data-offset-key="68ad842836584bfeb8f0c220d2ea2450:6">\]. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="aa3bc190e01f483580b9c6a2acdceabb"><span data-offset-key="aa3bc190e01f483580b9c6a2acdceabb:0">Return an encoded version of the string as a bytes object. The default for </span><span data-offset-key="aa3bc190e01f483580b9c6a2acdceabb:5">*errors*</span><span data-offset-key="aa3bc190e01f483580b9c6a2acdceabb:6"> is </span><span data-offset-key="aa3bc190e01f483580b9c6a2acdceabb:7">`'strict'`</span><span data-offset-key="aa3bc190e01f483580b9c6a2acdceabb:8">, meaning that encoding errors raise a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#UnicodeError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d8bcd5ec6daa4a6ea77b89bd76ec7b73"><span data-offset-key="d8bcd5ec6daa4a6ea77b89bd76ec7b73:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">UnicodeError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="5e972ff501dd46bd82dd8c27f4569342"><span data-offset-key="5e972ff501dd46bd82dd8c27f4569342:0">. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="77ad63eb1b95471d8186a0ad9f5b4da4"><span data-offset-key="77ad63eb1b95471d8186a0ad9f5b4da4:0">By default, the </span><span data-offset-key="77ad63eb1b95471d8186a0ad9f5b4da4:1">*errors*</span><span data-offset-key="77ad63eb1b95471d8186a0ad9f5b4da4:2"> argument is not checked for best performances, but only used at the first encoding error. Enable the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/devmode.html#devmode" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="30718ec1058f4dd093a2c66235258be5"><span data-offset-key="30718ec1058f4dd093a2c66235258be5:0">Python Development Mode</span></span></a><span data-key="20773e4ba2404e629d2b9c99440a5c00"><span data-offset-key="20773e4ba2404e629d2b9c99440a5c00:0">, or use a debug build to check </span><span data-offset-key="20773e4ba2404e629d2b9c99440a5c00:1">*errors*</span><span data-offset-key="20773e4ba2404e629d2b9c99440a5c00:2">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d7b4c9dd43bb4a48805ef21e37d57e4c"><span data-offset-key="d7b4c9dd43bb4a48805ef21e37d57e4c:0">Changed in version 3.9: The </span><span data-offset-key="d7b4c9dd43bb4a48805ef21e37d57e4c:1">*errors*</span><span data-offset-key="d7b4c9dd43bb4a48805ef21e37d57e4c:2"> is now checked in development mode and in debug mode.</span><span data-offset-key="d7b4c9dd43bb4a48805ef21e37d57e4c:3">`str.endswith`</span><span data-offset-key="d7b4c9dd43bb4a48805ef21e37d57e4c:4">(</span><span data-offset-key="d7b4c9dd43bb4a48805ef21e37d57e4c:5">*suffix*</span><span data-offset-key="d7b4c9dd43bb4a48805ef21e37d57e4c:6">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="d7b4c9dd43bb4a48805ef21e37d57e4c:7">*start*</span><span data-offset-key="d7b4c9dd43bb4a48805ef21e37d57e4c:8">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="d7b4c9dd43bb4a48805ef21e37d57e4c:9">*end*</span><span data-offset-key="d7b4c9dd43bb4a48805ef21e37d57e4c:10">\]\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2cf5c438eed645f6a1e91218f977ea61"><span data-offset-key="2cf5c438eed645f6a1e91218f977ea61:0">Return </span><span data-offset-key="2cf5c438eed645f6a1e91218f977ea61:1">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="2cf5c438eed645f6a1e91218f977ea61:2"> if the string ends with the specified </span><span data-offset-key="2cf5c438eed645f6a1e91218f977ea61:3">*suffix*</span><span data-offset-key="2cf5c438eed645f6a1e91218f977ea61:4">, otherwise return </span><span data-offset-key="2cf5c438eed645f6a1e91218f977ea61:5">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="2cf5c438eed645f6a1e91218f977ea61:6">. </span><span data-offset-key="2cf5c438eed645f6a1e91218f977ea61:7">*suffix*</span><span data-offset-key="2cf5c438eed645f6a1e91218f977ea61:8"> can also be a tuple of suffixes to look for. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b2bf6015f24a4712a14026b9cea0f36a"><span data-offset-key="b2bf6015f24a4712a14026b9cea0f36a:0">Return a copy of the string where all tab characters are replaced by one or more spaces, depending on the current column and the given tab size. Tab positions occur every </span><span data-offset-key="b2bf6015f24a4712a14026b9cea0f36a:1">*tabsize*</span><span data-offset-key="b2bf6015f24a4712a14026b9cea0f36a:2"> characters (default is 8, giving tab positions at columns 0, 8, 16 and so on). To expand the string, the current column is set to zero and the string is examined character by character. If the character is a tab (</span><span data-offset-key="b2bf6015f24a4712a14026b9cea0f36a:3">`\t`</span><span data-offset-key="b2bf6015f24a4712a14026b9cea0f36a:4">), one or more space characters are inserted in the result until the current column is equal to the next tab position. (The tab character itself is not copied.) If the character is a newline (</span><span data-offset-key="b2bf6015f24a4712a14026b9cea0f36a:5">`\n`</span><span data-offset-key="b2bf6015f24a4712a14026b9cea0f36a:6">) or return (</span><span data-offset-key="b2bf6015f24a4712a14026b9cea0f36a:7">`\r`</span><span data-offset-key="b2bf6015f24a4712a14026b9cea0f36a:8">), it is copied and the current column is reset to zero. Any other character is copied unchanged and the current column is incremented by one regardless of how the character is represented when printed.&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> '01\t012\t0123\t01234'.expandtabs()'01      012     0123    01234'>>> '01\t012\t0123\t01234'.expandtabs(4)'01  012 0123    01234'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5cbcb4dc74ff480d8a8c4488d4102ead"><span data-offset-key="5cbcb4dc74ff480d8a8c4488d4102ead:0">`str.find`</span><span data-offset-key="5cbcb4dc74ff480d8a8c4488d4102ead:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="5cbcb4dc74ff480d8a8c4488d4102ead:2">*sub*</span><span data-offset-key="5cbcb4dc74ff480d8a8c4488d4102ead:3">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="5cbcb4dc74ff480d8a8c4488d4102ead:4">*start*</span><span data-offset-key="5cbcb4dc74ff480d8a8c4488d4102ead:5">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="5cbcb4dc74ff480d8a8c4488d4102ead:6">*end*</span><span data-offset-key="5cbcb4dc74ff480d8a8c4488d4102ead:7">\]\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ce9b1d78e651472bb41c4fc63c2f54d5"><span data-offset-key="ce9b1d78e651472bb41c4fc63c2f54d5:0">Return the lowest index in the string where substring </span><span data-offset-key="ce9b1d78e651472bb41c4fc63c2f54d5:1">*sub*</span><span data-offset-key="ce9b1d78e651472bb41c4fc63c2f54d5:2"> is found within the slice </span><span data-offset-key="ce9b1d78e651472bb41c4fc63c2f54d5:3">`s[start:end]`</span><span data-offset-key="ce9b1d78e651472bb41c4fc63c2f54d5:4">. Optional arguments </span><span data-offset-key="ce9b1d78e651472bb41c4fc63c2f54d5:5">*start*</span><span data-offset-key="ce9b1d78e651472bb41c4fc63c2f54d5:6"> and </span><span data-offset-key="ce9b1d78e651472bb41c4fc63c2f54d5:7">*end*</span><span data-offset-key="ce9b1d78e651472bb41c4fc63c2f54d5:8"> are interpreted as in slice notation. Return </span><span data-offset-key="ce9b1d78e651472bb41c4fc63c2f54d5:9">`-1`</span><span data-offset-key="ce9b1d78e651472bb41c4fc63c2f54d5:10"> if </span><span data-offset-key="ce9b1d78e651472bb41c4fc63c2f54d5:11">*sub*</span><span data-offset-key="ce9b1d78e651472bb41c4fc63c2f54d5:12"> is not found.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="17906e3cef5b440dad10a48145f85320"><span data-offset-key="17906e3cef5b440dad10a48145f85320:0">Note </span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="10768410acca4bd0b4647df3c5e188b5"><span data-offset-key="10768410acca4bd0b4647df3c5e188b5:0">The </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str.find" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9e62618ec0a64e39a9988f921fb2e326"><span data-offset-key="9e62618ec0a64e39a9988f921fb2e326:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">find()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="bc18eae7c0b14fe984599f756fe7ab1e"><span data-offset-key="bc18eae7c0b14fe984599f756fe7ab1e:0"> method should be used only if you need to know the position of </span><span data-offset-key="bc18eae7c0b14fe984599f756fe7ab1e:1">*sub*</span><span data-offset-key="bc18eae7c0b14fe984599f756fe7ab1e:2">. To check if </span><span data-offset-key="bc18eae7c0b14fe984599f756fe7ab1e:3">*sub*</span><span data-offset-key="bc18eae7c0b14fe984599f756fe7ab1e:4"> is a substring or not, use the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/expressions.html#in" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c1ed85798a4641c6afd4424f793ea82d"><span data-offset-key="c1ed85798a4641c6afd4424f793ea82d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">in</code></span></span></a><span data-key="23fce77fdb0a4d70b78d5dd7989bd8a5"><span data-offset-key="23fce77fdb0a4d70b78d5dd7989bd8a5:0"> operator:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> 'Py' in 'Python'True

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3491cac1f2dc4368820bae15c96a36ca"><span data-offset-key="3491cac1f2dc4368820bae15c96a36ca:0">`str.format`</span><span data-offset-key="3491cac1f2dc4368820bae15c96a36ca:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="3491cac1f2dc4368820bae15c96a36ca:2">*\*args*</span><span data-offset-key="3491cac1f2dc4368820bae15c96a36ca:3">, </span><span data-offset-key="3491cac1f2dc4368820bae15c96a36ca:4">*\*\*kwargs*</span><span data-offset-key="3491cac1f2dc4368820bae15c96a36ca:5">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a663cf279a7e45309e27d1d4b6d97a57"><span data-offset-key="a663cf279a7e45309e27d1d4b6d97a57:0">Perform a string formatting operation. The string on which this method is called can contain literal text or replacement fields delimited by braces </span><span data-offset-key="a663cf279a7e45309e27d1d4b6d97a57:1">`{}`</span><span data-offset-key="a663cf279a7e45309e27d1d4b6d97a57:2">. Each replacement field contains either the numeric index of a positional argument, or the name of a keyword argument. Returns a copy of the string where each replacement field is replaced with the string value of the corresponding argument.&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> "The sum of 1 + 2 is {0}".format(1+2)'The sum of 1 + 2 is 3'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="cbacc92410bf4264a99da1074e663048"><span data-offset-key="cbacc92410bf4264a99da1074e663048:0">See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/string.html#formatstrings" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c82e5f87562642c4ad27ac0b30b6aaf5"><span data-offset-key="c82e5f87562642c4ad27ac0b30b6aaf5:0">Format String Syntax</span></span></a><span data-key="0ff654e5443344489b9dda7b53593aa7"><span data-offset-key="0ff654e5443344489b9dda7b53593aa7:0"> for a description of the various formatting options that can be specified in format strings.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6e25bc16ff79472cbea9107d14fd7be8"><span data-offset-key="6e25bc16ff79472cbea9107d14fd7be8:0">Note </span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2ac91b1bd1444ccd9f043a8c8b7c4605"><span data-offset-key="2ac91b1bd1444ccd9f043a8c8b7c4605:0">When formatting a number (</span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c214652a17d344ec937d6aba12a323cc"><span data-offset-key="c214652a17d344ec937d6aba12a323cc:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">int</code></span></span></a><span data-key="83e5d6bc5f4f4a68b1d88633f177ace1"><span data-offset-key="83e5d6bc5f4f4a68b1d88633f177ace1:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#float" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="df33ecfa9cd24ac1a14947453d73517f"><span data-offset-key="df33ecfa9cd24ac1a14947453d73517f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">float</code></span></span></a><span data-key="cbd58af535ea4f68a8c8dc5562c1a398"><span data-offset-key="cbd58af535ea4f68a8c8dc5562c1a398:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#complex" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1c71f06497f5429f88d8a46607f99557"><span data-offset-key="1c71f06497f5429f88d8a46607f99557:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">complex</code></span></span></a><span data-key="1772ac579d3948a2852b5ca8eca72263"><span data-offset-key="1772ac579d3948a2852b5ca8eca72263:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/decimal.html#decimal.Decimal" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1015c2ce1b3e44b8b1790d41127afe2b"><span data-offset-key="1015c2ce1b3e44b8b1790d41127afe2b:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">decimal.Decimal</code></span></span></a><span data-key="c59728e43bd443288c2af4f67f36a1be"><span data-offset-key="c59728e43bd443288c2af4f67f36a1be:0"> and subclasses) with the </span><span data-offset-key="c59728e43bd443288c2af4f67f36a1be:1">`n`</span><span data-offset-key="c59728e43bd443288c2af4f67f36a1be:2"> type (ex: </span><span data-offset-key="c59728e43bd443288c2af4f67f36a1be:3">`'{:n}'.format(1234)`</span><span data-offset-key="c59728e43bd443288c2af4f67f36a1be:4">), the function temporarily sets the </span><span data-offset-key="c59728e43bd443288c2af4f67f36a1be:5">`LC_CTYPE`</span><span data-offset-key="c59728e43bd443288c2af4f67f36a1be:6"> locale to the </span><span data-offset-key="c59728e43bd443288c2af4f67f36a1be:7">`LC_NUMERIC`</span><span data-offset-key="c59728e43bd443288c2af4f67f36a1be:8"> locale to decode </span><span data-offset-key="c59728e43bd443288c2af4f67f36a1be:9">`decimal_point`</span><span data-offset-key="c59728e43bd443288c2af4f67f36a1be:10"> and </span><span data-offset-key="c59728e43bd443288c2af4f67f36a1be:11">`thousands_sep`</span><span data-offset-key="c59728e43bd443288c2af4f67f36a1be:12"> fields of </span><span data-offset-key="c59728e43bd443288c2af4f67f36a1be:13">`localeconv()`</span><span data-offset-key="c59728e43bd443288c2af4f67f36a1be:14"> if they are non-ASCII or longer than 1 byte, and the </span><span data-offset-key="c59728e43bd443288c2af4f67f36a1be:15">`LC_NUMERIC`</span><span data-offset-key="c59728e43bd443288c2af4f67f36a1be:16"> locale is different than the </span><span data-offset-key="c59728e43bd443288c2af4f67f36a1be:17">`LC_CTYPE`</span><span data-offset-key="c59728e43bd443288c2af4f67f36a1be:18"> locale. This temporary change affects other threads.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="726a47660b57446ba7dde5fe3199338f"><span data-offset-key="726a47660b57446ba7dde5fe3199338f:0">Changed in version 3.7: When formatting a number with the </span><span data-offset-key="726a47660b57446ba7dde5fe3199338f:1">`n`</span><span data-offset-key="726a47660b57446ba7dde5fe3199338f:2"> type, the function sets temporarily the </span><span data-offset-key="726a47660b57446ba7dde5fe3199338f:3">`LC_CTYPE`</span><span data-offset-key="726a47660b57446ba7dde5fe3199338f:4"> locale to the </span><span data-offset-key="726a47660b57446ba7dde5fe3199338f:5">`LC_NUMERIC`</span><span data-offset-key="726a47660b57446ba7dde5fe3199338f:6"> locale in some cases.</span><span data-offset-key="726a47660b57446ba7dde5fe3199338f:7">`str.format_map`</span><span data-offset-key="726a47660b57446ba7dde5fe3199338f:8">(</span><span data-offset-key="726a47660b57446ba7dde5fe3199338f:9">*mapping*</span><span data-offset-key="726a47660b57446ba7dde5fe3199338f:10">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="32c25615ee9b4293b11bff0495fb5ead"><span data-offset-key="32c25615ee9b4293b11bff0495fb5ead:0">Similar to </span><span data-offset-key="32c25615ee9b4293b11bff0495fb5ead:1">`str.format(**mapping)`</span><span data-offset-key="32c25615ee9b4293b11bff0495fb5ead:2">, except that </span><span data-offset-key="32c25615ee9b4293b11bff0495fb5ead:3">`mapping`</span><span data-offset-key="32c25615ee9b4293b11bff0495fb5ead:4"> is used directly and not copied to a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#dict" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="569530508da046e2bf013da37ca0a38d"><span data-offset-key="569530508da046e2bf013da37ca0a38d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">dict</code></span></span></a><span data-key="109df59a68804beb903e2f1fab4d4218"><span data-offset-key="109df59a68804beb903e2f1fab4d4218:0">. This is useful if for example </span><span data-offset-key="109df59a68804beb903e2f1fab4d4218:1">`mapping`</span><span data-offset-key="109df59a68804beb903e2f1fab4d4218:2"> is a dict subclass:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> class Default(dict):...     def __missing__(self, key):...         return key...>>> '{name} was born in {country}'.format_map(Default(name='Guido'))'Guido was born in country'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9c60dd3227a343d7b33fe77790009aeb"><span data-offset-key="9c60dd3227a343d7b33fe77790009aeb:0">New in version 3.2.</span><span data-offset-key="9c60dd3227a343d7b33fe77790009aeb:1">`str.index`</span><span data-offset-key="9c60dd3227a343d7b33fe77790009aeb:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="9c60dd3227a343d7b33fe77790009aeb:3">*sub*</span><span data-offset-key="9c60dd3227a343d7b33fe77790009aeb:4">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="9c60dd3227a343d7b33fe77790009aeb:5">*start*</span><span data-offset-key="9c60dd3227a343d7b33fe77790009aeb:6">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="9c60dd3227a343d7b33fe77790009aeb:7">*end*</span><span data-offset-key="9c60dd3227a343d7b33fe77790009aeb:8">\]\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="245d21701a0b40acbcba8b6c4ab1859e"><span data-offset-key="245d21701a0b40acbcba8b6c4ab1859e:0">Like </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str.find" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8ade5159018840d399c05c3df48d54d6"><span data-offset-key="8ade5159018840d399c05c3df48d54d6:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">find()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f543dd13a9ff4815bda29f7fb1920c6b"><span data-offset-key="f543dd13a9ff4815bda29f7fb1920c6b:0">, but raise </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#ValueError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1d5f1f2ac5ef4a869282ee013e5c3121"><span data-offset-key="1d5f1f2ac5ef4a869282ee013e5c3121:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">ValueError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ddbbd81783b74eb5ac4220af1cec90fe"><span data-offset-key="ddbbd81783b74eb5ac4220af1cec90fe:0"> when the substring is not found.</span><span data-offset-key="ddbbd81783b74eb5ac4220af1cec90fe:1">`str.isalnum`</span><span data-offset-key="ddbbd81783b74eb5ac4220af1cec90fe:2">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="747ce1257e514eebaf577cfcd875af68"><span data-offset-key="747ce1257e514eebaf577cfcd875af68:0">Return </span><span data-offset-key="747ce1257e514eebaf577cfcd875af68:1">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="747ce1257e514eebaf577cfcd875af68:2"> if all characters in the string are alphanumeric and there is at least one character, </span><span data-offset-key="747ce1257e514eebaf577cfcd875af68:3">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="747ce1257e514eebaf577cfcd875af68:4"> otherwise. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1eda100b59c14dfcba7d72ff978c298f"><span data-offset-key="1eda100b59c14dfcba7d72ff978c298f:0">Return </span><span data-offset-key="1eda100b59c14dfcba7d72ff978c298f:1">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="1eda100b59c14dfcba7d72ff978c298f:2"> if all characters in the string are alphabetic and there is at least one character, </span><span data-offset-key="1eda100b59c14dfcba7d72ff978c298f:3">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="1eda100b59c14dfcba7d72ff978c298f:4"> otherwise. Note that this is different from the “Alphabetic” property defined in the Unicode Standard.</span><span data-offset-key="1eda100b59c14dfcba7d72ff978c298f:5">`str.isascii`</span><span data-offset-key="1eda100b59c14dfcba7d72ff978c298f:6">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d211d8554bd34129a3533d4b34bc16a7"><span data-offset-key="d211d8554bd34129a3533d4b34bc16a7:0">Return </span><span data-offset-key="d211d8554bd34129a3533d4b34bc16a7:1">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="d211d8554bd34129a3533d4b34bc16a7:2"> if the string is empty or all characters in the string are ASCII, </span><span data-offset-key="d211d8554bd34129a3533d4b34bc16a7:3">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="d211d8554bd34129a3533d4b34bc16a7:4"> otherwise. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b8cbe9eaf67e4080b93fd08ccc90d9b6"><span data-offset-key="b8cbe9eaf67e4080b93fd08ccc90d9b6:0">New in version 3.7.</span><span data-offset-key="b8cbe9eaf67e4080b93fd08ccc90d9b6:1">`str.isdecimal`</span><span data-offset-key="b8cbe9eaf67e4080b93fd08ccc90d9b6:2">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3d043cb7ffd14ad7956fd6b5d3138fea"><span data-offset-key="3d043cb7ffd14ad7956fd6b5d3138fea:0">Return </span><span data-offset-key="3d043cb7ffd14ad7956fd6b5d3138fea:1">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="3d043cb7ffd14ad7956fd6b5d3138fea:2"> if all characters in the string are decimal characters and there is at least one character, </span><span data-offset-key="3d043cb7ffd14ad7956fd6b5d3138fea:3">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="3d043cb7ffd14ad7956fd6b5d3138fea:4"> otherwise. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fb91f7363a074a4abe1ca4c79210fe3e"><span data-offset-key="fb91f7363a074a4abe1ca4c79210fe3e:0">Return </span><span data-offset-key="fb91f7363a074a4abe1ca4c79210fe3e:1">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="fb91f7363a074a4abe1ca4c79210fe3e:2"> if all characters in the string are digits and there is at least one character, </span><span data-offset-key="fb91f7363a074a4abe1ca4c79210fe3e:3">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="fb91f7363a074a4abe1ca4c79210fe3e:4"> otherwise. Digits include decimal characters and digits that need special handling, such as the compatibility superscript digits. This covers digits which cannot be used to form numbers in base 10, like the Kharosthi numbers. Formally, a digit is a character that has the property value Numeric\_Type=Digit or Numeric\_Type=Decimal.</span><span data-offset-key="fb91f7363a074a4abe1ca4c79210fe3e:5">`str.isidentifier`</span><span data-offset-key="fb91f7363a074a4abe1ca4c79210fe3e:6">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2b792160b9cf47ab949e7cddcd695d8e"><span data-offset-key="2b792160b9cf47ab949e7cddcd695d8e:0">Return </span><span data-offset-key="2b792160b9cf47ab949e7cddcd695d8e:1">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="2b792160b9cf47ab949e7cddcd695d8e:2"> if the string is a valid identifier according to the language definition, section </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/lexical_analysis.html#identifiers" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bf804f9fd57b40a7a2d9fcc65ba19690"><span data-offset-key="bf804f9fd57b40a7a2d9fcc65ba19690:0">Identifiers and keywords</span></span></a><span data-key="2dbe1fdf6b3d4888ac74e63479bef9c3"><span data-offset-key="2dbe1fdf6b3d4888ac74e63479bef9c3:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="160d9fc4ec954fffbcc219e4a8183f16"><span data-offset-key="160d9fc4ec954fffbcc219e4a8183f16:0">Call </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/keyword.html#keyword.iskeyword" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c979877fe1dc4b6b98eab10a6f8ae205"><span data-offset-key="c979877fe1dc4b6b98eab10a6f8ae205:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">keyword.iskeyword()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="e2b99f52aa9f4cf9a2835b7ab966be87"><span data-offset-key="e2b99f52aa9f4cf9a2835b7ab966be87:0"> to test whether string </span><span data-offset-key="e2b99f52aa9f4cf9a2835b7ab966be87:1">`s`</span><span data-offset-key="e2b99f52aa9f4cf9a2835b7ab966be87:2"> is a reserved identifier, such as </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/compound_stmts.html#def" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5b66cd19c8ca4baa9ef9423bd018e902"><span data-offset-key="5b66cd19c8ca4baa9ef9423bd018e902:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">def</code></span></span></a><span data-key="4eba731fabb24a96a49d07cec116d47e"><span data-offset-key="4eba731fabb24a96a49d07cec116d47e:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/compound_stmts.html#class" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5a5842bbe40649728642f9a932387300"><span data-offset-key="5a5842bbe40649728642f9a932387300:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">class</code></span></span></a><span data-key="706f3df29bdc4604b53390de2b8a1a22"><span data-offset-key="706f3df29bdc4604b53390de2b8a1a22:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f5578d81c179429ea90b24b6b4d9f5a6"><span data-offset-key="f5578d81c179429ea90b24b6b4d9f5a6:0">Example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> from keyword import iskeyword​>>> 'hello'.isidentifier(), iskeyword('hello')True, False>>> 'def'.isidentifier(), iskeyword('def')True, True

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b2c26468c3ce4766af1f9bc5deff7909"><span data-offset-key="b2c26468c3ce4766af1f9bc5deff7909:0">Return </span><span data-offset-key="b2c26468c3ce4766af1f9bc5deff7909:1">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="b2c26468c3ce4766af1f9bc5deff7909:2"> if all characters in the string are numeric characters, and there is at least one character, </span><span data-offset-key="b2c26468c3ce4766af1f9bc5deff7909:3">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="b2c26468c3ce4766af1f9bc5deff7909:4"> otherwise. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e9872adf009d4d979751a2f8df76d710"><span data-offset-key="e9872adf009d4d979751a2f8df76d710:0">Return </span><span data-offset-key="e9872adf009d4d979751a2f8df76d710:1">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="e9872adf009d4d979751a2f8df76d710:2"> if all characters in the string are printable or the string is empty, </span><span data-offset-key="e9872adf009d4d979751a2f8df76d710:3">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="e9872adf009d4d979751a2f8df76d710:4"> otherwise. Nonprintable characters are those characters defined in the Unicode character database as “Other” or “Separator”, excepting the ASCII space (0x20) which is considered printable. (Note that printable characters in this context are those which should not be escaped when </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#repr" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="93e4e2efdb064304a23c0184f6568da5"><span data-offset-key="93e4e2efdb064304a23c0184f6568da5:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">repr()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="1f80c0f5bf1b429ab6dda43cff6bb635"><span data-offset-key="1f80c0f5bf1b429ab6dda43cff6bb635:0"> is invoked on a string. It has no bearing on the handling of strings written to </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.stdout" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5d0f92b94930471ca5a370b96d062322"><span data-offset-key="5d0f92b94930471ca5a370b96d062322:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.stdout</code></span></span></a><span data-key="97fb068b3a604cba9d27262400f1c99f"><span data-offset-key="97fb068b3a604cba9d27262400f1c99f:0"> or </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.stderr" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5bb22e1e56cc4c04988eb70de8864434"><span data-offset-key="5bb22e1e56cc4c04988eb70de8864434:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.stderr</code></span></span></a><span data-key="c9030707cda54b04a15c6e1bbf533e9a"><span data-offset-key="c9030707cda54b04a15c6e1bbf533e9a:0">.)</span><span data-offset-key="c9030707cda54b04a15c6e1bbf533e9a:1">`str.isspace`</span><span data-offset-key="c9030707cda54b04a15c6e1bbf533e9a:2">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5c790f73530046289ae80137333a97be"><span data-offset-key="5c790f73530046289ae80137333a97be:0">A character is </span><span data-offset-key="5c790f73530046289ae80137333a97be:1">*whitespace*</span><span data-offset-key="5c790f73530046289ae80137333a97be:2"> if in the Unicode character database (see </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/unicodedata.html#module-unicodedata" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ff976929fecd4443a9bd61467fc9902f"><span data-offset-key="ff976929fecd4443a9bd61467fc9902f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">unicodedata</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d323be1f037d4aec90a3dd00bde950c2"><span data-offset-key="d323be1f037d4aec90a3dd00bde950c2:0">), either its general category is </span><span data-offset-key="d323be1f037d4aec90a3dd00bde950c2:1">`Zs`</span><span data-offset-key="d323be1f037d4aec90a3dd00bde950c2:2"> (“Separator, space”), or its bidirectional class is one of </span><span data-offset-key="d323be1f037d4aec90a3dd00bde950c2:3">`WS`</span><span data-offset-key="d323be1f037d4aec90a3dd00bde950c2:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="d323be1f037d4aec90a3dd00bde950c2:5">`B`</span><span data-offset-key="d323be1f037d4aec90a3dd00bde950c2:6">, or </span><span data-offset-key="d323be1f037d4aec90a3dd00bde950c2:7">`S`</span><span data-offset-key="d323be1f037d4aec90a3dd00bde950c2:8">.</span><span data-offset-key="d323be1f037d4aec90a3dd00bde950c2:9">`str.istitle`</span><span data-offset-key="d323be1f037d4aec90a3dd00bde950c2:10">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1bc068983a82457588cd90f4fabd6a23"><span data-offset-key="1bc068983a82457588cd90f4fabd6a23:0">The lowercasing algorithm used is described in section 3.13 of the Unicode Standard.</span><span data-offset-key="1bc068983a82457588cd90f4fabd6a23:1">`str.lstrip`</span><span data-offset-key="1bc068983a82457588cd90f4fabd6a23:2">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="1bc068983a82457588cd90f4fabd6a23:3">*chars*</span><span data-offset-key="1bc068983a82457588cd90f4fabd6a23:4">\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="70656278f1bf426caf6e14cb72cec21a"><span data-offset-key="70656278f1bf426caf6e14cb72cec21a:0">Return a copy of the string with leading characters removed. If omitted or </span><span data-offset-key="70656278f1bf426caf6e14cb72cec21a:3">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="70656278f1bf426caf6e14cb72cec21a:4">, the </span><span data-offset-key="70656278f1bf426caf6e14cb72cec21a:5">*chars*</span><span data-offset-key="70656278f1bf426caf6e14cb72cec21a:6"> argument defaults to removing whitespace.     >>> '   spacious   '.lstrip()'spacious   '>>> 'www.example.com'.lstrip('cmowz.')'example.com'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7a51065abec546feb3c8a3b45a732cb8"><span data-offset-key="7a51065abec546feb3c8a3b45a732cb8:0">See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str.removeprefix" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0d72c02a452a43059f95b872a6f1aa45"><span data-offset-key="0d72c02a452a43059f95b872a6f1aa45:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str.removeprefix()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="932a70366cce4eed9987d49670ac4a43"><span data-offset-key="932a70366cce4eed9987d49670ac4a43:0"> for a method that will remove a single prefix string rather than all of a set of characters. For example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> 'Arthur: three!'.lstrip('Arthur: ')'ee!'>>> 'Arthur: three!'.removeprefix('Arthur: ')'three!'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b1bc19838ff54c24bd4e9a5e51bb0ed8"><span data-offset-key="b1bc19838ff54c24bd4e9a5e51bb0ed8:0">This static method returns a translation table usable for </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str.translate" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4953de5c7b1c49a082b6ba62578f15c2"><span data-offset-key="4953de5c7b1c49a082b6ba62578f15c2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str.translate()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="7037c5c3d2014480bd9be64cc72a62b8"><span data-offset-key="7037c5c3d2014480bd9be64cc72a62b8:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d99304fe955b47328cc3d3922fd8827d"><span data-offset-key="d99304fe955b47328cc3d3922fd8827d:0">If there is only one argument, it must be a dictionary mapping Unicode ordinals (integers) or characters (strings of length 1) to Unicode ordinals, strings (of arbitrary lengths) or </span><span data-offset-key="d99304fe955b47328cc3d3922fd8827d:1">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="d99304fe955b47328cc3d3922fd8827d:2">. Character keys will then be converted to ordinals.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="88507f5249114778b6ebf872259c946d"><span data-offset-key="88507f5249114778b6ebf872259c946d:0">If there are two arguments, they must be strings of equal length, and in the resulting dictionary, each character in x will be mapped to the character at the same position in y. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="19168368dc8a44c1b7e24c330c2ea7bf"><span data-offset-key="19168368dc8a44c1b7e24c330c2ea7bf:0">Return a list of the words in the string, using </span><span data-offset-key="19168368dc8a44c1b7e24c330c2ea7bf:1">*sep*</span><span data-offset-key="19168368dc8a44c1b7e24c330c2ea7bf:2"> as the delimiter string. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1d6719a3bcd34304b1d58a2a212b4f1e"><span data-offset-key="1d6719a3bcd34304b1d58a2a212b4f1e:0">Return a copy of the string with trailing characters removed.
