    >>> '   spacious   '.rstrip()'   spacious'>>> 'mississippi'.rstrip('ipz')'mississ'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0a212037bcb34fc199c17465681d9893"><span data-offset-key="0a212037bcb34fc199c17465681d9893:0">See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str.removesuffix" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="95d7712a8b2c4198a832eb8bc4397ced"><span data-offset-key="95d7712a8b2c4198a832eb8bc4397ced:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str.removesuffix()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ae6fefe90c804960bf2691c8bf518287"><span data-offset-key="ae6fefe90c804960bf2691c8bf518287:0"> for a method that will remove a single suffix string rather than all of a set of characters. For example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> 'Monty Python'.rstrip(' Python')'M'>>> 'Monty Python'.removesuffix(' Python')'Monty'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="db56a1908a6e496fac7421fe08764d8d"><span data-offset-key="db56a1908a6e496fac7421fe08764d8d:0">`str.split`</span><span data-offset-key="db56a1908a6e496fac7421fe08764d8d:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="db56a1908a6e496fac7421fe08764d8d:2">*sep=None*</span><span data-offset-key="db56a1908a6e496fac7421fe08764d8d:3">, </span><span data-offset-key="db56a1908a6e496fac7421fe08764d8d:4">*maxsplit=-1*</span><span data-offset-key="db56a1908a6e496fac7421fe08764d8d:5">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c03bd2f1311e40fa889c50ba2207688b"><span data-offset-key="c03bd2f1311e40fa889c50ba2207688b:0">Return a list of the words in the string, using </span><span data-offset-key="c03bd2f1311e40fa889c50ba2207688b:1">*sep*</span><span data-offset-key="c03bd2f1311e40fa889c50ba2207688b:2"> as the delimiter string. If </span><span data-offset-key="c03bd2f1311e40fa889c50ba2207688b:3">*maxsplit*</span><span data-offset-key="c03bd2f1311e40fa889c50ba2207688b:4"> is given, at most </span><span data-offset-key="c03bd2f1311e40fa889c50ba2207688b:5">*maxsplit*</span><span data-offset-key="c03bd2f1311e40fa889c50ba2207688b:6"> splits are done (thus, the list will have at most </span><span data-offset-key="c03bd2f1311e40fa889c50ba2207688b:7">`maxsplit+1`</span><span data-offset-key="c03bd2f1311e40fa889c50ba2207688b:8"> elements). If </span><span data-offset-key="c03bd2f1311e40fa889c50ba2207688b:9">*maxsplit*</span><span data-offset-key="c03bd2f1311e40fa889c50ba2207688b:10"> is not specified or </span><span data-offset-key="c03bd2f1311e40fa889c50ba2207688b:11">`-1`</span><span data-offset-key="c03bd2f1311e40fa889c50ba2207688b:12">, then there is no limit on the number of splits (all possible splits are made).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="997f90e9eebb45ac95f75bf26ed5ea43"><span data-offset-key="997f90e9eebb45ac95f75bf26ed5ea43:0">If </span><span data-offset-key="997f90e9eebb45ac95f75bf26ed5ea43:1">*sep*</span><span data-offset-key="997f90e9eebb45ac95f75bf26ed5ea43:2"> is given, consecutive delimiters are not grouped together and are deemed to delimit empty strings (for example, </span><span data-offset-key="997f90e9eebb45ac95f75bf26ed5ea43:3">`'1,,2'.split(',')`</span><span data-offset-key="997f90e9eebb45ac95f75bf26ed5ea43:4"> returns </span><span data-offset-key="997f90e9eebb45ac95f75bf26ed5ea43:5">`['1', '',                                       '2']`</span><span data-offset-key="997f90e9eebb45ac95f75bf26ed5ea43:6">). The </span><span data-offset-key="997f90e9eebb45ac95f75bf26ed5ea43:7">*sep*</span><span data-offset-key="997f90e9eebb45ac95f75bf26ed5ea43:8"> argument may consist of multiple characters (for example, </span><span data-offset-key="997f90e9eebb45ac95f75bf26ed5ea43:9">`'1<>2<>3'.split('<>')`</span><span data-offset-key="997f90e9eebb45ac95f75bf26ed5ea43:10"> returns </span><span data-offset-key="997f90e9eebb45ac95f75bf26ed5ea43:11">`['1', '2',                                       '3']`</span><span data-offset-key="997f90e9eebb45ac95f75bf26ed5ea43:12">). Splitting an empty string with a specified separator returns </span><span data-offset-key="997f90e9eebb45ac95f75bf26ed5ea43:13">`['']`</span><span data-offset-key="997f90e9eebb45ac95f75bf26ed5ea43:14">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="073094961eba4891b9e0ba6e8680f915"><span data-offset-key="073094961eba4891b9e0ba6e8680f915:0">For example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> '1,2,3'.split(',')['1', '2', '3']>>> '1,2,3'.split(',', maxsplit=1)['1', '2,3']>>> '1,2,,3,'.split(',')['1', '2', '', '3', '']

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9e140c81d3fe4e09a8abc8cb2bf207fd"><span data-offset-key="9e140c81d3fe4e09a8abc8cb2bf207fd:0">If </span><span data-offset-key="9e140c81d3fe4e09a8abc8cb2bf207fd:1">*sep*</span><span data-offset-key="9e140c81d3fe4e09a8abc8cb2bf207fd:2"> is not specified or is </span><span data-offset-key="9e140c81d3fe4e09a8abc8cb2bf207fd:3">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="9e140c81d3fe4e09a8abc8cb2bf207fd:4">, a different splitting algorithm is applied: runs of consecutive whitespace are regarded as a single separator, and the result will contain no empty strings at the start or end if the string has leading or trailing whitespace. Consequently, splitting an empty string or a string consisting of just whitespace with a </span><span data-offset-key="9e140c81d3fe4e09a8abc8cb2bf207fd:5">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="9e140c81d3fe4e09a8abc8cb2bf207fd:6"> separator returns </span><span data-offset-key="9e140c81d3fe4e09a8abc8cb2bf207fd:7">`[]`</span><span data-offset-key="9e140c81d3fe4e09a8abc8cb2bf207fd:8">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="75b19c76e96d4b35ae37f6e5a1fbc5d2"><span data-offset-key="75b19c76e96d4b35ae37f6e5a1fbc5d2:0">For example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> '1 2 3'.split()['1', '2', '3']>>> '1 2 3'.split(maxsplit=1)['1', '2 3']>>> '   1   2   3   '.split()['1', '2', '3']

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="cb5915bcd0ea47409fe1a41c16e0e3fd"><span data-offset-key="cb5915bcd0ea47409fe1a41c16e0e3fd:0">`str.splitlines`</span><span data-offset-key="cb5915bcd0ea47409fe1a41c16e0e3fd:1">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="cb5915bcd0ea47409fe1a41c16e0e3fd:2">*keepends*</span><span data-offset-key="cb5915bcd0ea47409fe1a41c16e0e3fd:3">\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c8b415cdbcd84951b104ff0b19e20e33"><span data-offset-key="c8b415cdbcd84951b104ff0b19e20e33:0">Return a list of the lines in the string, breaking at line boundaries. Line breaks are not included in the resulting list unless </span><span data-offset-key="c8b415cdbcd84951b104ff0b19e20e33:1">*keepends*</span><span data-offset-key="c8b415cdbcd84951b104ff0b19e20e33:2"> is given and true.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f7bb71d8d8d34f3ca9ae264752e3ef5d"><span data-offset-key="f7bb71d8d8d34f3ca9ae264752e3ef5d:0">This method splits on the following line boundaries. In particular, the boundaries are a superset of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-universal-newlines" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="beaab7d4052e449db0ee596ff6a495ce"><span data-offset-key="beaab7d4052e449db0ee596ff6a495ce:0">universal newlines</span></span></a><span data-key="0629ae061d47435cb97097103365dd11"><span data-offset-key="0629ae061d47435cb97097103365dd11:0">.</span></span></span>

<table><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><tbody><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span data-offset-key="e888618c849840178c69f2b15011d609:0">Representation</span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span Feed</span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-offset-key="828d3777b68841f9a54aed77295a899f:1"> or </span><span data-offset-key="828d3777b68841f9a54aed77295a899f:2"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-offset-key="cb8f9b46eb8d4d9da5c69ed0219b7592:2"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">\x0c</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: Feed</span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-slate-leaf="true">\x1c</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span Separator</span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e84d1e78d1d24222a654c2b4ddd00e97"><span data-offset-key="e84d1e78d1d24222a654c2b4ddd00e97:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">\x1e</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ec4871db590447c4b2940119cd2eee38"><span data-offset-key="ec4871db590447c4b2940119cd2eee38:0">Record Separator</span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="even"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e208003cd04447fba1f23e43ddb87f53"><span data-offset-key="e208003cd04447fba1f23e43ddb87f53:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">\x85</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="00c1eabdb87a483c8d3af3c99df904b4"><span data-offset-key="00c1eabdb87a483c8d3af3c99df904b4:0">Next Line (C1 Control Code)</span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f3815565661547aa85661af9fae496ba"><span data-offset-key="f3815565661547aa85661af9fae496ba:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">\u2028</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3e297457724d449ab38a35a8936ec514"><span data-offset-key="3e297457724d449ab38a35a8936ec514:0">Line Separator</span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="even"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a270cc06d11d4bdca92d98b7f9fd9b29"><span data-offset-key="a270cc06d11d4bdca92d98b7f9fd9b29:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">\u2029</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4915a5ee26b24d8db959acd043aae128"><span data-offset-key="4915a5ee26b24d8db959acd043aae128:0">Paragraph Separator</span></span></span></p></td></tr></tbody></table>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="53c49574c9bf42099f6d874ffce4a3ee"><span data-offset-key="53c49574c9bf42099f6d874ffce4a3ee:0">Changed in version 3.2: </span><span data-offset-key="53c49574c9bf42099f6d874ffce4a3ee:1">`\v`</span><span data-offset-key="53c49574c9bf42099f6d874ffce4a3ee:2"> and </span><span data-offset-key="53c49574c9bf42099f6d874ffce4a3ee:3">`\f`</span><span data-offset-key="53c49574c9bf42099f6d874ffce4a3ee:4"> added to list of line boundaries.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="17267600bed144559d74b768d464ddfd"><span data-offset-key="17267600bed144559d74b768d464ddfd:0">For example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> 'ab c\n\nde fg\rkl\r\n'.splitlines()['ab c', '', 'de fg', 'kl']>>> 'ab c\n\nde fg\rkl\r\n'.splitlines(keepends=True)['ab c\n', '\n', 'de fg\r', 'kl\r\n']

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="263772e06fe041d59daefac4db35447d"><span data-offset-key="263772e06fe041d59daefac4db35447d:0">Unlike </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str.split" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e69fa15c233b44698d40a22e252efe7b"><span data-offset-key="e69fa15c233b44698d40a22e252efe7b:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">split()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a6f35d60cdfa4a659ae4a0c3831157dc"><span data-offset-key="a6f35d60cdfa4a659ae4a0c3831157dc:0"> when a delimiter string </span><span data-offset-key="a6f35d60cdfa4a659ae4a0c3831157dc:1">*sep*</span><span data-offset-key="a6f35d60cdfa4a659ae4a0c3831157dc:2"> is given, this method returns an empty list for the empty string, and a terminal line break does not result in an extra line:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> "".splitlines()[]>>> "One line\n".splitlines()['One line']

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2b3b3d2c81094e3ca3a1595d43adade0"><span data-offset-key="2b3b3d2c81094e3ca3a1595d43adade0:0">For comparison, </span><span data-offset-key="2b3b3d2c81094e3ca3a1595d43adade0:1">`split('\n')`</span><span data-offset-key="2b3b3d2c81094e3ca3a1595d43adade0:2"> gives:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> ''.split('\n')['']>>> 'Two lines\n'.split('\n')['Two lines', '']

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="cbbfc5c3893749f7bbcfcb75c5a3ee2e"><span data-offset-key="cbbfc5c3893749f7bbcfcb75c5a3ee2e:0">`str.startswith`</span><span data-offset-key="cbbfc5c3893749f7bbcfcb75c5a3ee2e:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="cbbfc5c3893749f7bbcfcb75c5a3ee2e:2">*prefix*</span><span data-offset-key="cbbfc5c3893749f7bbcfcb75c5a3ee2e:3">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="cbbfc5c3893749f7bbcfcb75c5a3ee2e:4">*start*</span><span data-offset-key="cbbfc5c3893749f7bbcfcb75c5a3ee2e:5">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="cbbfc5c3893749f7bbcfcb75c5a3ee2e:6">*end*</span><span data-offset-key="cbbfc5c3893749f7bbcfcb75c5a3ee2e:7">\]\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="13f63fa1540547e48b504293cc4f4f16"><span data-offset-key="13f63fa1540547e48b504293cc4f4f16:0">Return </span><span data-offset-key="13f63fa1540547e48b504293cc4f4f16:1">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="13f63fa1540547e48b504293cc4f4f16:2"> if string starts with the </span><span data-offset-key="13f63fa1540547e48b504293cc4f4f16:3">*prefix*</span><span data-offset-key="13f63fa1540547e48b504293cc4f4f16:4">, otherwise return </span><span data-offset-key="13f63fa1540547e48b504293cc4f4f16:5">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="13f63fa1540547e48b504293cc4f4f16:6">. </span><span data-offset-key="13f63fa1540547e48b504293cc4f4f16:7">*prefix*</span><span data-offset-key="13f63fa1540547e48b504293cc4f4f16:8"> can also be a tuple of prefixes to look for. With optional </span><span data-offset-key="13f63fa1540547e48b504293cc4f4f16:9">*start*</span><span data-offset-key="13f63fa1540547e48b504293cc4f4f16:10">, test string beginning at that position. With optional </span><span data-offset-key="13f63fa1540547e48b504293cc4f4f16:11">*end*</span><span data-offset-key="13f63fa1540547e48b504293cc4f4f16:12">, stop comparing string at that position.</span><span data-offset-key="13f63fa1540547e48b504293cc4f4f16:13">`str.strip`</span><span data-offset-key="13f63fa1540547e48b504293cc4f4f16:14">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="13f63fa1540547e48b504293cc4f4f16:15">*chars*</span><span data-offset-key="13f63fa1540547e48b504293cc4f4f16:16">\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6ed456eeb5e0483fab27fa89a1882e62"><span data-offset-key="6ed456eeb5e0483fab27fa89a1882e62:0">Return a copy of the string with the leading and trailing characters removed. The </span><span data-offset-key="6ed456eeb5e0483fab27fa89a1882e62:1">*chars*</span><span data-offset-key="6ed456eeb5e0483fab27fa89a1882e62:2"> argument is a string specifying the set of characters to be removed. If omitted or </span><span data-offset-key="6ed456eeb5e0483fab27fa89a1882e62:3">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="6ed456eeb5e0483fab27fa89a1882e62:4">, the </span><span data-offset-key="6ed456eeb5e0483fab27fa89a1882e62:5">*chars*</span><span data-offset-key="6ed456eeb5e0483fab27fa89a1882e62:6"> argument defaults to removing whitespace. The </span><span data-offset-key="6ed456eeb5e0483fab27fa89a1882e62:7">*chars*</span><span data-offset-key="6ed456eeb5e0483fab27fa89a1882e62:8"> argument is not a prefix or suffix; rather, all combinations of its values are stripped:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> '   spacious   '.strip()'spacious'>>> 'www.example.com'.strip('cmowz.')'example'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2ea59641b3b046d58501053205e9a954"><span data-offset-key="2ea59641b3b046d58501053205e9a954:0">The outermost leading and trailing </span><span data-offset-key="2ea59641b3b046d58501053205e9a954:1">*chars*</span><span data-offset-key="2ea59641b3b046d58501053205e9a954:2"> argument values are stripped from the string. Characters are removed from the leading end until reaching a string character that is not contained in the set of characters in </span><span data-offset-key="2ea59641b3b046d58501053205e9a954:3">*chars*</span><span data-offset-key="2ea59641b3b046d58501053205e9a954:4">. A similar action takes place on the trailing end. For example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> comment_string = '#....... Section 3.2.1 Issue #32 .......'>>> comment_string.strip('.#! ')'Section 3.2.1 Issue #32'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d93dcdcd0395499f97f26ab4fd40a64d"><span data-offset-key="d93dcdcd0395499f97f26ab4fd40a64d:0">`str.swapcase`</span><span data-offset-key="d93dcdcd0395499f97f26ab4fd40a64d:1">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2e43700e22c042a5b990437dca29a739"><span data-offset-key="2e43700e22c042a5b990437dca29a739:0">Return a copy of the string with uppercase characters converted to lowercase and vice versa. Note that it is not necessarily true that </span><span data-offset-key="2e43700e22c042a5b990437dca29a739:1">`s.swapcase().swapcase() == s`</span><span data-offset-key="2e43700e22c042a5b990437dca29a739:2">.</span><span data-offset-key="2e43700e22c042a5b990437dca29a739:3">`str.title`</span><span data-offset-key="2e43700e22c042a5b990437dca29a739:4">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f56223c855514c4ea32ccf208d3b6299"><span data-offset-key="f56223c855514c4ea32ccf208d3b6299:0">Return a titlecased version of the string where words start with an uppercase character and the remaining characters are lowercase.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="39997cacd33e46bc93c9852f7297dc43"><span data-offset-key="39997cacd33e46bc93c9852f7297dc43:0">For example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> 'Hello world'.title()'Hello World'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2c3e75eaa0164734aedee82dfb5ebb93"><span data-offset-key="2c3e75eaa0164734aedee82dfb5ebb93:0">The algorithm uses a simple language-independent definition of a word as groups of consecutive letters. The definition works in many contexts but it means that apostrophes in contractions and possessives form word boundaries, which may not be the desired result:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> "they're bill's friends from the UK".title()"They'Re Bill'S Friends From The Uk"

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9c1e2c49e95046f28c845d7e4a142dea"><span data-offset-key="9c1e2c49e95046f28c845d7e4a142dea:0">A workaround for apostrophes can be constructed using regular expressions:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> import re>>> def titlecase(s):...     return re.sub(r"[A-Za-z]+('[A-Za-z]+)?",...                   lambda mo: mo.group(0).capitalize(),...                   s)...>>> titlecase("they're bill's friends.")"They're Bill's Friends."

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="67ebf7945a564f4db41caa2741177f69"><span data-offset-key="67ebf7945a564f4db41caa2741177f69:0">`str.translate`</span><span data-offset-key="67ebf7945a564f4db41caa2741177f69:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="67ebf7945a564f4db41caa2741177f69:2">*table*</span><span data-offset-key="67ebf7945a564f4db41caa2741177f69:3">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="23bbd4e8579f48e5a9fc8bc2de95dfb8"><span data-offset-key="23bbd4e8579f48e5a9fc8bc2de95dfb8:0">Return a copy of the string in which each character has been mapped through the given translation table. The table must be an object that implements indexing via </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__getitem__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="297289e8fcba4547982eeaeab6dc6623"><span data-offset-key="297289e8fcba4547982eeaeab6dc6623:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__getitem__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="30884a6c0bc5437db0b4b32d0fa44a56"><span data-offset-key="30884a6c0bc5437db0b4b32d0fa44a56:0">, typically a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-mapping" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b530b0a30fac465999bc984dd7cb20b0"><span data-offset-key="b530b0a30fac465999bc984dd7cb20b0:0">mapping</span></span></a><span data-key="a73667345c2d443fa130f818c96d4fd5"><span data-offset-key="a73667345c2d443fa130f818c96d4fd5:0"> or </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-sequence" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="fe1af104b7c148e0bb138102edfd850d"><span data-offset-key="fe1af104b7c148e0bb138102edfd850d:0">sequence</span></span></a><span data-key="17818ac663ff4b6a88706b8d3a7b1a0d"><span data-offset-key="17818ac663ff4b6a88706b8d3a7b1a0d:0">. When indexed by a Unicode ordinal (an integer), the table object can do any of the following: return a Unicode ordinal or a string, to map the character to one or more other characters; return </span><span data-offset-key="17818ac663ff4b6a88706b8d3a7b1a0d:1">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="17818ac663ff4b6a88706b8d3a7b1a0d:2">, to delete the character from the return string; or raise a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#LookupError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a87de1299f2342c5aa5bdac81bfd532b"><span data-offset-key="a87de1299f2342c5aa5bdac81bfd532b:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">LookupError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="716fc7c47e5545fd93023368067230ff"><span data-offset-key="716fc7c47e5545fd93023368067230ff:0"> exception, to map the character to itself.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="60358e613d5f4eca99947241baf570ce"><span data-offset-key="60358e613d5f4eca99947241baf570ce:0">You can use </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str.maketrans" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b96004b28200452f815438a9f35a42ff"><span data-offset-key="b96004b28200452f815438a9f35a42ff:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str.maketrans()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="2fc6a588a76241d58010b2081fa15277"><span data-offset-key="2fc6a588a76241d58010b2081fa15277:0"> to create a translation map from character-to-character mappings in different formats.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b5fd4b6fffe24382a85febd786423843"><span data-offset-key="b5fd4b6fffe24382a85febd786423843:0">See also the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/codecs.html#module-codecs" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ae5deaa8b1634e3e972e9525d5e251af"><span data-offset-key="ae5deaa8b1634e3e972e9525d5e251af:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">codecs</code></span></span></a><span data-key="274135d1d4f44623a6491937b95c306e"><span data-offset-key="274135d1d4f44623a6491937b95c306e:0"> module for a more flexible approach to custom character mappings.</span><span data-offset-key="274135d1d4f44623a6491937b95c306e:1">`str.upper`</span><span data-offset-key="274135d1d4f44623a6491937b95c306e:2">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="11e3e04260ea4b3cb826e88714f24408"><span data-offset-key="11e3e04260ea4b3cb826e88714f24408:0">Return a copy of the string with all the cased characters </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#id15" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="beaf2386c0da45faa58a0640a42ea585"><span data-offset-key="beaf2386c0da45faa58a0640a42ea585:0">4</span></span></a><span data-key="4890a7ae40654367b342ce83147704ab"><span data-offset-key="4890a7ae40654367b342ce83147704ab:0"> converted to uppercase. Note that </span><span data-offset-key="4890a7ae40654367b342ce83147704ab:1">`s.upper().isupper()`</span><span data-offset-key="4890a7ae40654367b342ce83147704ab:2"> might be </span><span data-offset-key="4890a7ae40654367b342ce83147704ab:3">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="4890a7ae40654367b342ce83147704ab:4"> if </span><span data-offset-key="4890a7ae40654367b342ce83147704ab:5">`s`</span><span data-offset-key="4890a7ae40654367b342ce83147704ab:6"> contains uncased characters or if the Unicode category of the resulting character(s) is not “Lu” (Letter, uppercase), but e.g. “Lt” (Letter, titlecase).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6b26c52f60c34f839c312bd2ecdcd5fc"><span data-offset-key="6b26c52f60c34f839c312bd2ecdcd5fc:0">The uppercasing algorithm used is described in section 3.13 of the Unicode Standard.</span><span data-offset-key="6b26c52f60c34f839c312bd2ecdcd5fc:1">`str.zfill`</span><span data-offset-key="6b26c52f60c34f839c312bd2ecdcd5fc:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="6b26c52f60c34f839c312bd2ecdcd5fc:3">*width*</span><span data-offset-key="6b26c52f60c34f839c312bd2ecdcd5fc:4">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9e0236ff292648ff81be13d136ce2682"><span data-offset-key="9e0236ff292648ff81be13d136ce2682:0">Return a copy of the string left filled with ASCII </span><span data-offset-key="9e0236ff292648ff81be13d136ce2682:1">`'0'`</span><span data-offset-key="9e0236ff292648ff81be13d136ce2682:2"> digits to make a string of length </span><span data-offset-key="9e0236ff292648ff81be13d136ce2682:3">*width*</span><span data-offset-key="9e0236ff292648ff81be13d136ce2682:4">. A leading sign prefix (</span><span data-offset-key="9e0236ff292648ff81be13d136ce2682:5">`'+'`</span><span data-offset-key="9e0236ff292648ff81be13d136ce2682:6">/</span><span data-offset-key="9e0236ff292648ff81be13d136ce2682:7">`'-'`</span><span data-offset-key="9e0236ff292648ff81be13d136ce2682:8">) is handled by inserting the padding </span><span data-offset-key="9e0236ff292648ff81be13d136ce2682:9">*after*</span><span data-offset-key="9e0236ff292648ff81be13d136ce2682:10"> the sign character rather than before. The original string is returned if </span><span data-offset-key="9e0236ff292648ff81be13d136ce2682:11">*width*</span><span data-offset-key="9e0236ff292648ff81be13d136ce2682:12"> is less than or equal to </span><span data-offset-key="9e0236ff292648ff81be13d136ce2682:13">`len(s)`</span><span data-offset-key="9e0236ff292648ff81be13d136ce2682:14">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="bcf9573cd9d94423a43c426a36dfe5c1"><span data-offset-key="bcf9573cd9d94423a43c426a36dfe5c1:0">For example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> "42".zfill(5)'00042'>>> "-42".zfill(5)'-0042'

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9cd1c0432cd54b378bc9c8dc5a384452"><span data-offset-key="9cd1c0432cd54b378bc9c8dc5a384452:0">`printf`</span><span data-offset-key="9cd1c0432cd54b378bc9c8dc5a384452:1">-style String Formatting</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1bd491f9967e4e9a9cb9ac8a504e03ec"><span data-offset-key="1bd491f9967e4e9a9cb9ac8a504e03ec:0">Note </span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b831af885806468fa9f1262b1ce57257"><span data-offset-key="b831af885806468fa9f1262b1ce57257:0">The formatting operations described here exhibit a variety of quirks that lead to a number of common errors (such as failing to display tuples and dictionaries correctly). Using the newer </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/lexical_analysis.html#f-strings" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="efc32b3d88924f4b9f93ea87eec67778"><span data-offset-key="efc32b3d88924f4b9f93ea87eec67778:0">formatted string literals</span></span></a><span data-key="12cc2a0d3de5476581f27d8b77b2e2c2"><span data-offset-key="12cc2a0d3de5476581f27d8b77b2e2c2:0">, the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str.format" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a5736ddae3434a359577ed49496204d2"><span data-offset-key="a5736ddae3434a359577ed49496204d2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str.format()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="95510a8eefc949ed8d088e566de45499"><span data-offset-key="95510a8eefc949ed8d088e566de45499:0"> interface, or </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/string.html#template-strings" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e6f07e88aec14e0cb024a40025025265"><span data-offset-key="e6f07e88aec14e0cb024a40025025265:0">template strings</span></span></a><span data-key="42f33eb5c045442f98317a3c06f1dce5"><span data-offset-key="42f33eb5c045442f98317a3c06f1dce5:0"> may help avoid these errors. Each of these alternatives provides their own trade-offs and benefits of simplicity, flexibility, and/or extensibility.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3afc2f98df1b4442aa78ca93e6f2a017"><span data-offset-key="3afc2f98df1b4442aa78ca93e6f2a017:0">String objects have one unique built-in operation: the </span><span data-offset-key="3afc2f98df1b4442aa78ca93e6f2a017:1">`%`</span><span data-offset-key="3afc2f98df1b4442aa78ca93e6f2a017:2"> operator (modulo). This is also known as the string </span><span data-offset-key="3afc2f98df1b4442aa78ca93e6f2a017:3">*formatting*</span><span data-offset-key="3afc2f98df1b4442aa78ca93e6f2a017:4"> or </span><span data-offset-key="3afc2f98df1b4442aa78ca93e6f2a017:5">*interpolation*</span><span data-offset-key="3afc2f98df1b4442aa78ca93e6f2a017:6"> operator. Given </span><span data-offset-key="3afc2f98df1b4442aa78ca93e6f2a017:7">`format % values`</span><span data-offset-key="3afc2f98df1b4442aa78ca93e6f2a017:8"> (where </span><span data-offset-key="3afc2f98df1b4442aa78ca93e6f2a017:9">*format*</span><span data-offset-key="3afc2f98df1b4442aa78ca93e6f2a017:10"> is a string), </span><span data-offset-key="3afc2f98df1b4442aa78ca93e6f2a017:11">`%`</span><span data-offset-key="3afc2f98df1b4442aa78ca93e6f2a017:12"> conversion specifications in </span><span data-offset-key="3afc2f98df1b4442aa78ca93e6f2a017:13">*format*</span><span data-offset-key="3afc2f98df1b4442aa78ca93e6f2a017:14"> are replaced with zero or more elements of </span><span data-offset-key="3afc2f98df1b4442aa78ca93e6f2a017:15">*values*</span><span data-offset-key="3afc2f98df1b4442aa78ca93e6f2a017:16">. The effect is similar to using the </span><span data-offset-key="3afc2f98df1b4442aa78ca93e6f2a017:17">`sprintf()`</span><span data-offset-key="3afc2f98df1b4442aa78ca93e6f2a017:18"> in the C language.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1207d58605954d929de5c7a190b56731"><span data-offset-key="1207d58605954d929de5c7a190b56731:0">If </span><span data-offset-key="1207d58605954d929de5c7a190b56731:1">*format*</span><span data-offset-key="1207d58605954d929de5c7a190b56731:2"> requires a single argument, </span><span data-offset-key="1207d58605954d929de5c7a190b56731:3">*values*</span><span data-offset-key="1207d58605954d929de5c7a190b56731:4"> may be a single non-tuple object. </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#id16" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0b7ba557c9a3466cbe424d388e03d500"><span data-offset-key="0b7ba557c9a3466cbe424d388e03d500:0">5</span></span></a><span data-key="a3460249c00e44e499af694d9ba582f8"><span data-offset-key="a3460249c00e44e499af694d9ba582f8:0"> Otherwise, </span><span data-offset-key="a3460249c00e44e499af694d9ba582f8:1">*values*</span><span data-offset-key="a3460249c00e44e499af694d9ba582f8:2"> must be a tuple with exactly the number of items specified by the format string, or a single mapping object (for example, a dictionary).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="77b073d466a143b0911452ecab10d3c7"><span data-offset-key="77b073d466a143b0911452ecab10d3c7:0">A conversion specifier contains two or more characters and has the following components, which must occur in this order:</span></span></span>

1.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="bcd56ede6dd046b69d8ce0198b5b6289"><span data-offset-key="bcd56ede6dd046b69d8ce0198b5b6289:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="bcd56ede6dd046b69d8ce0198b5b6289:1">`'%'`</span><span data-offset-key="bcd56ede6dd046b69d8ce0198b5b6289:2"> character, which marks the start of the specifier.</span></span></span>

2.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5ee0602bb72d4ff1a3c655d993ea44a7"><span data-offset-key="5ee0602bb72d4ff1a3c655d993ea44a7:0">Mapping key (optional), consisting of a parenthesised sequence of characters (for example, </span><span data-offset-key="5ee0602bb72d4ff1a3c655d993ea44a7:1">`(somename)`</span><span data-offset-key="5ee0602bb72d4ff1a3c655d993ea44a7:2">).</span></span></span>

3.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="24bc17bd5448460fac5e0155905288b3"><span data-offset-key="24bc17bd5448460fac5e0155905288b3:0">Conversion flags (optional), which affect the result of some conversion types.</span></span></span>

4.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3c9e02190c9446b5b31b6d3fe4c05c03"><span data-offset-key="3c9e02190c9446b5b31b6d3fe4c05c03:0">Minimum field width (optional). If specified as an </span><span data-offset-key="3c9e02190c9446b5b31b6d3fe4c05c03:1">`'*'`</span><span data-offset-key="3c9e02190c9446b5b31b6d3fe4c05c03:2"> (asterisk), the actual width is read from the next element of the tuple in </span><span data-offset-key="3c9e02190c9446b5b31b6d3fe4c05c03:3">*values*</span><span data-offset-key="3c9e02190c9446b5b31b6d3fe4c05c03:4">, and the object to convert comes after the minimum field width and optional precision.</span></span></span>

5.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="dfc701d193e94388ab4a288ef173640e"><span data-offset-key="dfc701d193e94388ab4a288ef173640e:0">Precision (optional), given as a </span><span data-offset-key="dfc701d193e94388ab4a288ef173640e:1">`'.'`</span><span data-offset-key="dfc701d193e94388ab4a288ef173640e:2"> (dot) followed by the precision. If specified as </span><span data-offset-key="dfc701d193e94388ab4a288ef173640e:3">`'*'`</span><span data-offset-key="dfc701d193e94388ab4a288ef173640e:4"> (an asterisk), the actual precision is read from the next element of the tuple in </span><span data-offset-key="dfc701d193e94388ab4a288ef173640e:5">*values*</span><span data-offset-key="dfc701d193e94388ab4a288ef173640e:6">, and the value to convert comes after the precision.</span></span></span>

6.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="18f524cf0bf44696a82334e4dee62451"><span data-offset-key="18f524cf0bf44696a82334e4dee62451:0">Length modifier (optional).</span></span></span>

7.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ad44221f3dc541239b77585b2e45a1b2"><span data-offset-key="ad44221f3dc541239b77585b2e45a1b2:0">Conversion type.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="77c70328a68a4c69a56ad425c162db93"><span data-offset-key="77c70328a68a4c69a56ad425c162db93:0">When the right argument is a dictionary (or other mapping type), then the formats in the string </span><span data-offset-key="77c70328a68a4c69a56ad425c162db93:1">*must*</span><span data-offset-key="77c70328a68a4c69a56ad425c162db93:2"> include a parenthesised mapping key into that dictionary inserted immediately after the </span><span data-offset-key="77c70328a68a4c69a56ad425c162db93:3">`'%'`</span><span data-offset-key="77c70328a68a4c69a56ad425c162db93:4"> character. The mapping key selects the value to be formatted from the mapping. For example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> print('%(language)s has %(number)03d quote types.' %...       {'language': "Python", "number": 2})Python has 002 quote types.

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2b3fceb7e0514445a21e8d785eba8cb2"><span data-offset-key="2b3fceb7e0514445a21e8d785eba8cb2:0">In this case no </span><span data-offset-key="2b3fceb7e0514445a21e8d785eba8cb2:1">`*`</span><span data-offset-key="2b3fceb7e0514445a21e8d785eba8cb2:2"> specifiers may occur in a format (since they require a sequential parameter list).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="cf502b59f38a46a295b4ade238d2192e"><span data-offset-key="cf502b59f38a46a295b4ade238d2192e:0">The conversion flag characters are:</span></span></span>

<table><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><tbody><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span zero padded for numeric values.</span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="even"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span conversion if both are given).</span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span '</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span will precede the conversion (overrides a “space” flag).</span></span></span></p></td></tr></tbody></table>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e173da09c30a42b898714cc21955d9a0"><span data-offset-key="e173da09c30a42b898714cc21955d9a0:0">A length modifier (</span><span data-offset-key="e173da09c30a42b898714cc21955d9a0:1">`h`</span><span data-offset-key="e173da09c30a42b898714cc21955d9a0:2">, </span><span data-offset-key="e173da09c30a42b898714cc21955d9a0:3">`l`</span><span data-offset-key="e173da09c30a42b898714cc21955d9a0:4">, or </span><span data-offset-key="e173da09c30a42b898714cc21955d9a0:5">`L`</span><span data-offset-key="e173da09c30a42b898714cc21955d9a0:6">) may be present, but is ignored as it is not necessary for Python – so e.g. </span><span data-offset-key="e173da09c30a42b898714cc21955d9a0:7">`%ld`</span><span data-offset-key="e173da09c30a42b898714cc21955d9a0:8"> is identical to </span><span data-offset-key="e173da09c30a42b898714cc21955d9a0:9">`%d`</span><span data-offset-key="e173da09c30a42b898714cc21955d9a0:10">.</span></span></span>

format.</span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c4d00ff571da4978a6aaa76f9e8d485c"><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9c6a2a92f60b4f688f009c65ee813d2f"><span data-offset-key="9c6a2a92f60b4f688f009c65ee813d2f:0">Floating point format. Uses lowercase exponential format if exponent is less than -4 or not less than precision, decimal format otherwise.</span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="bfb28f21b55f4ecaa3926afa010b5311"><span data-offset-key="bfb28f21b55f4ecaa3926afa010b5311:0">(4)</span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3482995d09a148668b2f68f162a21009"><span data-offset-key="3482995d09a148668b2f68f162a21009:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">'G'</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="403843f268034fd79bb21f013ffd696d"><span data-offset-key="403843f268034fd79bb21f013ffd696d:0">Floating point format. Uses uppercase exponential format if exponent is less than -4 or not less than precision, decimal format otherwise.</span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="afd7fb28e2704215bedf914f7da11fc4"><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2781527458694532911692197ec3e826"><span data-offset-key="2781527458694532911692197ec3e826:0"><code class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="397637c18cd0404e9ad35d7f310a1cd8"><span data-offset-key="397637c18cd0404e9ad35d7f310a1cd8:0">Single character (accepts integer or single character string).</span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a902b13cabb44459a5a556e01a2a4b08"><span data-offset-key="a902b13cabb44459a5a556e01a2a4b08:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="odd"><td (converts any Python object using </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#repr" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-slate-leaf="true">repr()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="44962a292f634457aab64421f3889cc7"><span data-offset-key="44962a292f634457aab64421f3889cc7:0">).</span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7d22d50aeab543f6b25d97f3da58dea6"><span Python object using </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span
