data-slate-leaf="true">str()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="32bdf64b4cdf4e27981320d1b1f25d24"><span data-offset-key="32bdf64b4cdf4e27981320d1b1f25d24:0">).</span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c4e71ee1671f4f3abf886501b46a4319"><span data-offset-key="c4e71ee1671f4f3abf886501b46a4319:0">(5)</span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5b1be32575f440edba1abdf13907afb0"><span data-offset-key="5b1be32575f440edba1abdf13907afb0:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">'a'</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7ba1dd4abcc0499a8a062da34da96b7e"><span data-offset-key="7ba1dd4abcc0499a8a062da34da96b7e:0">String (converts any Python object using </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#ascii" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="205f1325b89b45c98372eef7b839d583"><span data-offset-key="205f1325b89b45c98372eef7b839d583:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">ascii()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d1acc7bdc1e34bb79a852d1231b3b538"><span data-offset-key="d1acc7bdc1e34bb79a852d1231b3b538:0">).</span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3892c86e53a14b00baae7a0cd678dd58"><span data-offset-key="3892c86e53a14b00baae7a0cd678dd58:0">(5)</span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="even"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a724690bb38b44c4a82a61b6588141b1"><span data-offset-key="a724690bb38b44c4a82a61b6588141b1:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">'%'</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="da30cf50343c4d858d7a0ab621911d13"><span data-offset-key="da30cf50343c4d858d7a0ab621911d13:0">No argument is converted, results in a </span><span data-offset-key="da30cf50343c4d858d7a0ab621911d13:1"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">'%'</code></span><span data-offset-key="da30cf50343c4d858d7a0ab621911d13:2"> character in the result.</span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="00abb28a4dfc4999aa7982583a3a2afc"><span data-offset-key="00abb28a4dfc4999aa7982583a3a2afc:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span></span></p></td></tr></tbody></table>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0eb502ed20f343e9a940f3a83183a7ba"><span data-offset-key="0eb502ed20f343e9a940f3a83183a7ba:0">Notes:</span></span></span>

1.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2b11bbeb1f684b0faa2a81c46047e170"><span data-offset-key="2b11bbeb1f684b0faa2a81c46047e170:0">The alternate form causes a leading octal specifier (</span><span data-offset-key="2b11bbeb1f684b0faa2a81c46047e170:1">`'0o'`</span><span data-offset-key="2b11bbeb1f684b0faa2a81c46047e170:2">) to be inserted before the first digit.</span></span></span>

2.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b2aed5d780b1497a9d4329f4ab00d462"><span data-offset-key="b2aed5d780b1497a9d4329f4ab00d462:0">The alternate form causes a leading </span><span data-offset-key="b2aed5d780b1497a9d4329f4ab00d462:1">`'0x'`</span><span data-offset-key="b2aed5d780b1497a9d4329f4ab00d462:2"> or </span><span data-offset-key="b2aed5d780b1497a9d4329f4ab00d462:3">`'0X'`</span><span data-offset-key="b2aed5d780b1497a9d4329f4ab00d462:4"> (depending on whether the </span><span data-offset-key="b2aed5d780b1497a9d4329f4ab00d462:5">`'x'`</span><span data-offset-key="b2aed5d780b1497a9d4329f4ab00d462:6"> or </span><span data-offset-key="b2aed5d780b1497a9d4329f4ab00d462:7">`'X'`</span><span data-offset-key="b2aed5d780b1497a9d4329f4ab00d462:8"> format was used) to be inserted before the first digit.</span></span></span>

3.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="192e014827ee4bf9badaf2b5ddbf7a3a"><span data-offset-key="192e014827ee4bf9badaf2b5ddbf7a3a:0">The alternate form causes the result to always contain a decimal point, even if no digits follow it.</span></span></span>

    <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="24f5b4e67a5547b5ba45dbe6db8aff88"><span data-offset-key="24f5b4e67a5547b5ba45dbe6db8aff88:0">The precision determines the number of digits after the decimal point and defaults to 6.</span></span></span>

4.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1da2f5245a7c4b0fb9ebadea4b43a9eb"><span data-offset-key="1da2f5245a7c4b0fb9ebadea4b43a9eb:0">The alternate form causes the result to always contain a decimal point, and trailing zeroes are not removed as they would otherwise be.</span></span></span>

    <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a486552016d84ab7913e6e117d92a58d"><span data-offset-key="a486552016d84ab7913e6e117d92a58d:0">The precision determines the number of significant digits before and after the decimal point and defaults to 6.</span></span></span>

5.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="97667ca9eee64eec8f2b7d630c204588"><span data-offset-key="97667ca9eee64eec8f2b7d630c204588:0">If precision is </span><span data-offset-key="97667ca9eee64eec8f2b7d630c204588:1">`N`</span><span data-offset-key="97667ca9eee64eec8f2b7d630c204588:2">, the output is truncated to </span><span data-offset-key="97667ca9eee64eec8f2b7d630c204588:3">`N`</span><span data-offset-key="97667ca9eee64eec8f2b7d630c204588:4"> characters.</span></span></span>

6.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a54427c370884e62b33524cdf04e92d4"><span data-offset-key="a54427c370884e62b33524cdf04e92d4:0">See </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0237" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7016ebc36b2e45559ed58175ff1f4262"><span data-offset-key="7016ebc36b2e45559ed58175ff1f4262:0"><strong>PEP 237</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="dbe4355b30b149e784c3a98d02e4ce62"><span data-offset-key="dbe4355b30b149e784c3a98d02e4ce62:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9dfbe2f3ec9141ae873ff655c63547ab"><span data-offset-key="9dfbe2f3ec9141ae873ff655c63547ab:0">Since Python strings have an explicit length, </span><span data-offset-key="9dfbe2f3ec9141ae873ff655c63547ab:1">`%s`</span><span data-offset-key="9dfbe2f3ec9141ae873ff655c63547ab:2"> conversions do not assume that </span><span data-offset-key="9dfbe2f3ec9141ae873ff655c63547ab:3">`'\0'`</span><span data-offset-key="9dfbe2f3ec9141ae873ff655c63547ab:4"> is the end of the string.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2fc22e20bef549efa8da970f1821eeb6"><span data-offset-key="2fc22e20bef549efa8da970f1821eeb6:0">Changed in version 3.1: </span><span data-offset-key="2fc22e20bef549efa8da970f1821eeb6:1">`%f`</span><span data-offset-key="2fc22e20bef549efa8da970f1821eeb6:2"> conversions for numbers whose absolute value is over 1e50 are no longer replaced by </span><span data-offset-key="2fc22e20bef549efa8da970f1821eeb6:3">`%g`</span><span data-offset-key="2fc22e20bef549efa8da970f1821eeb6:4"> conversions.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH600-23f228db--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="05fafe80482c44fab93ad3efb020fc2f"><span data-offset-key="05fafe80482c44fab93ad3efb020fc2f:0">Binary Sequence Types — </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="acdbdaa1a837494c874701565ff46cab"><span data-offset-key="acdbdaa1a837494c874701565ff46cab:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytes</code></span></span></a><span data-key="360367afe0d447e08561e42e947bd61f"><span data-offset-key="360367afe0d447e08561e42e947bd61f:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytearray" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7071396b434d4ca68414fc92ec3f3938"><span data-offset-key="7071396b434d4ca68414fc92ec3f3938:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytearray</code></span></span></a><span data-key="9d163ffc5a334631bfb5563930b30b6b"><span data-offset-key="9d163ffc5a334631bfb5563930b30b6b:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#memoryview" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a1facd85311a457083ef8179f5609273"><span data-offset-key="a1facd85311a457083ef8179f5609273:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">memoryview</code></span></span></a><span data-key="77d72d7068c84a8996e50f5616ba2b9c"><span data-offset-key="77d72d7068c84a8996e50f5616ba2b9c:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="cf06de879a4b482c9227ae25556d5a72"><span data-offset-key="cf06de879a4b482c9227ae25556d5a72:0">The core built-in types for manipulating binary data are </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2ff4118354614147a5ebe85daf1d7f09"><span data-offset-key="2ff4118354614147a5ebe85daf1d7f09:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytes</code></span></span></a><span data-key="c88f5e5619554b6b83f71f1ecbc98c0d"><span data-offset-key="c88f5e5619554b6b83f71f1ecbc98c0d:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytearray" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4c74a00717ac4cd8951221815477f006"><span data-offset-key="4c74a00717ac4cd8951221815477f006:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytearray</code></span></span></a><span data-key="25832d07d77d455e995295b73e3ccd36"><span data-offset-key="25832d07d77d455e995295b73e3ccd36:0">. They are supported by </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#memoryview" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bb5feed038a94a15918b1b82f5b7fe4a"><span data-offset-key="bb5feed038a94a15918b1b82f5b7fe4a:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">memoryview</code></span></span></a><span data-key="cd45abe65b78482494b1f87dd2e750fe"><span data-offset-key="cd45abe65b78482494b1f87dd2e750fe:0"> which uses the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/c-api/buffer.html#bufferobjects" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2763bd84b8914f669b5142c21b196b54"><span data-offset-key="2763bd84b8914f669b5142c21b196b54:0">buffer protocol</span></span></a><span data-key="0a505a7606854f9da3296dc19e6d16c7"><span data-offset-key="0a505a7606854f9da3296dc19e6d16c7:0"> to access the memory of other binary objects without needing to make a copy.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4449a6af89d94d7ca32ef7d154ab61e8"><span data-offset-key="4449a6af89d94d7ca32ef7d154ab61e8:0">The </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/array.html#module-array" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="47f539d78e994d7890990536f57e1aeb"><span data-offset-key="47f539d78e994d7890990536f57e1aeb:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">array</code></span></span></a><span data-key="9090838eab314cd5a816f18944588c4e"><span data-offset-key="9090838eab314cd5a816f18944588c4e:0"> module supports efficient storage of basic data types like 32-bit integers and IEEE754 double-precision floating values.</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6dc54352cf5f413a8f9bf459bbf99429"><span data-offset-key="6dc54352cf5f413a8f9bf459bbf99429:0">Bytes Objects</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e1864d16d84c472db89f38267cc17ce9"><span data-offset-key="e1864d16d84c472db89f38267cc17ce9:0">Bytes objects are immutable sequences of single bytes. Since many major binary protocols are based on the ASCII text encoding, bytes objects offer several methods that are only valid when working with ASCII compatible data and are closely related to string objects in a variety of other ways.</span><span data-offset-key="e1864d16d84c472db89f38267cc17ce9:1">*class* </span><span data-offset-key="e1864d16d84c472db89f38267cc17ce9:2">`bytes`</span><span data-offset-key="e1864d16d84c472db89f38267cc17ce9:3">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="e1864d16d84c472db89f38267cc17ce9:4">*source*</span><span data-offset-key="e1864d16d84c472db89f38267cc17ce9:5">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="e1864d16d84c472db89f38267cc17ce9:6">*encoding*</span><span data-offset-key="e1864d16d84c472db89f38267cc17ce9:7">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="e1864d16d84c472db89f38267cc17ce9:8">*errors*</span><span data-offset-key="e1864d16d84c472db89f38267cc17ce9:9">\]\]\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9dbd7b573b87492298286c39fb6fd86e"><span data-offset-key="9dbd7b573b87492298286c39fb6fd86e:0">Firstly, the syntax for bytes literals is largely the same as that for string literals, except that a </span><span data-offset-key="9dbd7b573b87492298286c39fb6fd86e:1">`b`</span><span data-offset-key="9dbd7b573b87492298286c39fb6fd86e:2"> prefix is added:</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d5e9cd6f550847f49017c94729d032ea"><span data-offset-key="d5e9cd6f550847f49017c94729d032ea:0">Single quotes: </span><span data-offset-key="d5e9cd6f550847f49017c94729d032ea:1">`b'still allows embedded                                             "double"                                             quotes'`</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c5ca37a5d2df4f689039baf078e2b90f"><span data-offset-key="c5ca37a5d2df4f689039baf078e2b90f:0">Double quotes: </span><span data-offset-key="c5ca37a5d2df4f689039baf078e2b90f:1">`b"still allows embedded                                             'single'                                             quotes"`</span><span data-offset-key="c5ca37a5d2df4f689039baf078e2b90f:2">.</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2aa72b4b209741469481291ba8fcd296"><span data-offset-key="2aa72b4b209741469481291ba8fcd296:0">Triple quoted: </span><span data-offset-key="2aa72b4b209741469481291ba8fcd296:1">`b'''3 single                                             quotes'''`</span><span data-offset-key="2aa72b4b209741469481291ba8fcd296:2">, </span><span data-offset-key="2aa72b4b209741469481291ba8fcd296:3">`b"""3 double                                             quotes"""`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="59825d965c4c482dbdcaf743c9a555db"><span data-offset-key="59825d965c4c482dbdcaf743c9a555db:0">Only ASCII characters are permitted in bytes literals (regardless of the declared source code encoding). Any binary values over 127 must be entered into bytes literals using the appropriate escape sequence.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="dad5f78ce00248b9b53421497af71cc5"><span data-offset-key="dad5f78ce00248b9b53421497af71cc5:0">As with string literals, bytes literals may also use a </span><span data-offset-key="dad5f78ce00248b9b53421497af71cc5:1">`r`</span><span data-offset-key="dad5f78ce00248b9b53421497af71cc5:2"> prefix to disable processing of escape sequences. See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/lexical_analysis.html#strings" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="203c444fbc554042b5e3bc21f274dabe"><span data-offset-key="203c444fbc554042b5e3bc21f274dabe:0">String and Bytes literals</span></span></a><span data-key="cc71982e25994cc98bafc70c282e688f"><span data-offset-key="cc71982e25994cc98bafc70c282e688f:0"> for more about the various forms of bytes literal, including supported escape sequences.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1863e0268f994730b2e1d1e9eace0f17"><span data-offset-key="1863e0268f994730b2e1d1e9eace0f17:0">While bytes literals and representations are based on ASCII text, bytes objects actually behave like immutable sequences of integers, with each value in the sequence restricted such that </span><span data-offset-key="1863e0268f994730b2e1d1e9eace0f17:1">`0 <= x < 256`</span><span data-offset-key="1863e0268f994730b2e1d1e9eace0f17:2"> (attempts to violate this restriction will trigger </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#ValueError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d09ccb1ee8124f4e86b959d9994c62ef"><span data-offset-key="d09ccb1ee8124f4e86b959d9994c62ef:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">ValueError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="1e17f1fa7cd6431f915479c0c223aa81"><span data-offset-key="1e17f1fa7cd6431f915479c0c223aa81:0">). This is done deliberately to emphasise that while many binary formats include ASCII based elements and can be usefully manipulated with some text-oriented algorithms, this is not generally the case for arbitrary binary data (blindly applying text processing algorithms to binary data formats that are not ASCII compatible will usually lead to data corruption).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="693280a3b450493c8c352b17d7160014"><span data-offset-key="693280a3b450493c8c352b17d7160014:0">In addition to the literal forms, bytes objects can be created in a number of other ways:</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8d48c457dcd94cb5b0552f29e9575d26"><span data-offset-key="8d48c457dcd94cb5b0552f29e9575d26:0">A zero-filled bytes object of a specified length: </span><span data-offset-key="8d48c457dcd94cb5b0552f29e9575d26:1">`bytes(10)`</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="64a0238e8ec849f5898b8784c5b5b3a9"><span data-offset-key="64a0238e8ec849f5898b8784c5b5b3a9:0">From an iterable of integers: </span><span data-offset-key="64a0238e8ec849f5898b8784c5b5b3a9:1">`bytes(range(20))`</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7e1830752f38461288a21b565180a4f7"><span data-offset-key="7e1830752f38461288a21b565180a4f7:0">Copying existing binary data via the buffer protocol: </span><span data-offset-key="7e1830752f38461288a21b565180a4f7:1">`bytes(obj)`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f3abd501e88f4195a7109c48223d6c96"><span data-offset-key="f3abd501e88f4195a7109c48223d6c96:0">Also see the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#func-bytes" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0a2b8d52520542adbce9e1b0e3315369"><span data-offset-key="0a2b8d52520542adbce9e1b0e3315369:0">bytes</span></span></a><span data-key="541adc6cf6bb4bb788d7bb19e26b1a4f"><span data-offset-key="541adc6cf6bb4bb788d7bb19e26b1a4f:0"> built-in.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7b5028143121428bb70e0ea3619d7978"><span data-offset-key="7b5028143121428bb70e0ea3619d7978:0">Since 2 hexadecimal digits correspond precisely to a single byte, hexadecimal numbers are a commonly used format for describing binary data. Accordingly, the bytes type has an additional class method to read data in that format:</span><span data-offset-key="7b5028143121428bb70e0ea3619d7978:1">*classmethod* </span><span data-offset-key="7b5028143121428bb70e0ea3619d7978:2">`fromhex`</span><span data-offset-key="7b5028143121428bb70e0ea3619d7978:3">(</span><span data-offset-key="7b5028143121428bb70e0ea3619d7978:4">*string*</span><span data-offset-key="7b5028143121428bb70e0ea3619d7978:5">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d10aff9a911c4a668d62c9486b2faaec"><span data-offset-key="d10aff9a911c4a668d62c9486b2faaec:0">This </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="32045f7833d841e3af0922444090a824"><span data-offset-key="32045f7833d841e3af0922444090a824:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytes</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a634c16cea624dff84da97c83bead9f8"><span data-offset-key="a634c16cea624dff84da97c83bead9f8:0"> class method returns a bytes object, decoding the given string object. The string must contain two hexadecimal digits per byte, with ASCII whitespace being ignored.&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> bytes.fromhex('2Ef0 F1f2  ')b'.\xf0\xf1\xf2'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="193ed4962258483ebfdbd41fedf06a4c"><span data-offset-key="193ed4962258483ebfdbd41fedf06a4c:0">Changed in version 3.7: </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes.fromhex" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="17f1b36ef1074865abe1f1cb9c8d6153"><span data-offset-key="17f1b36ef1074865abe1f1cb9c8d6153:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytes.fromhex()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="8c9e8c02c4fb46789accc50f16f6ab6f"><span data-offset-key="8c9e8c02c4fb46789accc50f16f6ab6f:0"> now skips all ASCII whitespace in the string, not just spaces.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="66adeea81b5847ad82e0c53722458823"><span data-offset-key="66adeea81b5847ad82e0c53722458823:0">A reverse conversion function exists to transform a bytes object into its hexadecimal representation.</span><span data-offset-key="66adeea81b5847ad82e0c53722458823:1">`hex`</span><span data-offset-key="66adeea81b5847ad82e0c53722458823:2">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="66adeea81b5847ad82e0c53722458823:3">*sep*</span><span data-offset-key="66adeea81b5847ad82e0c53722458823:4">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="66adeea81b5847ad82e0c53722458823:5">*bytes\_per\_sep*</span><span data-offset-key="66adeea81b5847ad82e0c53722458823:6">\]\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c6500d90d9ce468aa45061393bd37fb8"><span data-offset-key="c6500d90d9ce468aa45061393bd37fb8:0">Return a string object containing two hexadecimal digits for each byte in the instance.&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> b'\xf0\xf1\xf2'.hex()'f0f1f2'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="dc40be35dabb482686ce246a74f33984"><span data-offset-key="dc40be35dabb482686ce246a74f33984:0">If you want to make the hex string easier to read, you can specify a single character separator </span><span data-offset-key="dc40be35dabb482686ce246a74f33984:1">*sep*</span><span data-offset-key="dc40be35dabb482686ce246a74f33984:2"> parameter to include in the output. By default between each byte. A second optional </span><span data-offset-key="dc40be35dabb482686ce246a74f33984:3">*bytes\_per\_sep*</span><span data-offset-key="dc40be35dabb482686ce246a74f33984:4"> parameter controls the spacing. Positive values calculate the separator position from the right, negative values from the left.&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> value = b'\xf0\xf1\xf2'>>> value.hex('-')'f0-f1-f2'>>> value.hex('_', 2)'f0_f1f2'>>> b'UUDDLRLRAB'.hex(' ', -4)'55554444 4c524c52 4142'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5f529ba7df2c4327922ab8cfe4d45ccb"><span data-offset-key="5f529ba7df2c4327922ab8cfe4d45ccb:0">New in version 3.5.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d72df6fd03f44893a81bc2d04351d794"><span data-offset-key="d72df6fd03f44893a81bc2d04351d794:0">Changed in version 3.8: </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes.hex" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1d47fe2eec6349898cfbac7038951a3c"><span data-offset-key="1d47fe2eec6349898cfbac7038951a3c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytes.hex()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ab80afb23dcb4461aff1024a938bfb52"><span data-offset-key="ab80afb23dcb4461aff1024a938bfb52:0"> now supports optional </span><span data-offset-key="ab80afb23dcb4461aff1024a938bfb52:1">*sep*</span><span data-offset-key="ab80afb23dcb4461aff1024a938bfb52:2"> and </span><span data-offset-key="ab80afb23dcb4461aff1024a938bfb52:3">*bytes\_per\_sep*</span><span data-offset-key="ab80afb23dcb4461aff1024a938bfb52:4"> parameters to insert separators between bytes in the hex output.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="13eff45f8d934e398af0f5e8d37ae548"><span data-offset-key="13eff45f8d934e398af0f5e8d37ae548:0">Since bytes objects are sequences of integers (akin to a tuple), for a bytes object </span><span data-offset-key="13eff45f8d934e398af0f5e8d37ae548:1">*b*</span><span data-offset-key="13eff45f8d934e398af0f5e8d37ae548:2">, </span><span data-offset-key="13eff45f8d934e398af0f5e8d37ae548:3">`b[0]`</span><span data-offset-key="13eff45f8d934e398af0f5e8d37ae548:4"> will be an integer, while </span><span data-offset-key="13eff45f8d934e398af0f5e8d37ae548:5">`b[0:1]`</span><span data-offset-key="13eff45f8d934e398af0f5e8d37ae548:6"> will be a bytes object of length 1. (This contrasts with text strings, where both indexing and slicing will produce a string of length 1)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8044258ddf064640a35dca76299ef559"><span data-offset-key="8044258ddf064640a35dca76299ef559:0">The representation of bytes objects uses the literal format (</span><span data-offset-key="8044258ddf064640a35dca76299ef559:1">`b'...'`</span><span data-offset-key="8044258ddf064640a35dca76299ef559:2">) since it is often more useful than e.g. </span><span data-offset-key="8044258ddf064640a35dca76299ef559:3">`bytes([46, 46, 46])`</span><span data-offset-key="8044258ddf064640a35dca76299ef559:4">. You can always convert a bytes object into a list of integers using </span><span data-offset-key="8044258ddf064640a35dca76299ef559:5">`list(b)`</span><span data-offset-key="8044258ddf064640a35dca76299ef559:6">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2b894fca53b04d638687fffe504786e3"><span data-offset-key="2b894fca53b04d638687fffe504786e3:0">Note </span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d9e2907167934a10ae40133970d11da1"><span data-offset-key="d9e2907167934a10ae40133970d11da1:0">For Python 2.x users: In the Python 2.x series, a variety of implicit conversions between 8-bit strings (the closest thing 2.x offers to a built-in binary data type) and Unicode strings were permitted. This was a backwards compatibility workaround to account for the fact that Python originally only supported 8-bit text, and Unicode text was a later addition. In Python 3.x, those implicit conversions are gone - conversions between 8-bit binary data and Unicode text must be explicit, and bytes and string objects will always compare unequal.</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="03fa33ffe36047e38bd80a5e8ed57a0a"><span data-offset-key="03fa33ffe36047e38bd80a5e8ed57a0a:0">Bytearray Objects</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fd008ce146554414a978ceb6b80b7c9c"><span data-offset-key="fd008ce146554414a978ceb6b80b7c9c:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytearray" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bf5aec33dab94e90b39b7d0c6146499e"><span data-offset-key="bf5aec33dab94e90b39b7d0c6146499e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytearray</code></span></span></a><span data-key="24d42d1f92c449c59fbc92c1b87c6e0b"><span data-offset-key="24d42d1f92c449c59fbc92c1b87c6e0b:0"> objects are a mutable counterpart to </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2e2da3c9c82845c099009d08293ae858"><span data-offset-key="2e2da3c9c82845c099009d08293ae858:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytes</code></span></span></a><span data-key="618bd7a6e89541729504db173e0419f9"><span data-offset-key="618bd7a6e89541729504db173e0419f9:0"> objects.</span><span data-offset-key="618bd7a6e89541729504db173e0419f9:1">*class* </span><span data-offset-key="618bd7a6e89541729504db173e0419f9:2">`bytearray`</span><span data-offset-key="618bd7a6e89541729504db173e0419f9:3">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="618bd7a6e89541729504db173e0419f9:4">*source*</span><span data-offset-key="618bd7a6e89541729504db173e0419f9:5">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="618bd7a6e89541729504db173e0419f9:6">*encoding*</span><span data-offset-key="618bd7a6e89541729504db173e0419f9:7">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="618bd7a6e89541729504db173e0419f9:8">*errors*</span><span data-offset-key="618bd7a6e89541729504db173e0419f9:9">\]\]\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d5731f84a16c459ca7fdbf88bbe27bf3"><span data-offset-key="d5731f84a16c459ca7fdbf88bbe27bf3:0">There is no dedicated literal syntax for bytearray objects, instead they are always created by calling the constructor:</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4eeadd124bc743dfa858832e95276132"><span data-offset-key="4eeadd124bc743dfa858832e95276132:0">Creating an empty instance: </span><span data-offset-key="4eeadd124bc743dfa858832e95276132:1">`bytearray()`</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0409e9bf8a3948bfaede2e244e162d66"><span data-offset-key="0409e9bf8a3948bfaede2e244e162d66:0">Creating a zero-filled instance with a given length: </span><span data-offset-key="0409e9bf8a3948bfaede2e244e162d66:1">`bytearray(10)`</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4e87a3dda6d942a7b6bb5c2ca41bba0a"><span data-offset-key="4e87a3dda6d942a7b6bb5c2ca41bba0a:0">From an iterable of integers: </span><span data-offset-key="4e87a3dda6d942a7b6bb5c2ca41bba0a:1">`bytearray(range(20))`</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="11480f06b89f48cca59a1cf47e98345a"><span data-offset-key="11480f06b89f48cca59a1cf47e98345a:0">Copying existing binary data via the buffer protocol: </span><span data-offset-key="11480f06b89f48cca59a1cf47e98345a:1">`bytearray(b'Hi!')`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4950301539974d438ff598929395441b"><span data-offset-key="4950301539974d438ff598929395441b:0">As bytearray objects are mutable, they support the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#typesseq-mutable" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4f628af76a1046d79dbf8e29d6473aea"><span data-offset-key="4f628af76a1046d79dbf8e29d6473aea:0">mutable</span></span></a><span data-key="b3b5b6f3180e47279ef758c2ddb0f09a"><span data-offset-key="b3b5b6f3180e47279ef758c2ddb0f09a:0"> sequence operations in addition to the common bytes and bytearray operations described in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes-methods" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="763859f1134f4835b4f9bd803d992783"><span data-offset-key="763859f1134f4835b4f9bd803d992783:0">Bytes and Bytearray Operations</span></span></a><span data-key="25027d2b3b034536aeff31728307435c"><span data-offset-key="25027d2b3b034536aeff31728307435c:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="84101cbbcf8e41eaa1b4bd3cc8638dc2"><span data-offset-key="84101cbbcf8e41eaa1b4bd3cc8638dc2:0">Also see the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#func-bytearray" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="54585f8218374414acb1b027fea95968"><span data-offset-key="54585f8218374414acb1b027fea95968:0">bytearray</span></span></a><span data-key="1b15f5f3e56d46d09606496b588fa1e2"><span data-offset-key="1b15f5f3e56d46d09606496b588fa1e2:0"> built-in.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5cc110f1e92742c38417c20823beca06"><span data-offset-key="5cc110f1e92742c38417c20823beca06:0">Since 2 hexadecimal digits correspond precisely to a single byte, hexadecimal numbers are a commonly used format for describing binary data. Accordingly, the bytearray type has an additional class method to read data in that format:</span><span data-offset-key="5cc110f1e92742c38417c20823beca06:1">*classmethod* </span><span data-offset-key="5cc110f1e92742c38417c20823beca06:2">`fromhex`</span><span data-offset-key="5cc110f1e92742c38417c20823beca06:3">(</span><span data-offset-key="5cc110f1e92742c38417c20823beca06:4">*string*</span><span data-offset-key="5cc110f1e92742c38417c20823beca06:5">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="45a0ad82b5364e6eb000f7a388159c1e"><span data-offset-key="45a0ad82b5364e6eb000f7a388159c1e:0">This </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytearray" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b8f49fb9256b40d79bfab5f1701b325c"><span data-offset-key="b8f49fb9256b40d79bfab5f1701b325c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytearray</code></span></span></a><span data-key="2b47ef9ade894c049df3612a91d56df9"><span data-offset-key="2b47ef9ade894c049df3612a91d56df9:0"> class method returns bytearray object, decoding the given string object. The string must contain two hexadecimal digits per byte, with ASCII whitespace being ignored.&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> bytearray.fromhex('2Ef0 F1f2  ')bytearray(b'.\xf0\xf1\xf2')

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ed364f2fc10648a4b9d4bc3402d6626a"><span data-offset-key="ed364f2fc10648a4b9d4bc3402d6626a:0">Changed in version 3.7: </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytearray.fromhex" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7c75eab7906c4417af7338ba0bc5db57"><span data-offset-key="7c75eab7906c4417af7338ba0bc5db57:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytearray.fromhex()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="bfa8b8fca4534a28b2d499cbf2af5ace"><span data-offset-key="bfa8b8fca4534a28b2d499cbf2af5ace:0"> now skips all ASCII whitespace in the string, not just spaces.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b9e89c8ff7b042e2833fd489fff77a58"><span data-offset-key="b9e89c8ff7b042e2833fd489fff77a58:0">A reverse conversion function exists to transform a bytearray object into its hexadecimal representation.</span><span data-offset-key="b9e89c8ff7b042e2833fd489fff77a58:1">`hex`</span><span data-offset-key="b9e89c8ff7b042e2833fd489fff77a58:2">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="b9e89c8ff7b042e2833fd489fff77a58:3">*sep*</span><span data-offset-key="b9e89c8ff7b042e2833fd489fff77a58:4">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="b9e89c8ff7b042e2833fd489fff77a58:5">*bytes\_per\_sep*</span><span data-offset-key="b9e89c8ff7b042e2833fd489fff77a58:6">\]\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="726cfec45f8a4252b32a376c905bfda9"><span data-offset-key="726cfec45f8a4252b32a376c905bfda9:0">Return a string object containing two hexadecimal digits for each byte in the instance.&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> bytearray(b'\xf0\xf1\xf2').hex()'f0f1f2'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2630fc6f4c2c411e954d462155652578"><span data-offset-key="2630fc6f4c2c411e954d462155652578:0">New in version 3.5.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5c5e6398ced3489d968b3f99611a5790"><span data-offset-key="5c5e6398ced3489d968b3f99611a5790:0">Changed in version 3.8: Similar to </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes.hex" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="497eaaebfcf34b3a9cd1875f1cae32fc"><span data-offset-key="497eaaebfcf34b3a9cd1875f1cae32fc:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytes.hex()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="c75bd131ff5946f2847f763825c651e3"><span data-offset-key="c75bd131ff5946f2847f763825c651e3:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytearray.hex" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="cd50a6cea64c4a4caff24128a84fab89"><span data-offset-key="cd50a6cea64c4a4caff24128a84fab89:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytearray.hex()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="5ea4c2f11d9c4d55baf9cf26d9dc2ad1"><span data-offset-key="5ea4c2f11d9c4d55baf9cf26d9dc2ad1:0"> now supports optional </span><span data-offset-key="5ea4c2f11d9c4d55baf9cf26d9dc2ad1:1">*sep*</span><span data-offset-key="5ea4c2f11d9c4d55baf9cf26d9dc2ad1:2"> and </span><span data-offset-key="5ea4c2f11d9c4d55baf9cf26d9dc2ad1:3">*bytes\_per\_sep*</span><span data-offset-key="5ea4c2f11d9c4d55baf9cf26d9dc2ad1:4"> parameters to insert separators between bytes in the hex output.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="519cf9b10b5b4665b9d2d92505127a37"><span data-offset-key="519cf9b10b5b4665b9d2d92505127a37:0">Since bytearray objects are sequences of integers (akin to a list), for a bytearray object </span><span data-offset-key="519cf9b10b5b4665b9d2d92505127a37:1">*b*</span><span data-offset-key="519cf9b10b5b4665b9d2d92505127a37:2">, </span><span data-offset-key="519cf9b10b5b4665b9d2d92505127a37:3">`b[0]`</span><span data-offset-key="519cf9b10b5b4665b9d2d92505127a37:4"> will be an integer, while </span><span data-offset-key="519cf9b10b5b4665b9d2d92505127a37:5">`b[0:1]`</span><span data-offset-key="519cf9b10b5b4665b9d2d92505127a37:6"> will be a bytearray object of length 1. (This contrasts with text strings, where both indexing and slicing will produce a string of length 1)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="11ce5b55e3e74effb0f297c50cc8ad06"><span data-offset-key="11ce5b55e3e74effb0f297c50cc8ad06:0">The representation of bytearray objects uses the bytes literal format (</span><span data-offset-key="11ce5b55e3e74effb0f297c50cc8ad06:1">`bytearray(b'...')`</span><span data-offset-key="11ce5b55e3e74effb0f297c50cc8ad06:2">) since it is often more useful than e.g. </span><span data-offset-key="11ce5b55e3e74effb0f297c50cc8ad06:3">`bytearray([46, 46, 46])`</span><span data-offset-key="11ce5b55e3e74effb0f297c50cc8ad06:4">. You can always convert a bytearray object into a list of integers using </span><span data-offset-key="11ce5b55e3e74effb0f297c50cc8ad06:5">`list(b)`</span><span data-offset-key="11ce5b55e3e74effb0f297c50cc8ad06:6">.</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0cbe19d86c1c48988b172c9fc025f973"><span data-offset-key="0cbe19d86c1c48988b172c9fc025f973:0">Bytes and Bytearray Operations</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="eac159d7e06f4f7d9897742b7d53bc4a"><span data-offset-key="eac159d7e06f4f7d9897742b7d53bc4a:0">Both bytes and bytearray objects support the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#typesseq-common" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e70bc9aa87d245f58835d33df72b7236"><span data-offset-key="e70bc9aa87d245f58835d33df72b7236:0">common</span></span></a><span data-key="07aceb182ea24d9cb69d7c65cc823d31"><span data-offset-key="07aceb182ea24d9cb69d7c65cc823d31:0"> sequence operations. They interoperate not just with operands of the same type, but with any </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-bytes-like-object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c40e825e33b145eca20a7aea0cc43673"><span data-offset-key="c40e825e33b145eca20a7aea0cc43673:0">bytes-like object</span></span></a><span data-key="50ff7b58adde4685a1bcef1808451f29"><span data-offset-key="50ff7b58adde4685a1bcef1808451f29:0">. Due to this flexibility, they can be freely mixed in operations without causing errors. However, the return type of the result may depend on the order of operands.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="76782c60bc584e4194177364af85229a"><span data-offset-key="76782c60bc584e4194177364af85229a:0">Note </span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fa0999947b83410cabc01d50943554ec"><span data-offset-key="fa0999947b83410cabc01d50943554ec:0">The methods on bytes and bytearray objects don’t accept strings as their arguments, just as the methods on strings don’t accept bytes as their arguments. For example, you have to write:</span></span></span>

    a = "abc"b = a.replace("a", "f")

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="144bbd52710745bf8a80afb08a0f8acd"><span data-offset-key="144bbd52710745bf8a80afb08a0f8acd:0">and:</span></span></span>

    a = b"abc"b = a.replace(b"a", b"f")

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b123e96efa3444f18564d99ec3fc1062"><span data-offset-key="b123e96efa3444f18564d99ec3fc1062:0">Some bytes and bytearray operations assume the use of ASCII compatible binary formats, and hence should be avoided when working with arbitrary binary data. These restrictions are covered below.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="066d40058fd944c881fcfedc5f730b30"><span data-offset-key="066d40058fd944c881fcfedc5f730b30:0">Note </span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d8844ddd9f424fa5bb73883f74cf2689"><span data-offset-key="d8844ddd9f424fa5bb73883f74cf2689:0">Using these ASCII based operations to manipulate binary data that is not stored in an ASCII based format may lead to data corruption.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="47d3a6d76be446cfb731d925b8a343cf"><span data-offset-key="47d3a6d76be446cfb731d925b8a343cf:0">The following methods on bytes and bytearray objects can be used with arbitrary binary data.</span><span data-offset-key="47d3a6d76be446cfb731d925b8a343cf:1">`bytes.count`</span><span data-offset-key="47d3a6d76be446cfb731d925b8a343cf:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="47d3a6d76be446cfb731d925b8a343cf:3">*sub*</span><span data-offset-key="47d3a6d76be446cfb731d925b8a343cf:4">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="47d3a6d76be446cfb731d925b8a343cf:5">*start*</span><span data-offset-key="47d3a6d76be446cfb731d925b8a343cf:6">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="47d3a6d76be446cfb731d925b8a343cf:7">*end*</span><span data-offset-key="47d3a6d76be446cfb731d925b8a343cf:8">\]\])</span><span data-offset-key="47d3a6d76be446cfb731d925b8a343cf:9">`bytearray.count`</span><span data-offset-key="47d3a6d76be446cfb731d925b8a343cf:10">(</span><span data-offset-key="47d3a6d76be446cfb731d925b8a343cf:11">*sub*</span><span data-offset-key="47d3a6d76be446cfb731d925b8a343cf:12">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="47d3a6d76be446cfb731d925b8a343cf:13">*start*</span><span data-offset-key="47d3a6d76be446cfb731d925b8a343cf:14">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="47d3a6d76be446cfb731d925b8a343cf:15">*end*</span><span data-offset-key="47d3a6d76be446cfb731d925b8a343cf:16">\]\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="bde7e62887ba4ca5a625faab9c2506ad"><span data-offset-key="bde7e62887ba4ca5a625faab9c2506ad:0">Return the number of non-overlapping occurrences of subsequence </span><span data-offset-key="bde7e62887ba4ca5a625faab9c2506ad:1">*sub*</span><span data-offset-key="bde7e62887ba4ca5a625faab9c2506ad:2"> in the range \[</span><span data-offset-key="bde7e62887ba4ca5a625faab9c2506ad:3">*start*</span><span data-offset-key="bde7e62887ba4ca5a625faab9c2506ad:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="bde7e62887ba4ca5a625faab9c2506ad:5">*end*</span><span data-offset-key="bde7e62887ba4ca5a625faab9c2506ad:6">\]. Optional arguments </span><span data-offset-key="bde7e62887ba4ca5a625faab9c2506ad:7">*start*</span><span data-offset-key="bde7e62887ba4ca5a625faab9c2506ad:8"> and </span><span data-offset-key="bde7e62887ba4ca5a625faab9c2506ad:9">*end*</span><span data-offset-key="bde7e62887ba4ca5a625faab9c2506ad:10"> are interpreted as in slice notation.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ec9eb2a1e75d44ce9f965296bb503495"><span data-offset-key="ec9eb2a1e75d44ce9f965296bb503495:0">The subsequence to search for may be any </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-bytes-like-object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9b9ca48c56cf49d380f317cd2124c88c"><span data-offset-key="9b9ca48c56cf49d380f317cd2124c88c:0">bytes-like object</span></span></a><span data-key="dc260d9c959d426280f582e2e168d0e0"><span data-offset-key="dc260d9c959d426280f582e2e168d0e0:0"> or an integer in the range 0 to 255.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1644e40d3ef54492aed5799cb3e36e8f"><span data-offset-key="1644e40d3ef54492aed5799cb3e36e8f:0">Changed in version 3.3: Also accept an integer in the range 0 to 255 as the subsequence.</span><span data-offset-key="1644e40d3ef54492aed5799cb3e36e8f:1">`bytes.removeprefix`</span><span data-offset-key="1644e40d3ef54492aed5799cb3e36e8f:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="1644e40d3ef54492aed5799cb3e36e8f:3">*prefix*</span><span data-offset-key="1644e40d3ef54492aed5799cb3e36e8f:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="1644e40d3ef54492aed5799cb3e36e8f:5">*/*</span><span data-offset-key="1644e40d3ef54492aed5799cb3e36e8f:6">)</span><span data-offset-key="1644e40d3ef54492aed5799cb3e36e8f:7">`bytearray.removeprefix`</span><span data-offset-key="1644e40d3ef54492aed5799cb3e36e8f:8">(</span><span data-offset-key="1644e40d3ef54492aed5799cb3e36e8f:9">*prefix*</span><span data-offset-key="1644e40d3ef54492aed5799cb3e36e8f:10">, </span><span data-offset-key="1644e40d3ef54492aed5799cb3e36e8f:11">*/*</span><span data-offset-key="1644e40d3ef54492aed5799cb3e36e8f:12">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="cd246830a8054381bf9ee91e71ad4db3"><span data-offset-key="cd246830a8054381bf9ee91e71ad4db3:0">If the binary data starts with the </span><span data-offset-key="cd246830a8054381bf9ee91e71ad4db3:1">*prefix*</span><span data-offset-key="cd246830a8054381bf9ee91e71ad4db3:2"> string, return </span><span data-offset-key="cd246830a8054381bf9ee91e71ad4db3:3">`bytes[len(prefix):]`</span><span data-offset-key="cd246830a8054381bf9ee91e71ad4db3:4">. Otherwise, return a copy of the original binary data:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> b'TestHook'.removeprefix(b'Test')b'Hook'>>> b'BaseTestCase'.removeprefix(b'Test')b'BaseTestCase'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="883e9bf4869e49e69a3e1b0c88b56528"><span data-offset-key="883e9bf4869e49e69a3e1b0c88b56528:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="883e9bf4869e49e69a3e1b0c88b56528:1">*prefix*</span><span data-offset-key="883e9bf4869e49e69a3e1b0c88b56528:2"> may be any </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-bytes-like-object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d4c3c55802ed49fc977dce8d3cf93858"><span data-offset-key="d4c3c55802ed49fc977dce8d3cf93858:0">bytes-like object</span></span></a><span data-key="1216dc938c194255b118e40605aa4fbc"><span data-offset-key="1216dc938c194255b118e40605aa4fbc:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9ab57dcba485474ebd88b52e3ad1e70a"><span data-offset-key="9ab57dcba485474ebd88b52e3ad1e70a:0">Note </span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="bb497e40dfba47faa3d57fb1ee0b7aca"><span data-offset-key="bb497e40dfba47faa3d57fb1ee0b7aca:0">The bytearray version of this method does </span><span data-offset-key="bb497e40dfba47faa3d57fb1ee0b7aca:1">*not*</span><span data-offset-key="bb497e40dfba47faa3d57fb1ee0b7aca:2"> operate in place - it always produces a new object, even if no changes were made.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="eff3e5eb78f7419d869cbbf3eec2afa3"><span data-offset-key="eff3e5eb78f7419d869cbbf3eec2afa3:0">New in version 3.9.</span><span data-offset-key="eff3e5eb78f7419d869cbbf3eec2afa3:1">`bytes.removesuffix`</span><span data-offset-key="eff3e5eb78f7419d869cbbf3eec2afa3:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="eff3e5eb78f7419d869cbbf3eec2afa3:3">*suffix*</span><span data-offset-key="eff3e5eb78f7419d869cbbf3eec2afa3:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="eff3e5eb78f7419d869cbbf3eec2afa3:5">*/*</span><span data-offset-key="eff3e5eb78f7419d869cbbf3eec2afa3:6">)</span><span data-offset-key="eff3e5eb78f7419d869cbbf3eec2afa3:7">`bytearray.removesuffix`</span><span data-offset-key="eff3e5eb78f7419d869cbbf3eec2afa3:8">(</span><span data-offset-key="eff3e5eb78f7419d869cbbf3eec2afa3:9">*suffix*</span><span data-offset-key="eff3e5eb78f7419d869cbbf3eec2afa3:10">, </span><span data-offset-key="eff3e5eb78f7419d869cbbf3eec2afa3:11">*/*</span><span data-offset-key="eff3e5eb78f7419d869cbbf3eec2afa3:12">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="42ebafb8519e49949aafce690a231b5a"><span data-offset-key="42ebafb8519e49949aafce690a231b5a:0">If the binary data ends with the </span><span data-offset-key="42ebafb8519e49949aafce690a231b5a:1">*suffix*</span><span data-offset-key="42ebafb8519e49949aafce690a231b5a:2"> string and that </span><span data-offset-key="42ebafb8519e49949aafce690a231b5a:3">*suffix*</span><span data-offset-key="42ebafb8519e49949aafce690a231b5a:4"> is not empty, return </span><span data-offset-key="42ebafb8519e49949aafce690a231b5a:5">`bytes[:-len(suffix)]`</span><span data-offset-key="42ebafb8519e49949aafce690a231b5a:6">. Otherwise, return a copy of the original binary data:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> b'MiscTests'.removesuffix(b'Tests')b'Misc'>>> b'TmpDirMixin'.removesuffix(b'Tests')b'TmpDirMixin'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d2df54ba78ac43c9951c31f88601e446"><span data-offset-key="d2df54ba78ac43c9951c31f88601e446:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="d2df54ba78ac43c9951c31f88601e446:1">*suffix*</span><span data-offset-key="d2df54ba78ac43c9951c31f88601e446:2"> may be any </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-bytes-like-object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ba05cf78edf14fa1aaf547a317375e9c"><span data-offset-key="ba05cf78edf14fa1aaf547a317375e9c:0">bytes-like object</span></span></a><span data-key="a6e7e4e33c62498aa1c0b247502217c5"><span data-offset-key="a6e7e4e33c62498aa1c0b247502217c5:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a95a70f4d890417a94c72e017bee77a5"><span data-offset-key="a95a70f4d890417a94c72e017bee77a5:0">Note </span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3a7391039ca44662a014e5c253564e4e"><span data-offset-key="3a7391039ca44662a014e5c253564e4e:0">The bytearray version of this method does </span><span data-offset-key="3a7391039ca44662a014e5c253564e4e:1">*not*</span><span data-offset-key="3a7391039ca44662a014e5c253564e4e:2"> operate in place - it always produces a new object, even if no changes were made.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8980904683a24e90bd49f33427f43386"><span data-offset-key="8980904683a24e90bd49f33427f43386:0">New in version 3.9.</span><span data-offset-key="8980904683a24e90bd49f33427f43386:1">`bytes.decode`</span><span data-offset-key="8980904683a24e90bd49f33427f43386:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="8980904683a24e90bd49f33427f43386:3">*encoding="utf-8"*</span><span data-offset-key="8980904683a24e90bd49f33427f43386:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="8980904683a24e90bd49f33427f43386:5">*errors="strict"*</span><span data-offset-key="8980904683a24e90bd49f33427f43386:6">)</span><span data-offset-key="8980904683a24e90bd49f33427f43386:7">`bytearray.decode`</span><span data-offset-key="8980904683a24e90bd49f33427f43386:8">(</span><span data-offset-key="8980904683a24e90bd49f33427f43386:9">*encoding="utf-8"*</span><span data-offset-key="8980904683a24e90bd49f33427f43386:10">, </span><span data-offset-key="8980904683a24e90bd49f33427f43386:11">*errors="strict"*</span><span data-offset-key="8980904683a24e90bd49f33427f43386:12">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c6b19048969c4332a9172bcf0f5b8ac5"><span data-offset-key="c6b19048969c4332a9172bcf0f5b8ac5:0">Return a string decoded from the given bytes. Default encoding is </span><span data-offset-key="c6b19048969c4332a9172bcf0f5b8ac5:1">`'utf-8'`</span><span data-offset-key="c6b19048969c4332a9172bcf0f5b8ac5:2">. </span><span data-offset-key="c6b19048969c4332a9172bcf0f5b8ac5:3">*errors*</span><span data-offset-key="c6b19048969c4332a9172bcf0f5b8ac5:4"> may be given to set a different error handling scheme. The default for </span><span data-offset-key="c6b19048969c4332a9172bcf0f5b8ac5:5">*errors*</span><span data-offset-key="c6b19048969c4332a9172bcf0f5b8ac5:6"> is </span><span data-offset-key="c6b19048969c4332a9172bcf0f5b8ac5:7">`'strict'`</span><span data-offset-key="c6b19048969c4332a9172bcf0f5b8ac5:8">, meaning that encoding errors raise a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#UnicodeError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="83702a96aae84b89b06bc69e3f9d027f"><span data-offset-key="83702a96aae84b89b06bc69e3f9d027f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">UnicodeError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ccb3a9fe96c74541b693b673da7fd277"><span data-offset-key="ccb3a9fe96c74541b693b673da7fd277:0">. Other possible values are </span><span data-offset-key="ccb3a9fe96c74541b693b673da7fd277:1">`'ignore'`</span><span data-offset-key="ccb3a9fe96c74541b693b673da7fd277:2">, </span><span data-offset-key="ccb3a9fe96c74541b693b673da7fd277:3">`'replace'`</span><span data-offset-key="ccb3a9fe96c74541b693b673da7fd277:4"> and any other name registered via </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/codecs.html#codecs.register_error" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ecdd9a4ea06e4632b4c0d0ebd525245c"><span data-offset-key="ecdd9a4ea06e4632b4c0d0ebd525245c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">codecs.register_error()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="1c0f3d6e15634a0ea8dc4bcec2ea5088"><span data-offset-key="1c0f3d6e15634a0ea8dc4bcec2ea5088:0">, see section </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/codecs.html#error-handlers" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d80f4371f58747aa861c63c8b06f6942"><span data-offset-key="d80f4371f58747aa861c63c8b06f6942:0">Error Handlers</span></span></a><span data-key="e3c7b221c92e4058a3c2d67f9a9896c7"><span data-offset-key="e3c7b221c92e4058a3c2d67f9a9896c7:0">. For a list of possible encodings, see section </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/codecs.html#standard-encodings" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="530298b6db6e4f1aac3b0cdf795acb08"><span data-offset-key="530298b6db6e4f1aac3b0cdf795acb08:0">Standard Encodings</span></span></a><span data-key="10c40d0553cc475ca869b6d3f0fa1640"><span data-offset-key="10c40d0553cc475ca869b6d3f0fa1640:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="79a3ea74378043f3a2c7fa6c73c680a6"><span data-offset-key="79a3ea74378043f3a2c7fa6c73c680a6:0">By default, the </span><span data-offset-key="79a3ea74378043f3a2c7fa6c73c680a6:1">*errors*</span><span data-offset-key="79a3ea74378043f3a2c7fa6c73c680a6:2"> argument is not checked for best performances, but only used at the first decoding error. Enable the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/devmode.html#devmode" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f9151f85af0c4af7bca7c994a5b8ce6b"><span data-offset-key="f9151f85af0c4af7bca7c994a5b8ce6b:0">Python Development Mode</span></span></a><span data-key="67aed15ee8284d329faa99e259ce6f25"><span data-offset-key="67aed15ee8284d329faa99e259ce6f25:0">, or use a debug build to check </span><span data-offset-key="67aed15ee8284d329faa99e259ce6f25:1">*errors*</span><span data-offset-key="67aed15ee8284d329faa99e259ce6f25:2">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d3cddb19ef794b53b383f0fab603f413"><span data-offset-key="d3cddb19ef794b53b383f0fab603f413:0">Note </span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7751fcd1f8284eef97e13b97701be576"><span data-offset-key="7751fcd1f8284eef97e13b97701be576:0">Passing the </span><span data-offset-key="7751fcd1f8284eef97e13b97701be576:1">*encoding*</span><span data-offset-key="7751fcd1f8284eef97e13b97701be576:2"> argument to </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="743417f3bf1940f59becd1cd56d7ad6a"><span data-offset-key="743417f3bf1940f59becd1cd56d7ad6a:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str</code></span></span></a><span data-key="9ba506fed3234198bfbc1e1428e481c3"><span data-offset-key="9ba506fed3234198bfbc1e1428e481c3:0"> allows decoding any </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-bytes-like-object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="338b70a9fb4e49d890fd75b8799b1733"><span data-offset-key="338b70a9fb4e49d890fd75b8799b1733:0">bytes-like object</span></span></a><span data-key="de69ad5ed4af446aa9a9ebee517ba1e0"><span data-offset-key="de69ad5ed4af446aa9a9ebee517ba1e0:0"> directly, without needing to make a temporary bytes or bytearray object.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1c75c0cdbc634dcf81705c6641a262b3"><span data-offset-key="1c75c0cdbc634dcf81705c6641a262b3:0">Changed in version 3.1: Added support for keyword arguments.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="469ed50d90b64fdfb9611f697ce2b684"><span data-offset-key="469ed50d90b64fdfb9611f697ce2b684:0">Changed in version 3.9: The </span><span data-offset-key="469ed50d90b64fdfb9611f697ce2b684:1">*errors*</span><span data-offset-key="469ed50d90b64fdfb9611f697ce2b684:2"> is now checked in development mode and in debug mode.</span><span data-offset-key="469ed50d90b64fdfb9611f697ce2b684:3">`bytes.endswith`</span><span data-offset-key="469ed50d90b64fdfb9611f697ce2b684:4">(</span><span data-offset-key="469ed50d90b64fdfb9611f697ce2b684:5">*suffix*</span><span data-offset-key="469ed50d90b64fdfb9611f697ce2b684:6">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="469ed50d90b64fdfb9611f697ce2b684:7">*start*</span><span data-offset-key="469ed50d90b64fdfb9611f697ce2b684:8">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="469ed50d90b64fdfb9611f697ce2b684:9">*end*</span><span data-offset-key="469ed50d90b64fdfb9611f697ce2b684:10">\]\])</span><span data-offset-key="469ed50d90b64fdfb9611f697ce2b684:11">`bytearray.endswith`</span><span data-offset-key="469ed50d90b64fdfb9611f697ce2b684:12">(</span><span data-offset-key="469ed50d90b64fdfb9611f697ce2b684:13">*suffix*</span><span data-offset-key="469ed50d90b64fdfb9611f697ce2b684:14">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="469ed50d90b64fdfb9611f697ce2b684:15">*start*</span><span data-offset-key="469ed50d90b64fdfb9611f697ce2b684:16">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="469ed50d90b64fdfb9611f697ce2b684:17">*end*</span><span data-offset-key="469ed50d90b64fdfb9611f697ce2b684:18">\]\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="43019b9b7c8a44cbb21491db950416f6"><span data-offset-key="43019b9b7c8a44cbb21491db950416f6:0">Return </span><span data-offset-key="43019b9b7c8a44cbb21491db950416f6:1">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="43019b9b7c8a44cbb21491db950416f6:2"> if the binary data ends with the specified </span><span data-offset-key="43019b9b7c8a44cbb21491db950416f6:3">*suffix*</span><span data-offset-key="43019b9b7c8a44cbb21491db950416f6:4">, otherwise return </span><span data-offset-key="43019b9b7c8a44cbb21491db950416f6:5">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="43019b9b7c8a44cbb21491db950416f6:6">. </span><span data-offset-key="43019b9b7c8a44cbb21491db950416f6:7">*suffix*</span><span data-offset-key="43019b9b7c8a44cbb21491db950416f6:8"> can also be a tuple of suffixes to look for. With optional </span><span data-offset-key="43019b9b7c8a44cbb21491db950416f6:9">*start*</span><span data-offset-key="43019b9b7c8a44cbb21491db950416f6:10">, test beginning at that position. With optional </span><span data-offset-key="43019b9b7c8a44cbb21491db950416f6:11">*end*</span><span data-offset-key="43019b9b7c8a44cbb21491db950416f6:12">, stop comparing at that position.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="77d52fd96b344d26aad9f33b6c8a271c"><span data-offset-key="77d52fd96b344d26aad9f33b6c8a271c:0">The suffix(es) to search for may be any </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-bytes-like-object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="52cca141569b4e66909bd36886842864"><span data-offset-key="52cca141569b4e66909bd36886842864:0">bytes-like object</span></span></a><span data-key="4304489fd1c4422890f32d0ad3c7a336"><span data-offset-key="4304489fd1c4422890f32d0ad3c7a336:0">.</span><span data-offset-key="4304489fd1c4422890f32d0ad3c7a336:1">`bytes.find`</span><span data-offset-key="4304489fd1c4422890f32d0ad3c7a336:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="4304489fd1c4422890f32d0ad3c7a336:3">*sub*</span><span data-offset-key="4304489fd1c4422890f32d0ad3c7a336:4">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="4304489fd1c4422890f32d0ad3c7a336:5">*start*</span><span data-offset-key="4304489fd1c4422890f32d0ad3c7a336:6">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="4304489fd1c4422890f32d0ad3c7a336:7">*end*</span><span data-offset-key="4304489fd1c4422890f32d0ad3c7a336:8">\]\])</span><span data-offset-key="4304489fd1c4422890f32d0ad3c7a336:9">`bytearray.find`</span><span data-offset-key="4304489fd1c4422890f32d0ad3c7a336:10">(</span><span data-offset-key="4304489fd1c4422890f32d0ad3c7a336:11">*sub*</span><span data-offset-key="4304489fd1c4422890f32d0ad3c7a336:12">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="4304489fd1c4422890f32d0ad3c7a336:13">*start*</span><span data-offset-key="4304489fd1c4422890f32d0ad3c7a336:14">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="4304489fd1c4422890f32d0ad3c7a336:15">*end*</span><span data-offset-key="4304489fd1c4422890f32d0ad3c7a336:16">\]\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6e4aa4de20bf43e3830f53fe2d897f38"><span data-offset-key="6e4aa4de20bf43e3830f53fe2d897f38:0">Return the lowest index in the data where the subsequence </span><span data-offset-key="6e4aa4de20bf43e3830f53fe2d897f38:1">*sub*</span><span data-offset-key="6e4aa4de20bf43e3830f53fe2d897f38:2"> is found, such that </span><span data-offset-key="6e4aa4de20bf43e3830f53fe2d897f38:3">*sub*</span><span data-offset-key="6e4aa4de20bf43e3830f53fe2d897f38:4"> is contained in the slice </span><span data-offset-key="6e4aa4de20bf43e3830f53fe2d897f38:5">`s[start:end]`</span><span data-offset-key="6e4aa4de20bf43e3830f53fe2d897f38:6">. Optional arguments </span><span data-offset-key="6e4aa4de20bf43e3830f53fe2d897f38:7">*start*</span><span data-offset-key="6e4aa4de20bf43e3830f53fe2d897f38:8"> and </span><span data-offset-key="6e4aa4de20bf43e3830f53fe2d897f38:9">*end*</span><span data-offset-key="6e4aa4de20bf43e3830f53fe2d897f38:10"> are interpreted as in slice notation. Return </span><span data-offset-key="6e4aa4de20bf43e3830f53fe2d897f38:11">`-1`</span><span data-offset-key="6e4aa4de20bf43e3830f53fe2d897f38:12"> if </span><span data-offset-key="6e4aa4de20bf43e3830f53fe2d897f38:13">*sub*</span><span data-offset-key="6e4aa4de20bf43e3830f53fe2d897f38:14"> is not found.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c23903844dfc4bddad6358284e6292b2"><span data-offset-key="c23903844dfc4bddad6358284e6292b2:0">The </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes.find" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="74278e22a26d43969a72089c221cccab"><span data-offset-key="74278e22a26d43969a72089c221cccab:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">find()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="da439844bb134b5e9d4e837dd4955654"><span data-offset-key="da439844bb134b5e9d4e837dd4955654:0"> method should be used only if you need to know the position of </span><span data-offset-key="da439844bb134b5e9d4e837dd4955654:1">*sub*</span><span data-offset-key="da439844bb134b5e9d4e837dd4955654:2">. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="45f65565a8c1454abad87db11db02ce5"><span data-offset-key="45f65565a8c1454abad87db11db02ce5:0">Return a copy of the bytes or bytearray object where all bytes occurring in the optional argument </span><span data-offset-key="45f65565a8c1454abad87db11db02ce5:1">*delete*</span><span data-offset-key="45f65565a8c1454abad87db11db02ce5:2"> are removed, and the remaining bytes have been mapped through the given translation table, which must be a bytes object of length 256.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a8fca7b2d39b43819d3cf4216f37c0de"><span data-offset-key="a8fca7b2d39b43819d3cf4216f37c0de:0">You can use the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes.maketrans" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4c4cd6aa3c6e43ffb06b4e896cbb91bd"><span data-offset-key="4c4cd6aa3c6e43ffb06b4e896cbb91bd:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytes.maketrans()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="011ebe51d2174658b25bc177c3b5b339"><span data-offset-key="011ebe51d2174658b25bc177c3b5b339:0"> method to create a translation table.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6745a1e952444a06beee6ffa1b905c34"><span data-offset-key="6745a1e952444a06beee6ffa1b905c34:0">Set the </span><span data-offset-key="6745a1e952444a06beee6ffa1b905c34:1">*table*</span><span data-offset-key="6745a1e952444a06beee6ffa1b905c34:2"> argument to </span><span data-offset-key="6745a1e952444a06beee6ffa1b905c34:3">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="6745a1e952444a06beee6ffa1b905c34:4"> for translations that only delete characters:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="17e0c3344d01403b9649ed6181a41c74"><span data-offset-key="17e0c3344d01403b9649ed6181a41c74:0">Changed in version 3.6: </span><span data-offset-key="17e0c3344d01403b9649ed6181a41c74:1">*delete*</span><span data-offset-key="17e0c3344d01403b9649ed6181a41c74:2"> is now supported as a keyword argument.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c27cd1f07b1c43c79c3e9bfad4d8ae30"><span data-offset-key="c27cd1f07b1c43c79c3e9bfad4d8ae30:0">The following methods on bytes and bytearray objects have default behaviours that assume the use of ASCII compatible binary formats, but can still be used with arbitrary binary data by passing appropriate arguments. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="96b591a4c7c84547846014ef3e37991b"><span data-offset-key="96b591a4c7c84547846014ef3e37991b:0">Split the binary sequence into subsequences of the same type, using </span><span data-offset-key="96b591a4c7c84547846014ef3e37991b:1">*sep*</span><span data-offset-key="96b591a4c7c84547846014ef3e37991b:2"> as the delimiter string. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2a923b33e6f94398905a59bc50bb72cd"><span data-offset-key="2a923b33e6f94398905a59bc50bb72cd:0">Return a copy of the sequence with specified trailing bytes removed. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c60965ac47c54015a25606e709ebbca2"><span data-offset-key="c60965ac47c54015a25606e709ebbca2:0">The binary sequence of byte values to remove may be any </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-bytes-like-object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ed74f99e72b24a7cbfa45f64236ff77a"><span data-offset-key="ed74f99e72b24a7cbfa45f64236ff77a:0">bytes-like object</span></span></a><span data-key="893e14ac24da4701be2c181e4bd1ef50"><span data-offset-key="893e14ac24da4701be2c181e4bd1ef50:0">.
