    >>> b'Monty Python'.rstrip(b' Python')b'M'>>> b'Monty Python'.removesuffix(b' Python')b'Monty'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c5b5d23c6f074c4da277a4a050726206"><span data-offset-key="c5b5d23c6f074c4da277a4a050726206:0">Note </span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="13f74a02a65746029e2e621f077944f9"><span data-offset-key="13f74a02a65746029e2e621f077944f9:0">The bytearray version of this method does </span><span data-offset-key="13f74a02a65746029e2e621f077944f9:1">*not*</span><span data-offset-key="13f74a02a65746029e2e621f077944f9:2"> operate in place - it always produces a new object, even if no changes were made.</span><span data-offset-key="13f74a02a65746029e2e621f077944f9:3">`bytes.split`</span><span data-offset-key="13f74a02a65746029e2e621f077944f9:4">(</span><span data-offset-key="13f74a02a65746029e2e621f077944f9:5">*sep=None*</span><span data-offset-key="13f74a02a65746029e2e621f077944f9:6">, </span><span data-offset-key="13f74a02a65746029e2e621f077944f9:7">*maxsplit=-1*</span><span data-offset-key="13f74a02a65746029e2e621f077944f9:8">)</span><span data-offset-key="13f74a02a65746029e2e621f077944f9:9">`bytearray.split`</span><span data-offset-key="13f74a02a65746029e2e621f077944f9:10">(</span><span data-offset-key="13f74a02a65746029e2e621f077944f9:11">*sep=None*</span><span data-offset-key="13f74a02a65746029e2e621f077944f9:12">, </span><span data-offset-key="13f74a02a65746029e2e621f077944f9:13">*maxsplit=-1*</span><span data-offset-key="13f74a02a65746029e2e621f077944f9:14">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="144a29bad4124423bdded9a82001dc70"><span data-offset-key="144a29bad4124423bdded9a82001dc70:0">Split the binary sequence into subsequences of the same type, using </span><span data-offset-key="144a29bad4124423bdded9a82001dc70:1">*sep*</span><span data-offset-key="144a29bad4124423bdded9a82001dc70:2"> as the delimiter string. If </span><span data-offset-key="144a29bad4124423bdded9a82001dc70:3">*maxsplit*</span><span data-offset-key="144a29bad4124423bdded9a82001dc70:4"> is given and non-negative, at most </span><span data-offset-key="144a29bad4124423bdded9a82001dc70:5">*maxsplit*</span><span data-offset-key="144a29bad4124423bdded9a82001dc70:6"> splits are done (thus, the list will have at most </span><span data-offset-key="144a29bad4124423bdded9a82001dc70:7">`maxsplit+1`</span><span data-offset-key="144a29bad4124423bdded9a82001dc70:8"> elements). If </span><span data-offset-key="144a29bad4124423bdded9a82001dc70:9">*maxsplit*</span><span data-offset-key="144a29bad4124423bdded9a82001dc70:10"> is not specified or is </span><span data-offset-key="144a29bad4124423bdded9a82001dc70:11">`-1`</span><span data-offset-key="144a29bad4124423bdded9a82001dc70:12">, then there is no limit on the number of splits (all possible splits are made).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3da12d0ac3574d61840c77a2caedfd8d"><span data-offset-key="3da12d0ac3574d61840c77a2caedfd8d:0">If </span><span data-offset-key="3da12d0ac3574d61840c77a2caedfd8d:1">*sep*</span><span data-offset-key="3da12d0ac3574d61840c77a2caedfd8d:2"> is given, consecutive delimiters are not grouped together and are deemed to delimit empty subsequences (for example, </span><span data-offset-key="3da12d0ac3574d61840c77a2caedfd8d:3">`b'1,,2'.split(b',')`</span><span data-offset-key="3da12d0ac3574d61840c77a2caedfd8d:4"> returns </span><span data-offset-key="3da12d0ac3574d61840c77a2caedfd8d:5">`[b'1', b'',                                       b'2']`</span><span data-offset-key="3da12d0ac3574d61840c77a2caedfd8d:6">). The </span><span data-offset-key="3da12d0ac3574d61840c77a2caedfd8d:7">*sep*</span><span data-offset-key="3da12d0ac3574d61840c77a2caedfd8d:8"> argument may consist of a multibyte sequence (for example, </span><span data-offset-key="3da12d0ac3574d61840c77a2caedfd8d:9">`b'1<>2<>3'.split(b'<>')`</span><span data-offset-key="3da12d0ac3574d61840c77a2caedfd8d:10"> returns </span><span data-offset-key="3da12d0ac3574d61840c77a2caedfd8d:11">`[b'1', b'2',                                       b'3']`</span><span data-offset-key="3da12d0ac3574d61840c77a2caedfd8d:12">). Splitting an empty sequence with a specified separator returns </span><span data-offset-key="3da12d0ac3574d61840c77a2caedfd8d:13">`[b'']`</span><span data-offset-key="3da12d0ac3574d61840c77a2caedfd8d:14"> or </span><span data-offset-key="3da12d0ac3574d61840c77a2caedfd8d:15">`[bytearray(b'')]`</span><span data-offset-key="3da12d0ac3574d61840c77a2caedfd8d:16"> depending on the type of object being split. The </span><span data-offset-key="3da12d0ac3574d61840c77a2caedfd8d:17">*sep*</span><span data-offset-key="3da12d0ac3574d61840c77a2caedfd8d:18"> argument may be any </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-bytes-like-object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9a3a0641b383446daf28f55ebcbb5acf"><span data-offset-key="9a3a0641b383446daf28f55ebcbb5acf:0">bytes-like object</span></span></a><span data-key="c63711ad97db456abf1a510bc557afa5"><span data-offset-key="c63711ad97db456abf1a510bc557afa5:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a0c06bcc900e4f33ad90359cfc55f15b"><span data-offset-key="a0c06bcc900e4f33ad90359cfc55f15b:0">For example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> b'1,2,3'.split(b',')[b'1', b'2', b'3']>>> b'1,2,3'.split(b',', maxsplit=1)[b'1', b'2,3']>>> b'1,2,,3,'.split(b',')[b'1', b'2', b'', b'3', b'']

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="289b78007bb144c8a23cf2f490738a5c"><span data-offset-key="289b78007bb144c8a23cf2f490738a5c:0">If </span><span data-offset-key="289b78007bb144c8a23cf2f490738a5c:1">*sep*</span><span data-offset-key="289b78007bb144c8a23cf2f490738a5c:2"> is not specified or is </span><span data-offset-key="289b78007bb144c8a23cf2f490738a5c:3">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="289b78007bb144c8a23cf2f490738a5c:4">, a different splitting algorithm is applied: runs of consecutive ASCII whitespace are regarded as a single separator, and the result will contain no empty strings at the start or end if the sequence has leading or trailing whitespace. Consequently, splitting an empty sequence or a sequence consisting solely of ASCII whitespace without a specified separator returns </span><span data-offset-key="289b78007bb144c8a23cf2f490738a5c:5">`[]`</span><span data-offset-key="289b78007bb144c8a23cf2f490738a5c:6">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0475b388b70c4ef98c70ac6a7fc7de0c"><span data-offset-key="0475b388b70c4ef98c70ac6a7fc7de0c:0">For example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> b'1 2 3'.split()[b'1', b'2', b'3']>>> b'1 2 3'.split(maxsplit=1)[b'1', b'2 3']>>> b'   1   2   3   '.split()[b'1', b'2', b'3']

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0f7cd99ab8cb41879eee3b81e1ec70d7"><span data-offset-key="0f7cd99ab8cb41879eee3b81e1ec70d7:0">`bytes.strip`</span><span data-offset-key="0f7cd99ab8cb41879eee3b81e1ec70d7:1">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="0f7cd99ab8cb41879eee3b81e1ec70d7:2">*chars*</span><span data-offset-key="0f7cd99ab8cb41879eee3b81e1ec70d7:3">\])</span><span data-offset-key="0f7cd99ab8cb41879eee3b81e1ec70d7:4">`bytearray.strip`</span><span data-offset-key="0f7cd99ab8cb41879eee3b81e1ec70d7:5">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="0f7cd99ab8cb41879eee3b81e1ec70d7:6">*chars*</span><span data-offset-key="0f7cd99ab8cb41879eee3b81e1ec70d7:7">\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4df452e4d8f2475aae1ea2bfa54ff8e8"><span data-offset-key="4df452e4d8f2475aae1ea2bfa54ff8e8:0">Return a copy of the sequence with specified leading and trailing bytes removed. The </span><span data-offset-key="4df452e4d8f2475aae1ea2bfa54ff8e8:1">*chars*</span><span data-offset-key="4df452e4d8f2475aae1ea2bfa54ff8e8:2"> argument is a binary sequence specifying the set of byte values to be removed - the name refers to the fact this method is usually used with ASCII characters. If omitted or </span><span data-offset-key="4df452e4d8f2475aae1ea2bfa54ff8e8:3">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="4df452e4d8f2475aae1ea2bfa54ff8e8:4">, the </span><span data-offset-key="4df452e4d8f2475aae1ea2bfa54ff8e8:5">*chars*</span><span data-offset-key="4df452e4d8f2475aae1ea2bfa54ff8e8:6"> argument defaults to removing ASCII whitespace. The </span><span data-offset-key="4df452e4d8f2475aae1ea2bfa54ff8e8:7">*chars*</span><span data-offset-key="4df452e4d8f2475aae1ea2bfa54ff8e8:8"> argument is not a prefix or suffix; rather, all combinations of its values are stripped:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> b'   spacious   '.strip()b'spacious'>>> b'www.example.com'.strip(b'cmowz.')b'example'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c0b13cc3dc4c4ae892a1eb25a1adb8df"><span data-offset-key="c0b13cc3dc4c4ae892a1eb25a1adb8df:0">The binary sequence of byte values to remove may be any </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-bytes-like-object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ae09d4f5c7a84bf9ac20107d2d45c84c"><span data-offset-key="ae09d4f5c7a84bf9ac20107d2d45c84c:0">bytes-like object</span></span></a><span data-key="c011eed3fbe14e2e93ec5c7911ce88f3"><span data-offset-key="c011eed3fbe14e2e93ec5c7911ce88f3:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6e8fe3276e514c19adaafce30f8089e3"><span data-offset-key="6e8fe3276e514c19adaafce30f8089e3:0">Note </span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="bfb3c6e405864d8c81997405aaa00b7d"><span data-offset-key="bfb3c6e405864d8c81997405aaa00b7d:0">The bytearray version of this method does </span><span data-offset-key="bfb3c6e405864d8c81997405aaa00b7d:1">*not*</span><span data-offset-key="bfb3c6e405864d8c81997405aaa00b7d:2"> operate in place - it always produces a new object, even if no changes were made.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6b0ae53ea027473eb7440a7ee7d30e3b"><span data-offset-key="6b0ae53ea027473eb7440a7ee7d30e3b:0">The following methods on bytes and bytearray objects assume the use of ASCII compatible binary formats and should not be applied to arbitrary binary data. Note that all of the bytearray methods in this section do </span><span data-offset-key="6b0ae53ea027473eb7440a7ee7d30e3b:1">*not*</span><span data-offset-key="6b0ae53ea027473eb7440a7ee7d30e3b:2"> operate in place, and instead produce new objects.</span><span data-offset-key="6b0ae53ea027473eb7440a7ee7d30e3b:3">`bytes.capitalize`</span><span data-offset-key="6b0ae53ea027473eb7440a7ee7d30e3b:4">()</span><span data-offset-key="6b0ae53ea027473eb7440a7ee7d30e3b:5">`bytearray.capitalize`</span><span data-offset-key="6b0ae53ea027473eb7440a7ee7d30e3b:6">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6dcc04e47fd2410c8eb59dce40f9ba11"><span data-offset-key="6dcc04e47fd2410c8eb59dce40f9ba11:0">Return a copy of the sequence with each byte interpreted as an ASCII character, and the first byte capitalized and the rest lowercased. Non-ASCII byte values are passed through unchanged.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d5ea7b9957ef4c67aba8a9e7c8ac9a47"><span data-offset-key="d5ea7b9957ef4c67aba8a9e7c8ac9a47:0">Note </span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b6c5ade150594273830ab2a48079684a"><span data-offset-key="b6c5ade150594273830ab2a48079684a:0">The bytearray version of this method does </span><span data-offset-key="b6c5ade150594273830ab2a48079684a:1">*not*</span><span data-offset-key="b6c5ade150594273830ab2a48079684a:2"> operate in place - it always produces a new object, even if no changes were made.</span><span data-offset-key="b6c5ade150594273830ab2a48079684a:3">`bytes.expandtabs`</span><span data-offset-key="b6c5ade150594273830ab2a48079684a:4">(</span><span data-offset-key="b6c5ade150594273830ab2a48079684a:5">*tabsize=8*</span><span data-offset-key="b6c5ade150594273830ab2a48079684a:6">)</span><span data-offset-key="b6c5ade150594273830ab2a48079684a:7">`bytearray.expandtabs`</span><span data-offset-key="b6c5ade150594273830ab2a48079684a:8">(</span><span data-offset-key="b6c5ade150594273830ab2a48079684a:9">*tabsize=8*</span><span data-offset-key="b6c5ade150594273830ab2a48079684a:10">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="68b7b4b10426492ba20c7aaca0348484"><span data-offset-key="68b7b4b10426492ba20c7aaca0348484:0">Return a copy of the sequence where all ASCII tab characters are replaced by one or more ASCII spaces, depending on the current column and the given tab size. Tab positions occur every </span><span data-offset-key="68b7b4b10426492ba20c7aaca0348484:1">*tabsize*</span><span data-offset-key="68b7b4b10426492ba20c7aaca0348484:2"> bytes (default is 8, giving tab positions at columns 0, 8, 16 and so on). To expand the sequence, the current column is set to zero and the sequence is examined byte by byte. If the byte is an ASCII tab character (</span><span data-offset-key="68b7b4b10426492ba20c7aaca0348484:3">`b'\t'`</span><span data-offset-key="68b7b4b10426492ba20c7aaca0348484:4">), one or more space characters are inserted in the result until the current column is equal to the next tab position. (The tab character itself is not copied.) If the current byte is an ASCII newline (</span><span data-offset-key="68b7b4b10426492ba20c7aaca0348484:5">`b'\n'`</span><span data-offset-key="68b7b4b10426492ba20c7aaca0348484:6">) or carriage return (</span><span data-offset-key="68b7b4b10426492ba20c7aaca0348484:7">`b'\r'`</span><span data-offset-key="68b7b4b10426492ba20c7aaca0348484:8">), it is copied and the current column is reset to zero. Any other byte value is copied unchanged and the current column is incremented by one regardless of how the byte value is represented when printed:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> b'01\t012\t0123\t01234'.expandtabs()b'01      012     0123    01234'>>> b'01\t012\t0123\t01234'.expandtabs(4)b'01  012 0123    01234'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d2c8d3e0543f41c8aba8eab5727218c9"><span data-offset-key="d2c8d3e0543f41c8aba8eab5727218c9:0">Note </span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b10dc77d928640b5b7b2aa3b4a563c95"><span data-offset-key="b10dc77d928640b5b7b2aa3b4a563c95:0">The bytearray version of this method does </span><span data-offset-key="b10dc77d928640b5b7b2aa3b4a563c95:1">*not*</span><span data-offset-key="b10dc77d928640b5b7b2aa3b4a563c95:2"> operate in place - it always produces a new object, even if no changes were made.</span><span data-offset-key="b10dc77d928640b5b7b2aa3b4a563c95:3">`bytes.isalnum`</span><span data-offset-key="b10dc77d928640b5b7b2aa3b4a563c95:4">()</span><span data-offset-key="b10dc77d928640b5b7b2aa3b4a563c95:5">`bytearray.isalnum`</span><span data-offset-key="b10dc77d928640b5b7b2aa3b4a563c95:6">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="35010ab3f6ac46e6aa825faf60460fbc"><span data-offset-key="35010ab3f6ac46e6aa825faf60460fbc:0">Return </span><span data-offset-key="35010ab3f6ac46e6aa825faf60460fbc:1">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="35010ab3f6ac46e6aa825faf60460fbc:2"> if all bytes in the sequence are alphabetical ASCII characters or ASCII decimal digits and the sequence is not empty, </span><span data-offset-key="35010ab3f6ac46e6aa825faf60460fbc:3">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="35010ab3f6ac46e6aa825faf60460fbc:4"> otherwise. Alphabetic ASCII characters are those byte values in the sequence </span><span data-offset-key="35010ab3f6ac46e6aa825faf60460fbc:5">`b'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyzABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ'`</span><span data-offset-key="35010ab3f6ac46e6aa825faf60460fbc:6">. ASCII decimal digits are those byte values in the sequence </span><span data-offset-key="35010ab3f6ac46e6aa825faf60460fbc:7">`b'0123456789'`</span><span data-offset-key="35010ab3f6ac46e6aa825faf60460fbc:8">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b073420f19264c78a875bee36a719c9f"><span data-offset-key="b073420f19264c78a875bee36a719c9f:0">For example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> b'ABCabc1'.isalnum()True>>> b'ABC abc1'.isalnum()False

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="eaa0b733e50e42cc9707f8931931ab99"><span data-offset-key="eaa0b733e50e42cc9707f8931931ab99:0">`bytes.isalpha`</span><span data-offset-key="eaa0b733e50e42cc9707f8931931ab99:1">()</span><span data-offset-key="eaa0b733e50e42cc9707f8931931ab99:2">`bytearray.isalpha`</span><span data-offset-key="eaa0b733e50e42cc9707f8931931ab99:3">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7f9367f0ab914307b6c15f71a5c3f2e6"><span data-offset-key="7f9367f0ab914307b6c15f71a5c3f2e6:0">Return </span><span data-offset-key="7f9367f0ab914307b6c15f71a5c3f2e6:1">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="7f9367f0ab914307b6c15f71a5c3f2e6:2"> if all bytes in the sequence are alphabetic ASCII characters and the sequence is not empty, </span><span data-offset-key="7f9367f0ab914307b6c15f71a5c3f2e6:3">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="7f9367f0ab914307b6c15f71a5c3f2e6:4"> otherwise. Alphabetic ASCII characters are those byte values in the sequence </span><span data-offset-key="7f9367f0ab914307b6c15f71a5c3f2e6:5">`b'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyzABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ'`</span><span data-offset-key="7f9367f0ab914307b6c15f71a5c3f2e6:6">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="97a5988d6ea146958b77a0e209644d53"><span data-offset-key="97a5988d6ea146958b77a0e209644d53:0">For example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> b'ABCabc'.isalpha()True>>> b'ABCabc1'.isalpha()False

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e3bc172dfd244a86bc23b0846ae8b9bb"><span data-offset-key="e3bc172dfd244a86bc23b0846ae8b9bb:0">`bytes.isascii`</span><span data-offset-key="e3bc172dfd244a86bc23b0846ae8b9bb:1">()</span><span data-offset-key="e3bc172dfd244a86bc23b0846ae8b9bb:2">`bytearray.isascii`</span><span data-offset-key="e3bc172dfd244a86bc23b0846ae8b9bb:3">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1bc22f00d07c4a58a3aa61804065b94c"><span data-offset-key="1bc22f00d07c4a58a3aa61804065b94c:0">Return </span><span data-offset-key="1bc22f00d07c4a58a3aa61804065b94c:1">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="1bc22f00d07c4a58a3aa61804065b94c:2"> if the sequence is empty or all bytes in the sequence are ASCII, </span><span data-offset-key="1bc22f00d07c4a58a3aa61804065b94c:3">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="1bc22f00d07c4a58a3aa61804065b94c:4"> otherwise. ASCII bytes are in the range 0-0x7F.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="aadc7aee1b1b4d629370b453fbfb15f0"><span data-offset-key="aadc7aee1b1b4d629370b453fbfb15f0:0">Return </span><span data-offset-key="aadc7aee1b1b4d629370b453fbfb15f0:1">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="aadc7aee1b1b4d629370b453fbfb15f0:2"> if all bytes in the sequence are ASCII whitespace and the sequence is not empty, </span><span data-offset-key="aadc7aee1b1b4d629370b453fbfb15f0:3">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="aadc7aee1b1b4d629370b453fbfb15f0:4"> otherwise. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e924f652ca9f4c9dadfd947e3607e658"><span data-offset-key="e924f652ca9f4c9dadfd947e3607e658:0">Lowercase ASCII characters are those byte values in the sequence </span><span data-offset-key="e924f652ca9f4c9dadfd947e3607e658:1">`b'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz'`</span><span data-offset-key="e924f652ca9f4c9dadfd947e3607e658:2">. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f846a06ff50c447c9da85d54120f9aa5"><span data-offset-key="f846a06ff50c447c9da85d54120f9aa5:0">Lowercase ASCII characters are those byte values in the sequence </span><span data-offset-key="f846a06ff50c447c9da85d54120f9aa5:1">`b'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz'`</span><span data-offset-key="f846a06ff50c447c9da85d54120f9aa5:2">. Uppercase ASCII characters are those byte values in the sequence </span><span data-offset-key="f846a06ff50c447c9da85d54120f9aa5:3">`b'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ'`</span><span data-offset-key="f846a06ff50c447c9da85d54120f9aa5:4">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="587e7ccdbfe94a309a3d6d354042ca99"><span data-offset-key="587e7ccdbfe94a309a3d6d354042ca99:0">Note </span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3aeea445c64e4e7d8504d94a4e354358"><span data-offset-key="3aeea445c64e4e7d8504d94a4e354358:0">The bytearray version of this method does </span><span data-offset-key="3aeea445c64e4e7d8504d94a4e354358:1">*not*</span><span data-offset-key="3aeea445c64e4e7d8504d94a4e354358:2"> operate in place - it always produces a new object, even if no changes were made.</span><span data-offset-key="3aeea445c64e4e7d8504d94a4e354358:3">`bytes.splitlines`</span><span data-offset-key="3aeea445c64e4e7d8504d94a4e354358:4">(</span><span data-offset-key="3aeea445c64e4e7d8504d94a4e354358:5">*keepends=False*</span><span data-offset-key="3aeea445c64e4e7d8504d94a4e354358:6">)</span><span data-offset-key="3aeea445c64e4e7d8504d94a4e354358:7">`bytearray.splitlines`</span><span data-offset-key="3aeea445c64e4e7d8504d94a4e354358:8">(</span><span data-offset-key="3aeea445c64e4e7d8504d94a4e354358:9">*keepends=False*</span><span data-offset-key="3aeea445c64e4e7d8504d94a4e354358:10">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9d541eb7de8340e3abc4db555ed5efc9"><span data-offset-key="9d541eb7de8340e3abc4db555ed5efc9:0">Return a list of the lines in the binary sequence, breaking at ASCII line boundaries. This method uses the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-universal-newlines" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b4ed367c10bc4f25a848ddc839079b6b"><span data-offset-key="b4ed367c10bc4f25a848ddc839079b6b:0">universal newlines</span></span></a><span data-key="b88353fed6e14065ae5a8f0821451a64"><span data-offset-key="b88353fed6e14065ae5a8f0821451a64:0"> approach to splitting lines. Line breaks are not included in the resulting list unless </span><span data-offset-key="b88353fed6e14065ae5a8f0821451a64:1">*keepends*</span><span data-offset-key="b88353fed6e14065ae5a8f0821451a64:2"> is given and true.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="527bc5ffca8e4579b8720944922983fb"><span data-offset-key="527bc5ffca8e4579b8720944922983fb:0">For example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> b'ab c\n\nde fg\rkl\r\n'.splitlines()[b'ab c', b'', b'de fg', b'kl']>>> b'ab c\n\nde fg\rkl\r\n'.splitlines(keepends=True)[b'ab c\n', b'\n', b'de fg\r', b'kl\r\n']

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ef685437abff47cd974acd6ef69f4d9a"><span data-offset-key="ef685437abff47cd974acd6ef69f4d9a:0">Unlike </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes.split" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0d6ea3becb574b8bbcee928d67279f45"><span data-offset-key="0d6ea3becb574b8bbcee928d67279f45:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">split()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ed31b828ee28415da18f82c41a67f788"><span data-offset-key="ed31b828ee28415da18f82c41a67f788:0"> when a delimiter string </span><span data-offset-key="ed31b828ee28415da18f82c41a67f788:1">*sep*</span><span data-offset-key="ed31b828ee28415da18f82c41a67f788:2"> is given, this method returns an empty list for the empty string, and a terminal line break does not result in an extra line:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> b"".split(b'\n'), b"Two lines\n".split(b'\n')([b''], [b'Two lines', b''])>>> b"".splitlines(), b"One line\n".splitlines()([], [b'One line'])

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="974c67e27ffb4c6693f9869443b8ab0e"><span data-offset-key="974c67e27ffb4c6693f9869443b8ab0e:0">`bytes.swapcase`</span><span data-offset-key="974c67e27ffb4c6693f9869443b8ab0e:1">()</span><span data-offset-key="974c67e27ffb4c6693f9869443b8ab0e:2">`bytearray.swapcase`</span><span data-offset-key="974c67e27ffb4c6693f9869443b8ab0e:3">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f629a615f98749e99f3a3b4369bd8110"><span data-offset-key="f629a615f98749e99f3a3b4369bd8110:0">Return a copy of the sequence with all the lowercase ASCII characters converted to their corresponding uppercase counterpart and vice-versa.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="980642de049347a889c5522b9f3f7160"><span data-offset-key="980642de049347a889c5522b9f3f7160:0">For example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> b'Hello World'.swapcase()b'hELLO wORLD'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a08e27bcb7de47609bd3df62272d827b"><span data-offset-key="a08e27bcb7de47609bd3df62272d827b:0">Lowercase ASCII characters are those byte values in the sequence </span><span data-offset-key="a08e27bcb7de47609bd3df62272d827b:1">`b'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz'`</span><span data-offset-key="a08e27bcb7de47609bd3df62272d827b:2">. Uppercase ASCII characters are those byte values in the sequence </span><span data-offset-key="a08e27bcb7de47609bd3df62272d827b:3">`b'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ'`</span><span data-offset-key="a08e27bcb7de47609bd3df62272d827b:4">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="be62f752c07042d1a6c28bbd5b3659de"><span data-offset-key="be62f752c07042d1a6c28bbd5b3659de:0">Unlike </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str.swapcase" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b1950209d7494fe4a2987d5368bddd95"><span data-offset-key="b1950209d7494fe4a2987d5368bddd95:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str.swapcase()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="c372f32c1a8048cf9fdc17e6607fd2b4"><span data-offset-key="c372f32c1a8048cf9fdc17e6607fd2b4:0">, it is always the case that </span><span data-offset-key="c372f32c1a8048cf9fdc17e6607fd2b4:1">`bin.swapcase().swapcase() == bin`</span><span data-offset-key="c372f32c1a8048cf9fdc17e6607fd2b4:2"> for the binary versions. Case conversions are symmetrical in ASCII, even though that is not generally true for arbitrary Unicode code points.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6c5e6ac7283e463f84d99b26209a4609"><span data-offset-key="6c5e6ac7283e463f84d99b26209a4609:0">Note </span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5af07ff908914942a39a1386903627a1"><span data-offset-key="5af07ff908914942a39a1386903627a1:0">The bytearray version of this method does </span><span data-offset-key="5af07ff908914942a39a1386903627a1:1">*not*</span><span data-offset-key="5af07ff908914942a39a1386903627a1:2"> operate in place - it always produces a new object, even if no changes were made.</span><span data-offset-key="5af07ff908914942a39a1386903627a1:3">`bytes.title`</span><span data-offset-key="5af07ff908914942a39a1386903627a1:4">()</span><span data-offset-key="5af07ff908914942a39a1386903627a1:5">`bytearray.title`</span><span data-offset-key="5af07ff908914942a39a1386903627a1:6">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c4f2860722c44066878923c1761d4d68"><span data-offset-key="c4f2860722c44066878923c1761d4d68:0">Return a titlecased version of the binary sequence where words start with an uppercase ASCII character and the remaining characters are lowercase. Uncased byte values are left unmodified.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d83a473ddf5449cfb3019c2734d8e27b"><span data-offset-key="d83a473ddf5449cfb3019c2734d8e27b:0">For example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> b'Hello world'.title()b'Hello World'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="25e22cdbc3cd45159932eabbe53c5502"><span data-offset-key="25e22cdbc3cd45159932eabbe53c5502:0">Lowercase ASCII characters are those byte values in the sequence </span><span data-offset-key="25e22cdbc3cd45159932eabbe53c5502:1">`b'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz'`</span><span data-offset-key="25e22cdbc3cd45159932eabbe53c5502:2">. Uppercase ASCII characters are those byte values in the sequence </span><span data-offset-key="25e22cdbc3cd45159932eabbe53c5502:3">`b'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ'`</span><span data-offset-key="25e22cdbc3cd45159932eabbe53c5502:4">. All other byte values are uncased.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d17219002e8345b4acb1f1614fc692c0"><span data-offset-key="d17219002e8345b4acb1f1614fc692c0:0">The algorithm uses a simple language-independent definition of a word as groups of consecutive letters. The definition works in many contexts but it means that apostrophes in contractions and possessives form word boundaries, which may not be the desired result:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> b"they're bill's friends from the UK".title()b"They'Re Bill'S Friends From The Uk"

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="26d03be5d26d49379d8c330f0f3dd3cc"><span data-offset-key="26d03be5d26d49379d8c330f0f3dd3cc:0">A workaround for apostrophes can be constructed using regular expressions:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> import re>>> def titlecase(s):...     return re.sub(rb"[A-Za-z]+('[A-Za-z]+)?",...                   lambda mo: mo.group(0)[0:1].upper() +...                              mo.group(0)[1:].lower(),...                   s)...>>> titlecase(b"they're bill's friends.")b"They're Bill's Friends."

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ac32fd9ae8654844a5a67335155dcbf5"><span data-offset-key="ac32fd9ae8654844a5a67335155dcbf5:0">Note </span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="25e8253d2b9740c6a0001d8e7b64a9bc"><span data-offset-key="25e8253d2b9740c6a0001d8e7b64a9bc:0">The bytearray version of this method does </span><span data-offset-key="25e8253d2b9740c6a0001d8e7b64a9bc:1">*not*</span><span data-offset-key="25e8253d2b9740c6a0001d8e7b64a9bc:2"> operate in place - it always produces a new object, even if no changes were made.</span><span data-offset-key="25e8253d2b9740c6a0001d8e7b64a9bc:3">`bytes.upper`</span><span data-offset-key="25e8253d2b9740c6a0001d8e7b64a9bc:4">()</span><span data-offset-key="25e8253d2b9740c6a0001d8e7b64a9bc:5">`bytearray.upper`</span><span data-offset-key="25e8253d2b9740c6a0001d8e7b64a9bc:6">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="40374faea48f478395851f7ccec540db"><span data-offset-key="40374faea48f478395851f7ccec540db:0">Return a copy of the sequence with all the lowercase ASCII characters converted to their corresponding uppercase counterpart.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ecdf00268f184afdb59f28bae23bd0dc"><span data-offset-key="ecdf00268f184afdb59f28bae23bd0dc:0">For example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> b'Hello World'.upper()b'HELLO WORLD'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1ddfc9e270364d72bfa56d5c6e2db0b4"><span data-offset-key="1ddfc9e270364d72bfa56d5c6e2db0b4:0">Lowercase ASCII characters are those byte values in the sequence </span><span data-offset-key="1ddfc9e270364d72bfa56d5c6e2db0b4:1">`b'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz'`</span><span data-offset-key="1ddfc9e270364d72bfa56d5c6e2db0b4:2">. Uppercase ASCII characters are those byte values in the sequence </span><span data-offset-key="1ddfc9e270364d72bfa56d5c6e2db0b4:3">`b'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ'`</span><span data-offset-key="1ddfc9e270364d72bfa56d5c6e2db0b4:4">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7c9994e76d634094b8a50aa4a3e60d01"><span data-offset-key="7c9994e76d634094b8a50aa4a3e60d01:0">Note </span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8a263a2244a74941a20f4851dd6d49d6"><span data-offset-key="8a263a2244a74941a20f4851dd6d49d6:0">The bytearray version of this method does </span><span data-offset-key="8a263a2244a74941a20f4851dd6d49d6:1">*not*</span><span data-offset-key="8a263a2244a74941a20f4851dd6d49d6:2"> operate in place - it always produces a new object, even if no changes were made.</span><span data-offset-key="8a263a2244a74941a20f4851dd6d49d6:3">`bytes.zfill`</span><span data-offset-key="8a263a2244a74941a20f4851dd6d49d6:4">(</span><span data-offset-key="8a263a2244a74941a20f4851dd6d49d6:5">*width*</span><span data-offset-key="8a263a2244a74941a20f4851dd6d49d6:6">)</span><span data-offset-key="8a263a2244a74941a20f4851dd6d49d6:7">`bytearray.zfill`</span><span data-offset-key="8a263a2244a74941a20f4851dd6d49d6:8">(</span><span data-offset-key="8a263a2244a74941a20f4851dd6d49d6:9">*width*</span><span data-offset-key="8a263a2244a74941a20f4851dd6d49d6:10">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="01201ffb4fc541bcbe81fbb506011a07"><span data-offset-key="01201ffb4fc541bcbe81fbb506011a07:0">Return a copy of the sequence left filled with ASCII </span><span data-offset-key="01201ffb4fc541bcbe81fbb506011a07:1">`b'0'`</span><span data-offset-key="01201ffb4fc541bcbe81fbb506011a07:2"> digits to make a sequence of length </span><span data-offset-key="01201ffb4fc541bcbe81fbb506011a07:3">*width*</span><span data-offset-key="01201ffb4fc541bcbe81fbb506011a07:4">. A leading sign prefix (</span><span data-offset-key="01201ffb4fc541bcbe81fbb506011a07:5">`b'+'`</span><span data-offset-key="01201ffb4fc541bcbe81fbb506011a07:6">/ </span><span data-offset-key="01201ffb4fc541bcbe81fbb506011a07:7">`b'-'`</span><span data-offset-key="01201ffb4fc541bcbe81fbb506011a07:8">) is handled by inserting the padding </span><span data-offset-key="01201ffb4fc541bcbe81fbb506011a07:9">*after*</span><span data-offset-key="01201ffb4fc541bcbe81fbb506011a07:10"> the sign character rather than before. For </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e0443c779b4242b6b4b405b8cc183505"><span data-offset-key="e0443c779b4242b6b4b405b8cc183505:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytes</code></span></span></a><span data-key="67b287ea970240c883a0bd9f88e3600b"><span data-offset-key="67b287ea970240c883a0bd9f88e3600b:0"> objects, the original sequence is returned if </span><span data-offset-key="67b287ea970240c883a0bd9f88e3600b:1">*width*</span><span data-offset-key="67b287ea970240c883a0bd9f88e3600b:2"> is less than or equal to </span><span data-offset-key="67b287ea970240c883a0bd9f88e3600b:3">`len(seq)`</span><span data-offset-key="67b287ea970240c883a0bd9f88e3600b:4">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c4e662a8972a45528de0f6af5b0c3e35"><span data-offset-key="c4e662a8972a45528de0f6af5b0c3e35:0">For example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> b"42".zfill(5)b'00042'>>> b"-42".zfill(5)b'-0042'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="918970801a6541deb2f5bb3dd1061e3b"><span data-offset-key="918970801a6541deb2f5bb3dd1061e3b:0">Note </span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e9dee47c30e648549cac1c8102b9d309"><span data-offset-key="e9dee47c30e648549cac1c8102b9d309:0">The bytearray version of this method does </span><span data-offset-key="e9dee47c30e648549cac1c8102b9d309:1">*not*</span><span data-offset-key="e9dee47c30e648549cac1c8102b9d309:2"> operate in place - it always produces a new object, even if no changes were made.</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="53cbea9f22b84f5f81cde7fdbe3a023a"><span data-offset-key="53cbea9f22b84f5f81cde7fdbe3a023a:0">`printf`</span><span data-offset-key="53cbea9f22b84f5f81cde7fdbe3a023a:1">-style Bytes Formatting</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d4b22d1036784f46a85b6b14f8bfd468"><span data-offset-key="d4b22d1036784f46a85b6b14f8bfd468:0">Note </span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="51f4c893b2e14bbeab6ba9e95f48497a"><span data-offset-key="51f4c893b2e14bbeab6ba9e95f48497a:0">The formatting operations described here exhibit a variety of quirks that lead to a number of common errors (such as failing to display tuples and dictionaries correctly). If the value being printed may be a tuple or dictionary, wrap it in a tuple.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="beed87d6a8724b90a005b28b7dfa38b1"><span data-offset-key="beed87d6a8724b90a005b28b7dfa38b1:0">Bytes objects (</span><span data-offset-key="beed87d6a8724b90a005b28b7dfa38b1:1">`bytes`</span><span data-offset-key="beed87d6a8724b90a005b28b7dfa38b1:2">/</span><span data-offset-key="beed87d6a8724b90a005b28b7dfa38b1:3">`bytearray`</span><span data-offset-key="beed87d6a8724b90a005b28b7dfa38b1:4">) have one unique built-in operation: the </span><span data-offset-key="beed87d6a8724b90a005b28b7dfa38b1:5">`%`</span><span data-offset-key="beed87d6a8724b90a005b28b7dfa38b1:6"> operator (modulo). This is also known as the bytes </span><span data-offset-key="beed87d6a8724b90a005b28b7dfa38b1:7">*formatting*</span><span data-offset-key="beed87d6a8724b90a005b28b7dfa38b1:8"> or </span><span data-offset-key="beed87d6a8724b90a005b28b7dfa38b1:9">*interpolation*</span><span data-offset-key="beed87d6a8724b90a005b28b7dfa38b1:10"> operator. Given </span><span data-offset-key="beed87d6a8724b90a005b28b7dfa38b1:11">`format % values`</span><span data-offset-key="beed87d6a8724b90a005b28b7dfa38b1:12"> (where </span><span data-offset-key="beed87d6a8724b90a005b28b7dfa38b1:13">*format*</span><span data-offset-key="beed87d6a8724b90a005b28b7dfa38b1:14"> is a bytes object), </span><span data-offset-key="beed87d6a8724b90a005b28b7dfa38b1:15">`%`</span><span data-offset-key="beed87d6a8724b90a005b28b7dfa38b1:16"> conversion specifications in </span><span data-offset-key="beed87d6a8724b90a005b28b7dfa38b1:17">*format*</span><span data-offset-key="beed87d6a8724b90a005b28b7dfa38b1:18"> are replaced with zero or more elements of </span><span data-offset-key="beed87d6a8724b90a005b28b7dfa38b1:19">*values*</span><span data-offset-key="beed87d6a8724b90a005b28b7dfa38b1:20">. The effect is similar to using the </span><span data-offset-key="beed87d6a8724b90a005b28b7dfa38b1:21">`sprintf()`</span><span data-offset-key="beed87d6a8724b90a005b28b7dfa38b1:22"> in the C language.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="31d264b03d3d435880b6859421f87ef8"><span data-offset-key="31d264b03d3d435880b6859421f87ef8:0">If </span><span data-offset-key="31d264b03d3d435880b6859421f87ef8:1">*format*</span><span data-offset-key="31d264b03d3d435880b6859421f87ef8:2"> requires a single argument, </span><span data-offset-key="31d264b03d3d435880b6859421f87ef8:3">*values*</span><span data-offset-key="31d264b03d3d435880b6859421f87ef8:4"> may be a single non-tuple object. </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#id16" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="320f90a0f88e45b486a5bd1591c276b5"><span data-offset-key="320f90a0f88e45b486a5bd1591c276b5:0">5</span></span></a><span data-key="c91309a1376e4a97b764f23770945c96"><span data-offset-key="c91309a1376e4a97b764f23770945c96:0"> Otherwise, </span><span data-offset-key="c91309a1376e4a97b764f23770945c96:1">*values*</span><span data-offset-key="c91309a1376e4a97b764f23770945c96:2"> must be a tuple with exactly the number of items specified by the format bytes object, or a single mapping object (for example, a dictionary).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6ed21d75287c4c33b4a66a40dd3a8adc"><span data-offset-key="6ed21d75287c4c33b4a66a40dd3a8adc:0">A conversion specifier contains two or more characters and has the following components, which must occur in this order:</span></span></span>

1.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c5a0fe7ed8694c3286211a6aaac950f9"><span data-offset-key="c5a0fe7ed8694c3286211a6aaac950f9:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="c5a0fe7ed8694c3286211a6aaac950f9:1">`'%'`</span><span data-offset-key="c5a0fe7ed8694c3286211a6aaac950f9:2"> character, which marks the start of the specifier.</span></span></span>

2.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="630648224a2748648ceb241d55ed95f8"><span data-offset-key="630648224a2748648ceb241d55ed95f8:0">Mapping key (optional), consisting of a parenthesised sequence of characters (for example, </span><span data-offset-key="630648224a2748648ceb241d55ed95f8:1">`(somename)`</span><span data-offset-key="630648224a2748648ceb241d55ed95f8:2">).</span></span></span>

3.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2d8d8e963a9f42bd936a8c670e9213d9"><span data-offset-key="2d8d8e963a9f42bd936a8c670e9213d9:0">Conversion flags (optional), which affect the result of some conversion types.</span></span></span>

4.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="dff506f318aa4f73bb4a89c20984bb83"><span data-offset-key="dff506f318aa4f73bb4a89c20984bb83:0">Minimum field width (optional). If specified as an </span><span data-offset-key="dff506f318aa4f73bb4a89c20984bb83:1">`'*'`</span><span data-offset-key="dff506f318aa4f73bb4a89c20984bb83:2"> (asterisk), the actual width is read from the next element of the tuple in </span><span data-offset-key="dff506f318aa4f73bb4a89c20984bb83:3">*values*</span><span data-offset-key="dff506f318aa4f73bb4a89c20984bb83:4">, and the object to convert comes after the minimum field width and optional precision.</span></span></span>

5.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a711bad613534db1a6e9bb030045d4fc"><span data-offset-key="a711bad613534db1a6e9bb030045d4fc:0">Precision (optional), given as a </span><span data-offset-key="a711bad613534db1a6e9bb030045d4fc:1">`'.'`</span><span data-offset-key="a711bad613534db1a6e9bb030045d4fc:2"> (dot) followed by the precision. If specified as </span><span data-offset-key="a711bad613534db1a6e9bb030045d4fc:3">`'*'`</span><span data-offset-key="a711bad613534db1a6e9bb030045d4fc:4"> (an asterisk), the actual precision is read from the next element of the tuple in </span><span data-offset-key="a711bad613534db1a6e9bb030045d4fc:5">*values*</span><span data-offset-key="a711bad613534db1a6e9bb030045d4fc:6">, and the value to convert comes after the precision.</span></span></span>

6.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="daa524b618e24787b4d435e0d3c7278e"><span data-offset-key="daa524b618e24787b4d435e0d3c7278e:0">Length modifier (optional).</span></span></span>

7.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="66ef048cd4cd45a8b2ec5ca191d17792"><span data-offset-key="66ef048cd4cd45a8b2ec5ca191d17792:0">Conversion type.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3c8d69655cde429383a4bf46e9f0e6bd"><span data-offset-key="3c8d69655cde429383a4bf46e9f0e6bd:0">When the right argument is a dictionary (or other mapping type), then the formats in the bytes object </span><span data-offset-key="3c8d69655cde429383a4bf46e9f0e6bd:1">*must*</span><span data-offset-key="3c8d69655cde429383a4bf46e9f0e6bd:2"> include a parenthesised mapping key into that dictionary inserted immediately after the </span><span data-offset-key="3c8d69655cde429383a4bf46e9f0e6bd:3">`'%'`</span><span data-offset-key="3c8d69655cde429383a4bf46e9f0e6bd:4"> character. The mapping key selects the value to be formatted from the mapping. For example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> print(b'%(language)s has %(number)03d quote types.' %...       {b'language': b"Python", b"number": 2})b'Python has 002 quote types.'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7867d9e611514ca29c03f9d2ce564542"><span data-offset-key="7867d9e611514ca29c03f9d2ce564542:0">In this case no </span><span data-offset-key="7867d9e611514ca29c03f9d2ce564542:1">`*`</span><span data-offset-key="7867d9e611514ca29c03f9d2ce564542:2"> specifiers may occur in a format (since they require a sequential parameter list).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2cf6b4b2aa5b4bb19db084b087d6c6fe"><span data-offset-key="2cf6b4b2aa5b4bb19db084b087d6c6fe:0">The conversion flag characters are:</span></span></span>

<table><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><tbody><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--UIH400-4e41e82a--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="cdc41980fa14471fa29629f6fc4de57b"><span data-offset-key="cdc41980fa14471fa29629f6fc4de57b:0">Flag</span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--UIH400-4e41e82a--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="891402e3bc74448d81a9fa6d1d0cb759"><span data-offset-key="891402e3bc74448d81a9fa6d1d0cb759:0">Meaning</span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="even"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="07f53513f3c04edbb0edeeb82496874d"><span data-offset-key="07f53513f3c04edbb0edeeb82496874d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">'#'</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="baad6befa5c04e93824b155ad644cd4b"><span data-offset-key="baad6befa5c04e93824b155ad644cd4b:0">The value conversion will use the “alternate form” (where defined below).</span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4f137921ece94c83bb99cb3a951b3646"><span data-offset-key="4f137921ece94c83bb99cb3a951b3646:0"><code class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1cc90d65d5864243b6816cd8f4802e6e"><span data-offset-key="1cc90d65d5864243b6816cd8f4802e6e:0">The conversion will be zero padded for numeric values.</span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="even"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6843d1d83bcf4e5c978dde910a5cf23a"><span data-offset-key="6843d1d83bcf4e5c978dde910a5cf23a:0">The converted value is left adjusted (overrides the </span><span data-offset-key="6843d1d83bcf4e5c978dde910a5cf23a:1"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">'0'</code></span><span data-offset-key="6843d1d83bcf4e5c978dde910a5cf23a:2"> conversion if both are given).</span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8b3ad0f28f364bb381fec41b02a34e92"><span data-offset-key="8b3ad0f28f364bb381fec41b02a34e92:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">' '</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-slate-leaf="true">'+'</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3eb509f8b8684d0c9ff3046b8ee2a538"><span data-offset-key="3eb509f8b8684d0c9ff3046b8ee2a538:0">A sign character (</span><span data-offset-key="3eb509f8b8684d0c9ff3046b8ee2a538:1"><code will precede the conversion (overrides a “space” flag).</span></span></span></p></td></tr></tbody></table>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e8a3d506e8354e82a1b555ead7a93c09"><span data-offset-key="e8a3d506e8354e82a1b555ead7a93c09:0">A length modifier (</span><span data-offset-key="e8a3d506e8354e82a1b555ead7a93c09:1">`h`</span><span data-offset-key="e8a3d506e8354e82a1b555ead7a93c09:2">, </span><span data-offset-key="e8a3d506e8354e82a1b555ead7a93c09:3">`l`</span><span data-offset-key="e8a3d506e8354e82a1b555ead7a93c09:4">, or </span><span data-offset-key="e8a3d506e8354e82a1b555ead7a93c09:5">`L`</span><span data-offset-key="e8a3d506e8354e82a1b555ead7a93c09:6">) may be present, but is ignored as it is not necessary for Python – so e.g. </span><span data-offset-key="e8a3d506e8354e82a1b555ead7a93c09:7">`%ld`</span><span data-offset-key="e8a3d506e8354e82a1b555ead7a93c09:8"> is identical to </span><span data-offset-key="e8a3d506e8354e82a1b555ead7a93c09:9">`%d`</span><span data-offset-key="e8a3d506e8354e82a1b555ead7a93c09:10">.</span></span></span>
