<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="47ff064a54cb464a83de42f0f248acd5"><span data-offset-key="47ff064a54cb464a83de42f0f248acd5:0">Test whether the set is a proper subset of </span><span data-offset-key="47ff064a54cb464a83de42f0f248acd5:1">*other*</span><span data-offset-key="47ff064a54cb464a83de42f0f248acd5:2">, that is, </span><span data-offset-key="47ff064a54cb464a83de42f0f248acd5:3">`set <= other and set != other`</span><span data-offset-key="47ff064a54cb464a83de42f0f248acd5:4">.</span><span data-offset-key="47ff064a54cb464a83de42f0f248acd5:5">`issuperset`</span><span data-offset-key="47ff064a54cb464a83de42f0f248acd5:6">(</span><span data-offset-key="47ff064a54cb464a83de42f0f248acd5:7">*other*</span><span data-offset-key="47ff064a54cb464a83de42f0f248acd5:8">)</span><span data-offset-key="47ff064a54cb464a83de42f0f248acd5:9">`set >= other`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a8d5d36f3114426d9453b774c709372d"><span data-offset-key="a8d5d36f3114426d9453b774c709372d:0">Test whether every element in </span><span data-offset-key="a8d5d36f3114426d9453b774c709372d:1">*other*</span><span data-offset-key="a8d5d36f3114426d9453b774c709372d:2"> is in the set.</span><span data-offset-key="a8d5d36f3114426d9453b774c709372d:3">`set > other`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="21daf7857eab4596844abb039fb7505a"><span data-offset-key="21daf7857eab4596844abb039fb7505a:0">Test whether the set is a proper superset of </span><span data-offset-key="21daf7857eab4596844abb039fb7505a:1">*other*</span><span data-offset-key="21daf7857eab4596844abb039fb7505a:2">, that is, </span><span data-offset-key="21daf7857eab4596844abb039fb7505a:3">`set >= other and set != other`</span><span data-offset-key="21daf7857eab4596844abb039fb7505a:4">.</span><span data-offset-key="21daf7857eab4596844abb039fb7505a:5">`union`</span><span data-offset-key="21daf7857eab4596844abb039fb7505a:6">(</span><span data-offset-key="21daf7857eab4596844abb039fb7505a:7">*\*others*</span><span data-offset-key="21daf7857eab4596844abb039fb7505a:8">)</span><span data-offset-key="21daf7857eab4596844abb039fb7505a:9">`set | other | ...`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d6b2a3233ec5446086c5de3eec138b97"><span data-offset-key="d6b2a3233ec5446086c5de3eec138b97:0">Return a new set with elements from the set and all others.</span><span data-offset-key="d6b2a3233ec5446086c5de3eec138b97:1">`intersection`</span><span data-offset-key="d6b2a3233ec5446086c5de3eec138b97:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="d6b2a3233ec5446086c5de3eec138b97:3">*\*others*</span><span data-offset-key="d6b2a3233ec5446086c5de3eec138b97:4">)</span><span data-offset-key="d6b2a3233ec5446086c5de3eec138b97:5">`set & other & ...`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="43bf3ac3ef054a948cd6b3390bb866b9"><span data-offset-key="43bf3ac3ef054a948cd6b3390bb866b9:0">Return a new set with elements common to the set and all others.</span><span data-offset-key="43bf3ac3ef054a948cd6b3390bb866b9:1">`difference`</span><span data-offset-key="43bf3ac3ef054a948cd6b3390bb866b9:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="43bf3ac3ef054a948cd6b3390bb866b9:3">*\*others*</span><span data-offset-key="43bf3ac3ef054a948cd6b3390bb866b9:4">)</span><span data-offset-key="43bf3ac3ef054a948cd6b3390bb866b9:5">`set - other - ...`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="597ffa476870437293de5b0db5df3f92"><span data-offset-key="597ffa476870437293de5b0db5df3f92:0">Return a new set with elements in the set that are not in the others.</span><span data-offset-key="597ffa476870437293de5b0db5df3f92:1">`symmetric_difference`</span><span data-offset-key="597ffa476870437293de5b0db5df3f92:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="597ffa476870437293de5b0db5df3f92:3">*other*</span><span data-offset-key="597ffa476870437293de5b0db5df3f92:4">)</span><span data-offset-key="597ffa476870437293de5b0db5df3f92:5">`set ^ other`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="03438663d859483c877526fd4544b2a0"><span data-offset-key="03438663d859483c877526fd4544b2a0:0">Return a new set with elements in either the set or </span><span data-offset-key="03438663d859483c877526fd4544b2a0:1">*other*</span><span data-offset-key="03438663d859483c877526fd4544b2a0:2"> but not both.</span><span data-offset-key="03438663d859483c877526fd4544b2a0:3">`copy`</span><span data-offset-key="03438663d859483c877526fd4544b2a0:4">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b64a580f73a94b53ae1d47b8853cb132"><span data-offset-key="b64a580f73a94b53ae1d47b8853cb132:0">Return a shallow copy of the set.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="75972278879c45b586a2a0f8d28494ca"><span data-offset-key="75972278879c45b586a2a0f8d28494ca:0">Note, the non-operator versions of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#frozenset.union" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="980dc8f26f974886a713f5edfe6d070c"><span data-offset-key="980dc8f26f974886a713f5edfe6d070c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">union()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ae675582dd1b42db954500ddc51179e6"><span data-offset-key="ae675582dd1b42db954500ddc51179e6:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#frozenset.intersection" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="533437da4aae4adbb0a66084fabbd676"><span data-offset-key="533437da4aae4adbb0a66084fabbd676:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">intersection()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a003f6c1fddf4ba4ad7c234e859440a9"><span data-offset-key="a003f6c1fddf4ba4ad7c234e859440a9:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#frozenset.difference" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8f2435bc2d5f4c0f9d6d39e5b1ecd56b"><span data-offset-key="8f2435bc2d5f4c0f9d6d39e5b1ecd56b:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">difference()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="2141df9ddad5421f8d5b72591f322433"><span data-offset-key="2141df9ddad5421f8d5b72591f322433:0">, and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#frozenset.symmetric_difference" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="338a4a85cef24f9893ee1b7f8c93e6ce"><span data-offset-key="338a4a85cef24f9893ee1b7f8c93e6ce:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">symmetric_difference()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="94347a1708e4445eb1a3d353c12b337f"><span data-offset-key="94347a1708e4445eb1a3d353c12b337f:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#frozenset.issubset" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6d1d926f7f504cafa9465438887ba66c"><span data-offset-key="6d1d926f7f504cafa9465438887ba66c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">issubset()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="bc2c2c066f154356a4f8414720ad3478"><span data-offset-key="bc2c2c066f154356a4f8414720ad3478:0">, and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#frozenset.issuperset" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c2a3a1e5bc6846cabd8bc720cecbaa2a"><span data-offset-key="c2a3a1e5bc6846cabd8bc720cecbaa2a:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">issuperset()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ed74ab68633348f09f6ca89b26548a6c"><span data-offset-key="ed74ab68633348f09f6ca89b26548a6c:0"> methods will accept any iterable as an argument. In contrast, their operator based counterparts require their arguments to be sets. This precludes error-prone constructions like </span><span data-offset-key="ed74ab68633348f09f6ca89b26548a6c:1">`set('abc') &                                       'cbs'`</span><span data-offset-key="ed74ab68633348f09f6ca89b26548a6c:2"> in favor of the more readable </span><span data-offset-key="ed74ab68633348f09f6ca89b26548a6c:3">`set('abc').intersection('cbs')`</span><span data-offset-key="ed74ab68633348f09f6ca89b26548a6c:4">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6715c2b373634bbeaf9deb869808adba"><span data-offset-key="6715c2b373634bbeaf9deb869808adba:0">Both </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#set" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8775a04df8c44079ae86f0fc98311d1a"><span data-offset-key="8775a04df8c44079ae86f0fc98311d1a:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">set</code></span></span></a><span data-key="fa158f7f83674a06b3a779e4fbfee6df"><span data-offset-key="fa158f7f83674a06b3a779e4fbfee6df:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#frozenset" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="34e6ce1226c541b99297e5cc8e679530"><span data-offset-key="34e6ce1226c541b99297e5cc8e679530:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">frozenset</code></span></span></a><span data-key="dbdb9df7c5e64b7685a9b93d47862160"><span data-offset-key="dbdb9df7c5e64b7685a9b93d47862160:0"> support set to set comparisons. Two sets are equal if and only if every element of each set is contained in the other (each is a subset of the other). A set is less than another set if and only if the first set is a proper subset of the second set (is a subset, but is not equal). A set is greater than another set if and only if the first set is a proper superset of the second set (is a superset, but is not equal).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="72e8cd495d1e4225a936f25e775eaa76"><span data-offset-key="72e8cd495d1e4225a936f25e775eaa76:0">Instances of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#set" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f044639bd7384724a6e3d193d7e70a97"><span data-offset-key="f044639bd7384724a6e3d193d7e70a97:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">set</code></span></span></a><span data-key="3b40138ac13c42bf8816e7aa13479baa"><span data-offset-key="3b40138ac13c42bf8816e7aa13479baa:0"> are compared to instances of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#frozenset" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2973419eb6524c8bb70c8a065fb2557e"><span data-offset-key="2973419eb6524c8bb70c8a065fb2557e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">frozenset</code></span></span></a><span data-key="b2865ff3afb2403d96229380cce241c5"><span data-offset-key="b2865ff3afb2403d96229380cce241c5:0"> based on their members. For example, </span><span data-offset-key="b2865ff3afb2403d96229380cce241c5:1">`set('abc') ==                                       frozenset('abc')`</span><span data-offset-key="b2865ff3afb2403d96229380cce241c5:2"> returns </span><span data-offset-key="b2865ff3afb2403d96229380cce241c5:3">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="b2865ff3afb2403d96229380cce241c5:4"> and so does </span><span data-offset-key="b2865ff3afb2403d96229380cce241c5:5">`set('abc') in                                       set([frozenset('abc')])`</span><span data-offset-key="b2865ff3afb2403d96229380cce241c5:6">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="72b110af630645959d167a3320f03795"><span data-offset-key="72b110af630645959d167a3320f03795:0">The subset and equality comparisons do not generalize to a total ordering function. For example, any two nonempty disjoint sets are not equal and are not subsets of each other, so </span><span data-offset-key="72b110af630645959d167a3320f03795:1">*all*</span><span data-offset-key="72b110af630645959d167a3320f03795:2"> of the following return </span><span data-offset-key="72b110af630645959d167a3320f03795:3">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="72b110af630645959d167a3320f03795:4">: </span><span data-offset-key="72b110af630645959d167a3320f03795:5">`a<b`</span><span data-offset-key="72b110af630645959d167a3320f03795:6">, </span><span data-offset-key="72b110af630645959d167a3320f03795:7">`a==b`</span><span data-offset-key="72b110af630645959d167a3320f03795:8">, or </span><span data-offset-key="72b110af630645959d167a3320f03795:9">`a>b`</span><span data-offset-key="72b110af630645959d167a3320f03795:10">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7870e44766484bccb4f74d95fe7ba198"><span data-offset-key="7870e44766484bccb4f74d95fe7ba198:0">Since sets only define partial ordering (subset relationships), the output of the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#list.sort" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="709e33e38ca14f6b92ec98113069daf3"><span data-offset-key="709e33e38ca14f6b92ec98113069daf3:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">list.sort()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="35b08a863a3642078a5b984a6b833355"><span data-offset-key="35b08a863a3642078a5b984a6b833355:0"> method is undefined for lists of sets.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5a75a447f4b344d2ad2e60981b011262"><span data-offset-key="5a75a447f4b344d2ad2e60981b011262:0">Set elements, like dictionary keys, must be </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-hashable" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ca7271cd3d374410ba7c11efbeca2640"><span data-offset-key="ca7271cd3d374410ba7c11efbeca2640:0">hashable</span></span></a><span data-key="c896a730bd8c40e0b920b8b57296b423"><span data-offset-key="c896a730bd8c40e0b920b8b57296b423:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="272a4a1e7f1044d3aeb4e7aa6c7de447"><span data-offset-key="272a4a1e7f1044d3aeb4e7aa6c7de447:0">Binary operations that mix </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#set" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="879fe0a873454db29a21f38695e9d75f"><span data-offset-key="879fe0a873454db29a21f38695e9d75f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">set</code></span></span></a><span data-key="5a7c5ce0bf0f4a6988b3219fb7a5c1fa"><span data-offset-key="5a7c5ce0bf0f4a6988b3219fb7a5c1fa:0"> instances with </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#frozenset" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bf53381217c445779e2c14624387406c"><span data-offset-key="bf53381217c445779e2c14624387406c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">frozenset</code></span></span></a><span data-key="3681813381a84c90b82880ffb09a4d14"><span data-offset-key="3681813381a84c90b82880ffb09a4d14:0"> return the type of the first operand. For example: </span><span data-offset-key="3681813381a84c90b82880ffb09a4d14:1">`frozenset('ab') |                                       set('bc')`</span><span data-offset-key="3681813381a84c90b82880ffb09a4d14:2"> returns an instance of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#frozenset" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="51272e0cbd87493b9fc4672ea68ff058"><span data-offset-key="51272e0cbd87493b9fc4672ea68ff058:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">frozenset</code></span></span></a><span data-key="9c2c14c464884e2f93c24446e3def8c9"><span data-offset-key="9c2c14c464884e2f93c24446e3def8c9:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a5e4fa2d2a5e436f836d0d3cc5888918"><span data-offset-key="a5e4fa2d2a5e436f836d0d3cc5888918:0">The following table lists operations available for </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#set" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="80cf7d1f81d44704b9e43e60d997f91a"><span data-offset-key="80cf7d1f81d44704b9e43e60d997f91a:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">set</code></span></span></a><span data-key="5a065ddcd50e4a91ba4c33af24cf25d5"><span data-offset-key="5a065ddcd50e4a91ba4c33af24cf25d5:0"> that do not apply to immutable instances of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#frozenset" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a8c20afd260a43eaa17af76997159c32"><span data-offset-key="a8c20afd260a43eaa17af76997159c32:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">frozenset</code></span></span></a><span data-key="93d4a165fbe64bb699f49115674bea8c"><span data-offset-key="93d4a165fbe64bb699f49115674bea8c:0">:</span><span data-offset-key="93d4a165fbe64bb699f49115674bea8c:1">`update`</span><span data-offset-key="93d4a165fbe64bb699f49115674bea8c:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="93d4a165fbe64bb699f49115674bea8c:3">*\*others*</span><span data-offset-key="93d4a165fbe64bb699f49115674bea8c:4">)</span><span data-offset-key="93d4a165fbe64bb699f49115674bea8c:5">`set |= other | ...`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ca7838df2b0d45b7866059148da6eed4"><span data-offset-key="ca7838df2b0d45b7866059148da6eed4:0">Update the set, adding elements from all others.</span><span data-offset-key="ca7838df2b0d45b7866059148da6eed4:1">`intersection_update`</span><span data-offset-key="ca7838df2b0d45b7866059148da6eed4:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="ca7838df2b0d45b7866059148da6eed4:3">*\*others*</span><span data-offset-key="ca7838df2b0d45b7866059148da6eed4:4">)</span><span data-offset-key="ca7838df2b0d45b7866059148da6eed4:5">`set &= other & ...`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a2dfd6230c8c4c12816833b2a5dd0ecf"><span data-offset-key="a2dfd6230c8c4c12816833b2a5dd0ecf:0">Update the set, keeping only elements found in it and all others.</span><span data-offset-key="a2dfd6230c8c4c12816833b2a5dd0ecf:1">`difference_update`</span><span data-offset-key="a2dfd6230c8c4c12816833b2a5dd0ecf:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="a2dfd6230c8c4c12816833b2a5dd0ecf:3">*\*others*</span><span data-offset-key="a2dfd6230c8c4c12816833b2a5dd0ecf:4">)</span><span data-offset-key="a2dfd6230c8c4c12816833b2a5dd0ecf:5">`set -= other | ...`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="810badf130a4444d888188378e6ed6e8"><span data-offset-key="810badf130a4444d888188378e6ed6e8:0">Update the set, removing elements found in others.</span><span data-offset-key="810badf130a4444d888188378e6ed6e8:1">`symmetric_difference_update`</span><span data-offset-key="810badf130a4444d888188378e6ed6e8:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="810badf130a4444d888188378e6ed6e8:3">*other*</span><span data-offset-key="810badf130a4444d888188378e6ed6e8:4">)</span><span data-offset-key="810badf130a4444d888188378e6ed6e8:5">`set ^= other`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="949e2a6c84c04fab94fedecc9f7fad1e"><span data-offset-key="949e2a6c84c04fab94fedecc9f7fad1e:0">Update the set, keeping only elements found in either set, but not in both.</span><span data-offset-key="949e2a6c84c04fab94fedecc9f7fad1e:1">`add`</span><span data-offset-key="949e2a6c84c04fab94fedecc9f7fad1e:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="949e2a6c84c04fab94fedecc9f7fad1e:3">*elem*</span><span data-offset-key="949e2a6c84c04fab94fedecc9f7fad1e:4">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0db18e6a3d2d4d2585a1a6b4a86fa02a"><span data-offset-key="0db18e6a3d2d4d2585a1a6b4a86fa02a:0">Add element </span><span data-offset-key="0db18e6a3d2d4d2585a1a6b4a86fa02a:1">*elem*</span><span data-offset-key="0db18e6a3d2d4d2585a1a6b4a86fa02a:2"> to the set.</span><span data-offset-key="0db18e6a3d2d4d2585a1a6b4a86fa02a:3">`remove`</span><span data-offset-key="0db18e6a3d2d4d2585a1a6b4a86fa02a:4">(</span><span data-offset-key="0db18e6a3d2d4d2585a1a6b4a86fa02a:5">*elem*</span><span data-offset-key="0db18e6a3d2d4d2585a1a6b4a86fa02a:6">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="84a6137a5e4b49bfbd044f6d09bcf20b"><span data-offset-key="84a6137a5e4b49bfbd044f6d09bcf20b:0">Remove element </span><span data-offset-key="84a6137a5e4b49bfbd044f6d09bcf20b:1">*elem*</span><span data-offset-key="84a6137a5e4b49bfbd044f6d09bcf20b:2"> from the set. Raises </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#KeyError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d58e6b6361c149a5ba2f916d894d4463"><span data-offset-key="d58e6b6361c149a5ba2f916d894d4463:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">KeyError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="4c7ca3d2c5934211804d9a91494223aa"><span data-offset-key="4c7ca3d2c5934211804d9a91494223aa:0"> if </span><span data-offset-key="4c7ca3d2c5934211804d9a91494223aa:1">*elem*</span><span data-offset-key="4c7ca3d2c5934211804d9a91494223aa:2"> is not contained in the set.</span><span data-offset-key="4c7ca3d2c5934211804d9a91494223aa:3">`discard`</span><span data-offset-key="4c7ca3d2c5934211804d9a91494223aa:4">(</span><span data-offset-key="4c7ca3d2c5934211804d9a91494223aa:5">*elem*</span><span data-offset-key="4c7ca3d2c5934211804d9a91494223aa:6">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b679b1279d564e5f8cbccd3e78eb70fb"><span data-offset-key="b679b1279d564e5f8cbccd3e78eb70fb:0">Remove element </span><span data-offset-key="b679b1279d564e5f8cbccd3e78eb70fb:1">*elem*</span><span data-offset-key="b679b1279d564e5f8cbccd3e78eb70fb:2"> from the set if it is present.</span><span data-offset-key="b679b1279d564e5f8cbccd3e78eb70fb:3">`pop`</span><span data-offset-key="b679b1279d564e5f8cbccd3e78eb70fb:4">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fca7215eeb224cd39cc50d9b5119d453"><span data-offset-key="fca7215eeb224cd39cc50d9b5119d453:0">Remove and return an arbitrary element from the set. Raises </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#KeyError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="45c970b3856d4130b65b43900d676175"><span data-offset-key="45c970b3856d4130b65b43900d676175:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">KeyError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="7e95a06f20e54226a9027a7c6079348c"><span data-offset-key="7e95a06f20e54226a9027a7c6079348c:0"> if the set is empty.</span><span data-offset-key="7e95a06f20e54226a9027a7c6079348c:1">`clear`</span><span data-offset-key="7e95a06f20e54226a9027a7c6079348c:2">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="261b7c26988c4cdc819cf07e2073b895"><span data-offset-key="261b7c26988c4cdc819cf07e2073b895:0">Remove all elements from the set.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7b941d325e83467197db84782bbad62a"><span data-offset-key="7b941d325e83467197db84782bbad62a:0">Note, the non-operator versions of the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#frozenset.update" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span accept any iterable as an argument.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e70db995aa834157885033f9f45788e2"><span data-offset-key="e70db995aa834157885033f9f45788e2:0">Note, the </span><span data-offset-key="e70db995aa834157885033f9f45788e2:1">*elem*</span><span data-offset-key="e70db995aa834157885033f9f45788e2:2"> argument to the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__contains__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5ee192c22b4f405daa177f226f360904"><span data-offset-key="5ee192c22b4f405daa177f226f360904:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__contains__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="51f14d3b26e44144b8b838ffe742fe5e"><span data-offset-key="51f14d3b26e44144b8b838ffe742fe5e:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#frozenset.remove" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="67a136ae3c9d4b65bdd02b0a37f3af10"><span data-offset-key="67a136ae3c9d4b65bdd02b0a37f3af10:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">remove()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="17b3b5b68d4c44c2b49677a6a6ffb0bb"><span data-offset-key="17b3b5b68d4c44c2b49677a6a6ffb0bb:0">, and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#frozenset.discard" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="222e385356864f2abc8308dd05efd74f"><span data-offset-key="222e385356864f2abc8308dd05efd74f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">discard()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="6e85396ab79b4e579072a2289d63a849"><span data-offset-key="6e85396ab79b4e579072a2289d63a849:0"> methods may be a set. To support searching for an equivalent frozenset, a temporary one is created from </span><span data-offset-key="6e85396ab79b4e579072a2289d63a849:1">*elem*</span><span data-offset-key="6e85396ab79b4e579072a2289d63a849:2">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH600-23f228db--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3362010cc5d24f5ca23f7aac6f5ed61c"><span data-offset-key="3362010cc5d24f5ca23f7aac6f5ed61c:0">Mapping Types — </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#dict" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c2b62441780d46e580ae397791ec575d"><span data-offset-key="c2b62441780d46e580ae397791ec575d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">dict</code></span></span></a><span data-key="be97b183d9b8405cbfc47718435ee969"><span data-offset-key="be97b183d9b8405cbfc47718435ee969:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="676be165bccb40669260e88802447224"><span data-offset-key="676be165bccb40669260e88802447224:0">A </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-mapping" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="cee99c793bb74ef4a3d2913f29a03f75"><span data-offset-key="cee99c793bb74ef4a3d2913f29a03f75:0">mapping</span></span></a><span data-key="1e7a973f80fd43d89a388bc81b40e810"><span data-offset-key="1e7a973f80fd43d89a388bc81b40e810:0"> object maps </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-hashable" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ce0b492b90234fb09e39fc946347abcf"><span data-offset-key="ce0b492b90234fb09e39fc946347abcf:0">hashable</span></span></a><span data-key="812f022d443846b3a09b7c7d1d114770"><span data-offset-key="812f022d443846b3a09b7c7d1d114770:0"> values to arbitrary objects. Mappings are mutable objects. There is currently only one standard mapping type, the </span><span data-offset-key="812f022d443846b3a09b7c7d1d114770:1">*dictionary*</span><span data-offset-key="812f022d443846b3a09b7c7d1d114770:2">. (For other containers see the built-in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#list" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4d21c1b3cf0242fdb62cfdb06cbcaed9"><span data-offset-key="4d21c1b3cf0242fdb62cfdb06cbcaed9:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">list</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a338497be1344dcda671f38aabdbda2b"><span data-offset-key="a338497be1344dcda671f38aabdbda2b:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#set" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="493e31ec1f1f4fffb211f4ade6b9773f"><span data-offset-key="493e31ec1f1f4fffb211f4ade6b9773f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">set</code></span></span></a><span data-key="175ebfe84532458d96bae68b549f8cac"><span data-offset-key="175ebfe84532458d96bae68b549f8cac:0">, and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#tuple" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b1a4754cf488466c9a31f35dc422be5c"><span data-offset-key="b1a4754cf488466c9a31f35dc422be5c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">tuple</code></span></span></a><span data-key="3a46c71a99d34fc7a0a8302769c8f591"><span data-offset-key="3a46c71a99d34fc7a0a8302769c8f591:0"> classes, and the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/collections.html#module-collections" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0ea64b88cbb24b6eb30853c61be8ac34"><span data-offset-key="0ea64b88cbb24b6eb30853c61be8ac34:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">collections</code></span></span></a><span data-key="b50d85bd840346ba848c987fdde6dc7e"><span data-offset-key="b50d85bd840346ba848c987fdde6dc7e:0"> module.)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="90d43c2dc7204b299f2ac6d12858cf9d"><span data-offset-key="90d43c2dc7204b299f2ac6d12858cf9d:0">A dictionary’s keys are </span><span data-offset-key="90d43c2dc7204b299f2ac6d12858cf9d:1">*almost*</span><span data-offset-key="90d43c2dc7204b299f2ac6d12858cf9d:2"> arbitrary values. Values that are not </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-hashable" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d6af84dc81664b5ebf08d4da7e32108a"><span data-offset-key="d6af84dc81664b5ebf08d4da7e32108a:0">hashable</span></span></a><span data-key="c887ea50805741a693276df8779a6dcc"><span data-offset-key="c887ea50805741a693276df8779a6dcc:0">, that is, values containing lists, dictionaries or other mutable types (that are compared by value rather than by object identity) may not be used as keys. Numeric types used for keys obey the normal rules for numeric comparison: if two numbers compare equal (such as </span><span data-offset-key="c887ea50805741a693276df8779a6dcc:1">`1`</span><span data-offset-key="c887ea50805741a693276df8779a6dcc:2"> and </span><span data-offset-key="c887ea50805741a693276df8779a6dcc:3">`1.0`</span><span data-offset-key="c887ea50805741a693276df8779a6dcc:4">) then they can be used interchangeably to index the same dictionary entry. (Note however, that since computers store floating-point numbers as approximations it is usually unwise to use them as dictionary keys.)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="644be539a14c48aa92eddf1bbde2effb"><span data-offset-key="644be539a14c48aa92eddf1bbde2effb:0">Dictionaries can be created by placing a comma-separated list of </span><span data-offset-key="644be539a14c48aa92eddf1bbde2effb:1">`key: value`</span><span data-offset-key="644be539a14c48aa92eddf1bbde2effb:2"> pairs within braces, for example: </span><span data-offset-key="644be539a14c48aa92eddf1bbde2effb:3">`{'jack': 4098,                                       'sjoerd': 4127}`</span><span data-offset-key="644be539a14c48aa92eddf1bbde2effb:4"> or </span><span data-offset-key="644be539a14c48aa92eddf1bbde2effb:5">`{4098: 'jack', 4127:                                       'sjoerd'}`</span><span data-offset-key="644be539a14c48aa92eddf1bbde2effb:6">, or by the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#dict" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="59221f64ad014bb68ec5fcffc8de5493"><span data-offset-key="59221f64ad014bb68ec5fcffc8de5493:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">dict</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f18517cc2bd248ff991ef066ae413350"><span data-offset-key="f18517cc2bd248ff991ef066ae413350:0"> constructor.</span><span data-offset-key="f18517cc2bd248ff991ef066ae413350:1">*class* </span><span data-offset-key="f18517cc2bd248ff991ef066ae413350:2">`dict`</span><span data-offset-key="f18517cc2bd248ff991ef066ae413350:3">(</span><span data-offset-key="f18517cc2bd248ff991ef066ae413350:4">*\*\*kwarg*</span><span data-offset-key="f18517cc2bd248ff991ef066ae413350:5">)</span><span data-offset-key="f18517cc2bd248ff991ef066ae413350:6">*class* </span><span data-offset-key="f18517cc2bd248ff991ef066ae413350:7">`dict`</span><span data-offset-key="f18517cc2bd248ff991ef066ae413350:8">(</span><span data-offset-key="f18517cc2bd248ff991ef066ae413350:9">*mapping*</span><span data-offset-key="f18517cc2bd248ff991ef066ae413350:10">, </span><span data-offset-key="f18517cc2bd248ff991ef066ae413350:11">*\*\*kwarg*</span><span data-offset-key="f18517cc2bd248ff991ef066ae413350:12">)</span><span data-offset-key="f18517cc2bd248ff991ef066ae413350:13">*class* </span><span data-offset-key="f18517cc2bd248ff991ef066ae413350:14">`dict`</span><span data-offset-key="f18517cc2bd248ff991ef066ae413350:15">(</span><span data-offset-key="f18517cc2bd248ff991ef066ae413350:16">*iterable*</span><span data-offset-key="f18517cc2bd248ff991ef066ae413350:17">, </span><span data-offset-key="f18517cc2bd248ff991ef066ae413350:18">*\*\*kwarg*</span><span data-offset-key="f18517cc2bd248ff991ef066ae413350:19">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="eaf803e763e940f980e24709764c693b"><span data-offset-key="eaf803e763e940f980e24709764c693b:0">Return a new dictionary initialized from an optional positional argument and a possibly empty set of keyword arguments.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ffcb7562ec4743eb99878a4df0fd4630"><span data-offset-key="ffcb7562ec4743eb99878a4df0fd4630:0">Dictionaries can be created by several means:</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f66817bf37e843d68294771ebb32fd50"><span data-offset-key="f66817bf37e843d68294771ebb32fd50:0">Use a comma-separated list of </span><span data-offset-key="f66817bf37e843d68294771ebb32fd50:1">`key: value`</span><span data-offset-key="f66817bf37e843d68294771ebb32fd50:2"> pairs within braces: </span><span data-offset-key="f66817bf37e843d68294771ebb32fd50:3">`{'jack': 4098,                                             'sjoerd': 4127}`</span><span data-offset-key="f66817bf37e843d68294771ebb32fd50:4"> or </span><span data-offset-key="f66817bf37e843d68294771ebb32fd50:5">`{4098: 'jack', 4127:                                             'sjoerd'}`</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="35b66c31bb31434e87e844fe5faef956"><span data-offset-key="35b66c31bb31434e87e844fe5faef956:0">Use a dict comprehension: </span><span data-offset-key="35b66c31bb31434e87e844fe5faef956:1">`{}`</span><span data-offset-key="35b66c31bb31434e87e844fe5faef956:2">, </span><span data-offset-key="35b66c31bb31434e87e844fe5faef956:3">`{x: x ** 2 for x in                                             range(10)}`</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ce92633ba75a465680ca9138c307b986"><span data-offset-key="ce92633ba75a465680ca9138c307b986:0">Use the type constructor: </span><span data-offset-key="ce92633ba75a465680ca9138c307b986:1">`dict()`</span><span data-offset-key="ce92633ba75a465680ca9138c307b986:2">, </span><span data-offset-key="ce92633ba75a465680ca9138c307b986:3">`dict([('foo', 100),                                             ('bar', 200)])`</span><span data-offset-key="ce92633ba75a465680ca9138c307b986:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="ce92633ba75a465680ca9138c307b986:5">`dict(foo=100, bar=200)`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="93010dde3e764528b81cfa5fde8d6548"><span data-offset-key="93010dde3e764528b81cfa5fde8d6548:0">If no positional argument is given, an empty dictionary is created. If a positional argument is given and it is a mapping object, a dictionary is created with the same key-value pairs as the mapping object. Otherwise, the positional argument must be an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-iterable" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7c3d30bd7f2644dc9958b0cdd5c5d9ed"><span data-offset-key="7c3d30bd7f2644dc9958b0cdd5c5d9ed:0">iterable</span></span></a><span data-key="c6cbfb404b4d49b0aadfad684b31e904"><span data-offset-key="c6cbfb404b4d49b0aadfad684b31e904:0"> object. Each item in the iterable must itself be an iterable with exactly two objects. The first object of each item becomes a key in the new dictionary, and the second object the corresponding value. If a key occurs more than once, the last value for that key becomes the corresponding value in the new dictionary.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ccc4d591cc7049e0b8609dbe4f5d0c38"><span data-offset-key="ccc4d591cc7049e0b8609dbe4f5d0c38:0">If keyword arguments are given, the keyword arguments and their values are added to the dictionary created from the positional argument. If a key being added is already present, the value from the keyword argument replaces the value from the positional argument.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1b1af67f0e5948efaf1d771c609de705"><span data-offset-key="1b1af67f0e5948efaf1d771c609de705:0">To illustrate, the following examples all return a dictionary equal to </span><span data-offset-key="1b1af67f0e5948efaf1d771c609de705:1">`{"one": 1, "two": 2,                                       "three": 3}`</span><span data-offset-key="1b1af67f0e5948efaf1d771c609de705:2">:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> a = dict(one=1, two=2, three=3)>>> b = {'one': 1, 'two': 2, 'three': 3}>>> c = dict(zip(['one', 'two', 'three'], [1, 2, 3]))>>> d = dict([('two', 2), ('one', 1), ('three', 3)])>>> e = dict({'three': 3, 'one': 1, 'two': 2})>>> f = dict({'one': 1, 'three': 3}, two=2)>>> a == b == c == d == e == fTrue

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="29222a7bd8eb4e4ab1868905b0e16f09"><span data-offset-key="29222a7bd8eb4e4ab1868905b0e16f09:0">Providing keyword arguments as in the first example only works for keys that are valid Python identifiers. Otherwise, any valid keys can be used.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6ff8828d257b4c50bdc6ab7e9ca6dfa7"><span data-offset-key="6ff8828d257b4c50bdc6ab7e9ca6dfa7:0">These are the operations that dictionaries support (and therefore, custom mapping types should support too):</span><span data-offset-key="6ff8828d257b4c50bdc6ab7e9ca6dfa7:1">`list(d)`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="73ce6a78791e46c784163c17893d225b"><span data-offset-key="73ce6a78791e46c784163c17893d225b:0">Return a list of all the keys used in the dictionary </span><span data-offset-key="73ce6a78791e46c784163c17893d225b:1">*d*</span><span data-offset-key="73ce6a78791e46c784163c17893d225b:2">.</span><span data-offset-key="73ce6a78791e46c784163c17893d225b:3">`len(d)`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="42a2be3d071c4cd491c32fa56e326fa0"><span data-offset-key="42a2be3d071c4cd491c32fa56e326fa0:0">Return the number of items in the dictionary </span><span data-offset-key="42a2be3d071c4cd491c32fa56e326fa0:1">*d*</span><span data-offset-key="42a2be3d071c4cd491c32fa56e326fa0:2">.</span><span data-offset-key="42a2be3d071c4cd491c32fa56e326fa0:3">`d[key]`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8819610de9f64310b7797446e9f13a11"><span data-offset-key="8819610de9f64310b7797446e9f13a11:0">Return the item of </span><span data-offset-key="8819610de9f64310b7797446e9f13a11:1">*d*</span><span data-offset-key="8819610de9f64310b7797446e9f13a11:2"> with key </span><span data-offset-key="8819610de9f64310b7797446e9f13a11:3">*key*</span><span data-offset-key="8819610de9f64310b7797446e9f13a11:4">. Raises a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#KeyError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e9b9e2ba73604f2093d0f48539b6c9d7"><span data-offset-key="e9b9e2ba73604f2093d0f48539b6c9d7:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">KeyError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a9277bfb00214c3d98e149ef949460cb"><span data-offset-key="a9277bfb00214c3d98e149ef949460cb:0"> if </span><span data-offset-key="a9277bfb00214c3d98e149ef949460cb:1">*key*</span><span data-offset-key="a9277bfb00214c3d98e149ef949460cb:2"> is not in the map.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="dd02d3e916c740a6aa795f0537182ce2"><span data-offset-key="dd02d3e916c740a6aa795f0537182ce2:0">If a subclass of dict defines a method </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__missing__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="dbbe9908cd5a480d91dd11f45e859ed2"><span data-offset-key="dbbe9908cd5a480d91dd11f45e859ed2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__missing__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ca6e9684815d4e7991d7df517c2dc1c3"><span data-offset-key="ca6e9684815d4e7991d7df517c2dc1c3:0"> and </span><span data-offset-key="ca6e9684815d4e7991d7df517c2dc1c3:1">*key*</span><span data-offset-key="ca6e9684815d4e7991d7df517c2dc1c3:2"> is not present, the </span><span data-offset-key="ca6e9684815d4e7991d7df517c2dc1c3:3">`d[key]`</span><span data-offset-key="ca6e9684815d4e7991d7df517c2dc1c3:4"> operation calls that method with the key </span><span data-offset-key="ca6e9684815d4e7991d7df517c2dc1c3:5">*key*</span><span data-offset-key="ca6e9684815d4e7991d7df517c2dc1c3:6"> as argument. The </span><span data-offset-key="ca6e9684815d4e7991d7df517c2dc1c3:7">`d[key]`</span><span data-offset-key="ca6e9684815d4e7991d7df517c2dc1c3:8"> operation then returns or raises whatever is returned or raised by the </span><span data-offset-key="ca6e9684815d4e7991d7df517c2dc1c3:9">`__missing__(key)`</span><span data-offset-key="ca6e9684815d4e7991d7df517c2dc1c3:10"> call. No other operations or methods invoke </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__missing__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="405b44844d014423aca127bebae0d64e"><span data-offset-key="405b44844d014423aca127bebae0d64e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__missing__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="2419821fa9224e5ea0537587de45dfd9"><span data-offset-key="2419821fa9224e5ea0537587de45dfd9:0">. If </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__missing__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ffb4517503dc4342827f4dfacaafd59a"><span data-offset-key="ffb4517503dc4342827f4dfacaafd59a:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__missing__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="fada76f46f9c4c25b33854ade4e6116d"><span data-offset-key="fada76f46f9c4c25b33854ade4e6116d:0"> is not defined, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#KeyError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8db793f055ae46339128d078fefd59e3"><span data-offset-key="8db793f055ae46339128d078fefd59e3:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">KeyError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="feee973e353b40b8bf4d73d1c0496327"><span data-offset-key="feee973e353b40b8bf4d73d1c0496327:0"> is raised. </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__missing__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9a16d91653f34628856d5437d40020e9"><span data-offset-key="9a16d91653f34628856d5437d40020e9:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__missing__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="5515c51efce6494ba9ed05fe147a2f69"><span data-offset-key="5515c51efce6494ba9ed05fe147a2f69:0"> must be a method; it cannot be an instance variable:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> class Counter(dict):...     def __missing__(self, key):...         return 0>>> c = Counter()>>> c['red']0>>> c['red'] += 1>>> c['red']1

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="767e88081b364a8ea5c12ece77e5fc28"><span data-offset-key="767e88081b364a8ea5c12ece77e5fc28:0">The example above shows part of the implementation of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/collections.html#collections.Counter" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="11c74ca724c34a929d0395a116b58aa8"><span data-offset-key="11c74ca724c34a929d0395a116b58aa8:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">collections.Counter</code></span></span></a><span data-key="962ddbd4153f4f5890b8240645edb2df"><span data-offset-key="962ddbd4153f4f5890b8240645edb2df:0">. A different </span><span data-offset-key="962ddbd4153f4f5890b8240645edb2df:1">`__missing__`</span><span data-offset-key="962ddbd4153f4f5890b8240645edb2df:2"> method is used by </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/collections.html#collections.defaultdict" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5090cf72aada4021aacd5bb866b9673f"><span data-offset-key="5090cf72aada4021aacd5bb866b9673f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">collections.defaultdict</code></span></span></a><span data-key="7cf2f846438b46be87321660c699d371"><span data-offset-key="7cf2f846438b46be87321660c699d371:0">.</span><span data-offset-key="7cf2f846438b46be87321660c699d371:1">`d[key] = value`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="15d3f823f0f04743a7ea9d8645106668"><span data-offset-key="15d3f823f0f04743a7ea9d8645106668:0">Set </span><span data-offset-key="15d3f823f0f04743a7ea9d8645106668:1">`d[key]`</span><span data-offset-key="15d3f823f0f04743a7ea9d8645106668:2"> to </span><span data-offset-key="15d3f823f0f04743a7ea9d8645106668:3">*value*</span><span data-offset-key="15d3f823f0f04743a7ea9d8645106668:4">.</span><span data-offset-key="15d3f823f0f04743a7ea9d8645106668:5">`del d[key]`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e77ad44352634ea4bde3b9b5f9f17647"><span data-offset-key="e77ad44352634ea4bde3b9b5f9f17647:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#dict.popitem" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="128db7e60ade4c64b23deb85247c48c7"><span data-offset-key="128db7e60ade4c64b23deb85247c48c7:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">popitem()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ea073da200f846058f72905d5f99ccbe"><span data-offset-key="ea073da200f846058f72905d5f99ccbe:0"> is useful to destructively iterate over a dictionary, as often used in set algorithms. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5d5a8adebfda4b6fab5d2ff69d790af0"><span data-offset-key="5d5a8adebfda4b6fab5d2ff69d790af0:0">Changed in version 3.7: LIFO order is now guaranteed. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="64d0f222d33c466bb0e19693b3c9f1c9"><span data-offset-key="64d0f222d33c466bb0e19693b3c9f1c9:0">Return a reverse iterator over the keys of the dictionary. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fed29ac9c7914c6dbee0705154a4913f"><span data-offset-key="fed29ac9c7914c6dbee0705154a4913f:0">New in version 3.8.</span><span data-offset-key="fed29ac9c7914c6dbee0705154a4913f:1">`setdefault`</span><span data-offset-key="fed29ac9c7914c6dbee0705154a4913f:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="fed29ac9c7914c6dbee0705154a4913f:3">*key*</span><span data-offset-key="fed29ac9c7914c6dbee0705154a4913f:4">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="fed29ac9c7914c6dbee0705154a4913f:5">*default*</span><span data-offset-key="fed29ac9c7914c6dbee0705154a4913f:6">\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9b1ba88abc2f4976832ba214983dc958"><span data-offset-key="9b1ba88abc2f4976832ba214983dc958:0">If </span><span data-offset-key="9b1ba88abc2f4976832ba214983dc958:1">*key*</span><span data-offset-key="9b1ba88abc2f4976832ba214983dc958:2"> is in the dictionary, return its value. If not, insert </span><span data-offset-key="9b1ba88abc2f4976832ba214983dc958:3">*key*</span><span data-offset-key="9b1ba88abc2f4976832ba214983dc958:4"> with a value of </span><span data-offset-key="9b1ba88abc2f4976832ba214983dc958:5">*default*</span><span data-offset-key="9b1ba88abc2f4976832ba214983dc958:6"> and return </span><span data-offset-key="9b1ba88abc2f4976832ba214983dc958:7">*default*</span><span data-offset-key="9b1ba88abc2f4976832ba214983dc958:8">. </span><span data-offset-key="9b1ba88abc2f4976832ba214983dc958:9">*default*</span><span data-offset-key="9b1ba88abc2f4976832ba214983dc958:10"> defaults to </span><span data-offset-key="9b1ba88abc2f4976832ba214983dc958:11">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="9b1ba88abc2f4976832ba214983dc958:12">.</span><span data-offset-key="9b1ba88abc2f4976832ba214983dc958:13">`update`</span><span data-offset-key="9b1ba88abc2f4976832ba214983dc958:14">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="9b1ba88abc2f4976832ba214983dc958:15">*other*</span><span data-offset-key="9b1ba88abc2f4976832ba214983dc958:16">\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d4dd1e71b740449e96053077dda2d9fe"><span data-offset-key="d4dd1e71b740449e96053077dda2d9fe:0">Update the dictionary with the key/value pairs from </span><span data-offset-key="d4dd1e71b740449e96053077dda2d9fe:1">*other*</span><span data-offset-key="d4dd1e71b740449e96053077dda2d9fe:2">, overwriting existing keys. Return </span><span data-offset-key="d4dd1e71b740449e96053077dda2d9fe:3">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="d4dd1e71b740449e96053077dda2d9fe:4">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f55259483c614083a9317d83ea1d5cbc"><span data-offset-key="f55259483c614083a9317d83ea1d5cbc:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#dict.update" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="73eafc4b37274ae39cd4ffa9951200ae"><span data-offset-key="73eafc4b37274ae39cd4ffa9951200ae:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">update()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="257b92f2fa114169bb6bac4bd285b7eb"><span data-offset-key="257b92f2fa114169bb6bac4bd285b7eb:0"> accepts either another dictionary object or an iterable of key/value pairs (as tuples or other iterables of length two). If keyword arguments are specified, the dictionary is then updated with those key/value pairs: </span><span data-offset-key="257b92f2fa114169bb6bac4bd285b7eb:1">`d.update(red=1, blue=2)`</span><span data-offset-key="257b92f2fa114169bb6bac4bd285b7eb:2">.</span><span data-offset-key="257b92f2fa114169bb6bac4bd285b7eb:3">`values`</span><span data-offset-key="257b92f2fa114169bb6bac4bd285b7eb:4">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="12e0221c494a41d1a4a7e655fbbc7bdb"><span data-offset-key="12e0221c494a41d1a4a7e655fbbc7bdb:0">Return a new view of the dictionary’s values. See the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#dict-views" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="066ca118a3f24a59b808ffdeaecaa50a"><span data-offset-key="066ca118a3f24a59b808ffdeaecaa50a:0">documentation of view objects</span></span></a><span data-key="6dc0adf04df845d9a1614491002d987a"><span data-offset-key="6dc0adf04df845d9a1614491002d987a:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2ccda976cce44838bbda6005129b7218"><span data-offset-key="2ccda976cce44838bbda6005129b7218:0">An equality comparison between one </span><span data-offset-key="2ccda976cce44838bbda6005129b7218:1">`dict.values()`</span><span data-offset-key="2ccda976cce44838bbda6005129b7218:2"> view and another will always return </span><span data-offset-key="2ccda976cce44838bbda6005129b7218:3">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="2ccda976cce44838bbda6005129b7218:4">.
