    >>> d = {'a': 1}>>> d.values() == d.values()False

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9f45bc4a24c94ef7a560cea6e4c05580"><span data-offset-key="9f45bc4a24c94ef7a560cea6e4c05580:0">`d | other`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f30ec52f670b4266b6f803336862bb7d"><span data-offset-key="f30ec52f670b4266b6f803336862bb7d:0">Create a new dictionary with the merged keys and values of </span><span data-offset-key="f30ec52f670b4266b6f803336862bb7d:1">*d*</span><span data-offset-key="f30ec52f670b4266b6f803336862bb7d:2"> and </span><span data-offset-key="f30ec52f670b4266b6f803336862bb7d:3">*other*</span><span data-offset-key="f30ec52f670b4266b6f803336862bb7d:4">, which must both be dictionaries. The values of </span><span data-offset-key="f30ec52f670b4266b6f803336862bb7d:5">*other*</span><span data-offset-key="f30ec52f670b4266b6f803336862bb7d:6"> take priority when </span><span data-offset-key="f30ec52f670b4266b6f803336862bb7d:7">*d*</span><span data-offset-key="f30ec52f670b4266b6f803336862bb7d:8"> and </span><span data-offset-key="f30ec52f670b4266b6f803336862bb7d:9">*other*</span><span data-offset-key="f30ec52f670b4266b6f803336862bb7d:10"> share keys.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b25f558d3c504ca8a524a843cbcb10e0"><span data-offset-key="b25f558d3c504ca8a524a843cbcb10e0:0">New in version 3.9.</span><span data-offset-key="b25f558d3c504ca8a524a843cbcb10e0:1">`d |= other`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a66b0157fe594fbcb570745c910f3c3a"><span data-offset-key="a66b0157fe594fbcb570745c910f3c3a:0">Update the dictionary </span><span data-offset-key="a66b0157fe594fbcb570745c910f3c3a:1">*d*</span><span data-offset-key="a66b0157fe594fbcb570745c910f3c3a:2"> with keys and values from </span><span data-offset-key="a66b0157fe594fbcb570745c910f3c3a:3">*other*</span><span data-offset-key="a66b0157fe594fbcb570745c910f3c3a:4">, which may be either a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-mapping" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="277f1bb5bd0b4ec59e1df52a688389d8"><span data-offset-key="277f1bb5bd0b4ec59e1df52a688389d8:0">mapping</span></span></a><span data-key="f5f22d0b276c4a8ba2c30310f07811dd"><span data-offset-key="f5f22d0b276c4a8ba2c30310f07811dd:0"> or an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-iterable" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9292ee2887a74d9fa9ebae0c671dc9e6"><span data-offset-key="9292ee2887a74d9fa9ebae0c671dc9e6:0">iterable</span></span></a><span data-key="f1acfe6667ba418396099c973f975355"><span data-offset-key="f1acfe6667ba418396099c973f975355:0"> of key/value pairs. The values of </span><span data-offset-key="f1acfe6667ba418396099c973f975355:1">*other*</span><span data-offset-key="f1acfe6667ba418396099c973f975355:2"> take priority when </span><span data-offset-key="f1acfe6667ba418396099c973f975355:3">*d*</span><span data-offset-key="f1acfe6667ba418396099c973f975355:4"> and </span><span data-offset-key="f1acfe6667ba418396099c973f975355:5">*other*</span><span data-offset-key="f1acfe6667ba418396099c973f975355:6"> share keys.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="89ec98d7a9814c2bbbec3c356e4b3ad4"><span data-offset-key="89ec98d7a9814c2bbbec3c356e4b3ad4:0">New in version 3.9.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="954e7d44ffd545bc85baf698b6551353"><span data-offset-key="954e7d44ffd545bc85baf698b6551353:0">Dictionaries compare equal if and only if they have the same </span><span data-offset-key="954e7d44ffd545bc85baf698b6551353:1">`(key, value)`</span><span data-offset-key="954e7d44ffd545bc85baf698b6551353:2"> pairs (regardless of ordering). Order comparisons (‘&lt;’, ‘&lt;=’, ‘&gt;=’, ‘&gt;’) raise </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#TypeError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="00cc65e67bae46658adaeee95e41ec09"><span data-offset-key="00cc65e67bae46658adaeee95e41ec09:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">TypeError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="b4f32b66c4db400580f81ca3262bbc3a"><span data-offset-key="b4f32b66c4db400580f81ca3262bbc3a:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ba1da465c7cc4c0183a608f7ff7be288"><span data-offset-key="ba1da465c7cc4c0183a608f7ff7be288:0">Dictionaries preserve insertion order. Note that updating a key does not affect the order. Keys added after deletion are inserted at the end.&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> d = {"one": 1, "two": 2, "three": 3, "four": 4}>>> d{'one': 1, 'two': 2, 'three': 3, 'four': 4}>>> list(d)['one', 'two', 'three', 'four']>>> list(d.values())[1, 2, 3, 4]>>> d["one"] = 42>>> d{'one': 42, 'two': 2, 'three': 3, 'four': 4}>>> del d["two"]>>> d["two"] = None>>> d{'one': 42, 'three': 3, 'four': 4, 'two': None}

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a6891c5da77348b1ae58ecba6d28b2d6"><span data-offset-key="a6891c5da77348b1ae58ecba6d28b2d6:0">Changed in version 3.7: Dictionary order is guaranteed to be insertion order. This behavior was an implementation detail of CPython from 3.6.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="abbc44aa810c45439ad15ffa1da7dbaf"><span data-offset-key="abbc44aa810c45439ad15ffa1da7dbaf:0">Dictionaries and dictionary views are reversible.&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> d = {"one": 1, "two": 2, "three": 3, "four": 4}>>> d{'one': 1, 'two': 2, 'three': 3, 'four': 4}>>> list(reversed(d))['four', 'three', 'two', 'one']>>> list(reversed(d.values()))[4, 3, 2, 1]>>> list(reversed(d.items()))[('four', 4), ('three', 3), ('two', 2), ('one', 1)]

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6aac14a0be134669a250535663d7de71"><span data-offset-key="6aac14a0be134669a250535663d7de71:0">Changed in version 3.8: Dictionaries are now reversible.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="152d29dcfa5f47f7bb8d011da240c7ab"><span data-offset-key="152d29dcfa5f47f7bb8d011da240c7ab:0">See also </span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="754fc72c87d249d2b4bdac57dd5bb8a9"><span data-offset-key="754fc72c87d249d2b4bdac57dd5bb8a9:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/types.html#types.MappingProxyType" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="36199573a2a44da1bb455cb7bc332cde"><span data-offset-key="36199573a2a44da1bb455cb7bc332cde:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">types.MappingProxyType</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d1a3ad4ceeba43febcf9d3e6c953c119"><span data-offset-key="d1a3ad4ceeba43febcf9d3e6c953c119:0"> can be used to create a read-only view of a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#dict" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0f3497bc432f45d1b9900c3c4e756512"><span data-offset-key="0f3497bc432f45d1b9900c3c4e756512:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">dict</code></span></span></a><span data-key="6af52502a1dd4e26b63b4b2c34c0268f"><span data-offset-key="6af52502a1dd4e26b63b4b2c34c0268f:0">.</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="869ec46e007740b29103669d3a7a6dcd"><span data-offset-key="869ec46e007740b29103669d3a7a6dcd:0">Dictionary view objects</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8d436e96789f478a9ab575ebc7516ae8"><span data-offset-key="8d436e96789f478a9ab575ebc7516ae8:0">The objects returned by </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#dict.keys" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c7ada039e7d04e8088d61423c751d6ce"><span data-offset-key="c7ada039e7d04e8088d61423c751d6ce:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">dict.keys()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f0bd2d66ad674905a7dac2f6bdd798f7"><span data-offset-key="f0bd2d66ad674905a7dac2f6bdd798f7:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#dict.values" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="40e72f64f1904a0ab2fd41d478436342"><span data-offset-key="40e72f64f1904a0ab2fd41d478436342:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">dict.values()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="e06d64de439c464ca9d832168404ea86"><span data-offset-key="e06d64de439c464ca9d832168404ea86:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#dict.items" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2d8f3ca0adc34a279d8b454b952df53a"><span data-offset-key="2d8f3ca0adc34a279d8b454b952df53a:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">dict.items()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a153058578be4728b6b5cc7d1e797cd9"><span data-offset-key="a153058578be4728b6b5cc7d1e797cd9:0"> are </span><span data-offset-key="a153058578be4728b6b5cc7d1e797cd9:1">*view objects*</span><span data-offset-key="a153058578be4728b6b5cc7d1e797cd9:2">. They provide a dynamic view on the dictionary’s entries, which means that when the dictionary changes, the view reflects these changes.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e934673c2e20481fbe9764c48965675e"><span data-offset-key="e934673c2e20481fbe9764c48965675e:0">Dictionary views can be iterated over to yield their respective data, and support membership tests:</span><span data-offset-key="e934673c2e20481fbe9764c48965675e:1">`len(dictview)`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e623a6784eff4f3283938a4a100d6f41"><span data-offset-key="e623a6784eff4f3283938a4a100d6f41:0">Return the number of entries in the dictionary.</span><span data-offset-key="e623a6784eff4f3283938a4a100d6f41:1">`iter(dictview)`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e04cbd6b9c14443d94a83bc957ce6918"><span data-offset-key="e04cbd6b9c14443d94a83bc957ce6918:0">Return an iterator over the keys, values or items (represented as tuples of </span><span data-offset-key="e04cbd6b9c14443d94a83bc957ce6918:1">`(key, value)`</span><span data-offset-key="e04cbd6b9c14443d94a83bc957ce6918:2">) in the dictionary.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c5d923a3c9f549b79dc85a7473938806"><span data-offset-key="c5d923a3c9f549b79dc85a7473938806:0">Keys and values are iterated over in insertion order. This allows the creation of </span><span data-offset-key="c5d923a3c9f549b79dc85a7473938806:1">`(value, key)`</span><span data-offset-key="c5d923a3c9f549b79dc85a7473938806:2"> pairs using </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#zip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a4fcdb0f356646c4b8defe007f0b89db"><span data-offset-key="a4fcdb0f356646c4b8defe007f0b89db:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">zip()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="eb3e4a4c56d94871aa08325a18b4b337"><span data-offset-key="eb3e4a4c56d94871aa08325a18b4b337:0">: </span><span data-offset-key="eb3e4a4c56d94871aa08325a18b4b337:1">`pairs = zip(d.values(), d.keys())`</span><span data-offset-key="eb3e4a4c56d94871aa08325a18b4b337:2">. Another way to create the same list is </span><span data-offset-key="eb3e4a4c56d94871aa08325a18b4b337:3">`pairs = [(v, k) for (k, v) in                                       d.items()]`</span><span data-offset-key="eb3e4a4c56d94871aa08325a18b4b337:4">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d20e701cf4c44a9a955783db16504d5b"><span data-offset-key="d20e701cf4c44a9a955783db16504d5b:0">Iterating views while adding or deleting entries in the dictionary may raise a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#RuntimeError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b890cc4a56b4427798cffcea8b75fa9a"><span data-offset-key="b890cc4a56b4427798cffcea8b75fa9a:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">RuntimeError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="8dc53d336d314eec9b2d27fc3319ebc9"><span data-offset-key="8dc53d336d314eec9b2d27fc3319ebc9:0"> or fail to iterate over all entries.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a0d94dc9faf84b22b6f8a71d2ce8d11d"><span data-offset-key="a0d94dc9faf84b22b6f8a71d2ce8d11d:0">Changed in version 3.7: Dictionary order is guaranteed to be insertion order.</span><span data-offset-key="a0d94dc9faf84b22b6f8a71d2ce8d11d:1">`x in dictview`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e32c48a7186148328b3670b79974d57a"><span data-offset-key="e32c48a7186148328b3670b79974d57a:0">Return </span><span data-offset-key="e32c48a7186148328b3670b79974d57a:1">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="e32c48a7186148328b3670b79974d57a:2"> if </span><span data-offset-key="e32c48a7186148328b3670b79974d57a:3">*x*</span><span data-offset-key="e32c48a7186148328b3670b79974d57a:4"> is in the underlying dictionary’s keys, values or items (in the latter case, </span><span data-offset-key="e32c48a7186148328b3670b79974d57a:5">*x*</span><span data-offset-key="e32c48a7186148328b3670b79974d57a:6"> should be a </span><span data-offset-key="e32c48a7186148328b3670b79974d57a:7">`(key, value)`</span><span data-offset-key="e32c48a7186148328b3670b79974d57a:8"> tuple).</span><span data-offset-key="e32c48a7186148328b3670b79974d57a:9">`reversed(dictview)`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9a2f7f90bfd740c1afa66afb3792d22a"><span data-offset-key="9a2f7f90bfd740c1afa66afb3792d22a:0">Return a reverse iterator over the keys, values or items of the dictionary. The view will be iterated in reverse order of the insertion.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b9742552fe564aa6ad8d9b149b368bc2"><span data-offset-key="b9742552fe564aa6ad8d9b149b368bc2:0">Changed in version 3.8: Dictionary views are now reversible.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="bd8b78660dfa4e9c9924080df3288d02"><span data-offset-key="bd8b78660dfa4e9c9924080df3288d02:0">Keys views are set-like since their entries are unique and hashable. If all values are hashable, so that </span><span data-offset-key="bd8b78660dfa4e9c9924080df3288d02:1">`(key, value)`</span><span data-offset-key="bd8b78660dfa4e9c9924080df3288d02:2"> pairs are unique and hashable, then the items view is also set-like. (Values views are not treated as set-like since the entries are generally not unique.) For set-like views, all of the operations defined for the abstract base class </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/collections.abc.html#collections.abc.Set" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f08f5c4afcb64ca58eac0baad8bc05bd"><span data-offset-key="f08f5c4afcb64ca58eac0baad8bc05bd:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">collections.abc.Set</code></span></span></a><span data-key="676fb8d98fa946708a785da153d480af"><span data-offset-key="676fb8d98fa946708a785da153d480af:0"> are available (for example, </span><span data-offset-key="676fb8d98fa946708a785da153d480af:1">`==`</span><span data-offset-key="676fb8d98fa946708a785da153d480af:2">, </span><span data-offset-key="676fb8d98fa946708a785da153d480af:3">`<`</span><span data-offset-key="676fb8d98fa946708a785da153d480af:4">, or </span><span data-offset-key="676fb8d98fa946708a785da153d480af:5">`^`</span><span data-offset-key="676fb8d98fa946708a785da153d480af:6">).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="bf338cd7a9d84b95b3a38b74af083b5e"><span data-offset-key="bf338cd7a9d84b95b3a38b74af083b5e:0">An example of dictionary view usage:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> dishes = {'eggs': 2, 'sausage': 1, 'bacon': 1, 'spam': 500}>>> keys = dishes.keys()>>> values = dishes.values()​>>> # iteration>>> n = 0>>> for val in values:...     n += val>>> print(n)504​>>> # keys and values are iterated over in the same order (insertion order)>>> list(keys)['eggs', 'sausage', 'bacon', 'spam']>>> list(values)[2, 1, 1, 500]​>>> # view objects are dynamic and reflect dict changes>>> del dishes['eggs']>>> del dishes['sausage']>>> list(keys)['bacon', 'spam']​>>> # set operations>>> keys & {'eggs', 'bacon', 'salad'}{'bacon'}>>> keys ^ {'sausage', 'juice'}{'juice', 'sausage', 'bacon', 'spam'}

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH600-23f228db--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="31bff80c152046ecb0e2d0e8063d329c"><span data-offset-key="31bff80c152046ecb0e2d0e8063d329c:0">Context Manager Types</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="39d5260f087745d0ba12bd161f713a88"><span data-offset-key="39d5260f087745d0ba12bd161f713a88:0">Python’s </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/compound_stmts.html#with" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f75febcad8f641efb8a0c614311fe125"><span data-offset-key="f75febcad8f641efb8a0c614311fe125:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">with</code></span></span></a><span data-key="29dc66eb45b848449b4e34f903e9cc4f"><span data-offset-key="29dc66eb45b848449b4e34f903e9cc4f:0"> statement supports the concept of a runtime context defined by a context manager. This is implemented using a pair of methods that allow user-defined classes to define a runtime context that is entered before the statement body is executed and exited when the statement ends:</span><span data-offset-key="29dc66eb45b848449b4e34f903e9cc4f:1">`contextmanager.__enter__`</span><span data-offset-key="29dc66eb45b848449b4e34f903e9cc4f:2">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="86ba0f6eedad4aaf95c0b4c37472648f"><span data-offset-key="86ba0f6eedad4aaf95c0b4c37472648f:0">Enter the runtime context and return either this object or another object related to the runtime context. The value returned by this method is bound to the identifier in the </span><span data-offset-key="86ba0f6eedad4aaf95c0b4c37472648f:1">`as`</span><span data-offset-key="86ba0f6eedad4aaf95c0b4c37472648f:2"> clause of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/compound_stmts.html#with" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0292995f5c2e4829bd0146a143a61d9e"><span data-offset-key="0292995f5c2e4829bd0146a143a61d9e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">with</code></span></span></a><span data-key="862be44b7d39444dab20d7871438c475"><span data-offset-key="862be44b7d39444dab20d7871438c475:0"> statements using this context manager.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ccd6203388c2474bafcf7b8fb6c5fcf1"><span data-offset-key="ccd6203388c2474bafcf7b8fb6c5fcf1:0">An example of a context manager that returns itself is a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-file-object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="aecef4ae1dee4eeb9ef32fe075efad7c"><span data-offset-key="aecef4ae1dee4eeb9ef32fe075efad7c:0">file object</span></span></a><span data-key="7dec8fc3287d49e4adf3d8564a87d294"><span data-offset-key="7dec8fc3287d49e4adf3d8564a87d294:0">. File objects return themselves from \_\_enter\_\_() to allow </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#open" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a182a2d743764d0e944a798a5f374c58"><span data-offset-key="a182a2d743764d0e944a798a5f374c58:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">open()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="39cd326ea07a4d458cb8fb2e96606fec"><span data-offset-key="39cd326ea07a4d458cb8fb2e96606fec:0"> to be used as the context expression in a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/compound_stmts.html#with" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f73e3e4c1aa74665ba48dc14dda2deb5"><span data-offset-key="f73e3e4c1aa74665ba48dc14dda2deb5:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">with</code></span></span></a><span data-key="5dd6584745f14cfe8baf541dc7ca403b"><span data-offset-key="5dd6584745f14cfe8baf541dc7ca403b:0"> statement.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="46fa9bd2128a411f8737259e700a70fe"><span data-offset-key="46fa9bd2128a411f8737259e700a70fe:0">An example of a context manager that returns a related object is the one returned by </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/decimal.html#decimal.localcontext" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7f2604431db7491fa44c27e5176e3512"><span data-offset-key="7f2604431db7491fa44c27e5176e3512:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">decimal.localcontext()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="8d46bcbd22174d0787bdfd7a4681540f"><span data-offset-key="8d46bcbd22174d0787bdfd7a4681540f:0">. These managers set the active decimal context to a copy of the original decimal context and then return the copy. This allows changes to be made to the current decimal context in the body of the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/compound_stmts.html#with" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e9de60dc3aed4247a2910642bb23ecf9"><span data-offset-key="e9de60dc3aed4247a2910642bb23ecf9:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">with</code></span></span></a><span data-key="69c727cfcba94e5895badd99f278a5f8"><span data-offset-key="69c727cfcba94e5895badd99f278a5f8:0"> statement without affecting code outside the </span><span data-offset-key="69c727cfcba94e5895badd99f278a5f8:1">`with`</span><span data-offset-key="69c727cfcba94e5895badd99f278a5f8:2"> statement.</span><span data-offset-key="69c727cfcba94e5895badd99f278a5f8:3">`contextmanager.__exit__`</span><span data-offset-key="69c727cfcba94e5895badd99f278a5f8:4">(</span><span data-offset-key="69c727cfcba94e5895badd99f278a5f8:5">*exc\_type*</span><span data-offset-key="69c727cfcba94e5895badd99f278a5f8:6">, </span><span data-offset-key="69c727cfcba94e5895badd99f278a5f8:7">*exc\_val*</span><span data-offset-key="69c727cfcba94e5895badd99f278a5f8:8">, </span><span data-offset-key="69c727cfcba94e5895badd99f278a5f8:9">*exc\_tb*</span><span data-offset-key="69c727cfcba94e5895badd99f278a5f8:10">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b236b1e2c1d7487b84e61539036bc93b"><span data-offset-key="b236b1e2c1d7487b84e61539036bc93b:0">Exit the runtime context and return a Boolean flag indicating if any exception that occurred should be suppressed. If an exception occurred while executing the body of the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/compound_stmts.html#with" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9013b83f2a694c08a327d96d96e8bfa2"><span data-offset-key="9013b83f2a694c08a327d96d96e8bfa2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">with</code></span></span></a><span data-key="1d1464db80e041b198be0950f9bbf3f0"><span data-offset-key="1d1464db80e041b198be0950f9bbf3f0:0"> statement, the arguments contain the exception type, value and traceback information. Otherwise, all three arguments are </span><span data-offset-key="1d1464db80e041b198be0950f9bbf3f0:1">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="1d1464db80e041b198be0950f9bbf3f0:2">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="18532509f9d24721829d593283eec902"><span data-offset-key="18532509f9d24721829d593283eec902:0">Returning a true value from this method will cause the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/compound_stmts.html#with" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0e4e7f872de34ef39bffcbd6d7106dd2"><span data-offset-key="0e4e7f872de34ef39bffcbd6d7106dd2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">with</code></span></span></a><span data-key="9357c76b32b54b6ebfca11c4b1c16369"><span data-offset-key="9357c76b32b54b6ebfca11c4b1c16369:0"> statement to suppress the exception and continue execution with the statement immediately following the </span><span data-offset-key="9357c76b32b54b6ebfca11c4b1c16369:1">`with`</span><span data-offset-key="9357c76b32b54b6ebfca11c4b1c16369:2"> statement. Otherwise the exception continues propagating after this method has finished executing. Exceptions that occur during execution of this method will replace any exception that occurred in the body of the </span><span data-offset-key="9357c76b32b54b6ebfca11c4b1c16369:3">`with`</span><span data-offset-key="9357c76b32b54b6ebfca11c4b1c16369:4"> statement.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="723222d3ef4c47ddbb399330667fc3d0"><span data-offset-key="723222d3ef4c47ddbb399330667fc3d0:0">The exception passed in should never be reraised explicitly - instead, this method should return a false value to indicate that the method completed successfully and does not want to suppress the raised exception. This allows context management code to easily detect whether or not an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#contextmanager.__exit__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="608206cea0054d0bbb82cbbc1b4d6ca7"><span data-offset-key="608206cea0054d0bbb82cbbc1b4d6ca7:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__exit__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="276b3a4e4f2b4d14abd67c1306f82f89"><span data-offset-key="276b3a4e4f2b4d14abd67c1306f82f89:0"> method has actually failed.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ab7a76b4dbc84a83906e0509e669ffb1"><span data-offset-key="ab7a76b4dbc84a83906e0509e669ffb1:0">Python defines several context managers to support easy thread synchronisation, prompt closure of files or other objects, and simpler manipulation of the active decimal arithmetic context. The specific types are not treated specially beyond their implementation of the context management protocol. See the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/contextlib.html#module-contextlib" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8f05b152fd4c4635a19dc0ec76ecca3c"><span data-offset-key="8f05b152fd4c4635a19dc0ec76ecca3c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">contextlib</code></span></span></a><span data-key="86b0b6c6fc094a9cbe13e7ed6efb4c20"><span data-offset-key="86b0b6c6fc094a9cbe13e7ed6efb4c20:0"> module for some examples.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="71382925fa874727aabdbe027d57f430"><span data-offset-key="71382925fa874727aabdbe027d57f430:0">Python’s </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-generator" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="24c7122c84c64f2297345d1dd4ab0e2d"><span data-offset-key="24c7122c84c64f2297345d1dd4ab0e2d:0">generator</span></span></a><span data-key="230adca4d270431c914764636e482bed"><span data-offset-key="230adca4d270431c914764636e482bed:0">s and the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/contextlib.html#contextlib.contextmanager" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="61c0c06698bc4bb8b58911004b9fb037"><span data-offset-key="61c0c06698bc4bb8b58911004b9fb037:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">contextlib.contextmanager</code></span></span></a><span data-key="01228d27f2ff44838aeec6c1c431c664"><span data-offset-key="01228d27f2ff44838aeec6c1c431c664:0"> decorator provide a convenient way to implement these protocols. If a generator function is decorated with the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/contextlib.html#contextlib.contextmanager" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="804f0311221b4484b9d478cbfdfc3728"><span data-offset-key="804f0311221b4484b9d478cbfdfc3728:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">contextlib.contextmanager</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ea1ba7147f6a45efac5a1a8a345a3e81"><span data-offset-key="ea1ba7147f6a45efac5a1a8a345a3e81:0"> decorator, it will return a context manager implementing the necessary </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__enter__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a8154d2d16cc4dab84b25e6f5ea1eed0"><span data-offset-key="a8154d2d16cc4dab84b25e6f5ea1eed0:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__enter__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="40abf8956d0f421f8423021e75288e67"><span data-offset-key="40abf8956d0f421f8423021e75288e67:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__exit__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="832901e450144a889622c928d9296306"><span data-offset-key="832901e450144a889622c928d9296306:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__exit__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="32aa821ee7c6448ca22af7d5afd64ef4"><span data-offset-key="32aa821ee7c6448ca22af7d5afd64ef4:0"> methods, rather than the iterator produced by an undecorated generator function.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="915f7eb67b244e76ab80d536e49d8ecd"><span data-offset-key="915f7eb67b244e76ab80d536e49d8ecd:0">Note that there is no specific slot for any of these methods in the type structure for Python objects in the Python/C API. Extension types wanting to define these methods must provide them as a normal Python accessible method. Compared to the overhead of setting up the runtime context, the overhead of a single class dictionary lookup is negligible.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH600-23f228db--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="41868b63a1834f459a26aeb161b31aa2"><span data-offset-key="41868b63a1834f459a26aeb161b31aa2:0">Generic Alias Type</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e05ffedddda745d2a43a51b3738cf2e5"><span data-offset-key="e05ffedddda745d2a43a51b3738cf2e5:0">`GenericAlias`</span><span data-offset-key="e05ffedddda745d2a43a51b3738cf2e5:1"> objects are created by subscripting a class (usually a container), such as </span><span data-offset-key="e05ffedddda745d2a43a51b3738cf2e5:2">`list[int]`</span><span data-offset-key="e05ffedddda745d2a43a51b3738cf2e5:3">. They are intended primarily for </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-annotation" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="65f20f5f0a8948f2856fd96e1388f5b9"><span data-offset-key="65f20f5f0a8948f2856fd96e1388f5b9:0">type annotations</span></span></a><span data-key="f8bdaeab4c9e47c89388437d7c41a392"><span data-offset-key="f8bdaeab4c9e47c89388437d7c41a392:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="408af1bb624247078c1a33ba9398ac6f"><span data-offset-key="408af1bb624247078c1a33ba9398ac6f:0">Usually, the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/expressions.html#subscriptions" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f109043bef4849f3a0b95a83b30de83c"><span data-offset-key="f109043bef4849f3a0b95a83b30de83c:0">subscription</span></span></a><span data-key="3ef109154f024b08b6fbbd69aa5d40de"><span data-offset-key="3ef109154f024b08b6fbbd69aa5d40de:0"> of container objects calls the method </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__getitem__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6c8e68f10b5b47e09ddda75d90c67f8e"><span data-offset-key="6c8e68f10b5b47e09ddda75d90c67f8e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__getitem__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="64a2f9a5020342f3b3882e110f990546"><span data-offset-key="64a2f9a5020342f3b3882e110f990546:0"> of the object. However, the subscription of some containers’ classes may call the classmethod </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__class_getitem__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4cde372f50304e97a1dde8b687f53824"><span data-offset-key="4cde372f50304e97a1dde8b687f53824:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__class_getitem__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ffb30bcb7dab47bfaa116c5e8005fbad"><span data-offset-key="ffb30bcb7dab47bfaa116c5e8005fbad:0"> of the class instead. The classmethod </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__class_getitem__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9536cd9e29d7485f87d366566811f834"><span data-offset-key="9536cd9e29d7485f87d366566811f834:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__class_getitem__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="88f14907d0ae4d90a9a4ed754a9f5350"><span data-offset-key="88f14907d0ae4d90a9a4ed754a9f5350:0"> should return a </span><span data-offset-key="88f14907d0ae4d90a9a4ed754a9f5350:1">`GenericAlias`</span><span data-offset-key="88f14907d0ae4d90a9a4ed754a9f5350:2"> object.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="de8c1e378ed64311bcbdf0107d901c43"><span data-offset-key="de8c1e378ed64311bcbdf0107d901c43:0">Note </span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="72774803af6d42fc919ae5c60711b750"><span data-offset-key="72774803af6d42fc919ae5c60711b750:0">If the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__getitem__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7a54c76e8f754f6782be361f8142fc8b"><span data-offset-key="7a54c76e8f754f6782be361f8142fc8b:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__getitem__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="54a3e808956e484abe105093272f1b65"><span data-offset-key="54a3e808956e484abe105093272f1b65:0"> of the class’ metaclass is present, it will take precedence over the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__class_getitem__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="61c012c4bb4d4f158846a2d78e4a3326"><span data-offset-key="61c012c4bb4d4f158846a2d78e4a3326:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__class_getitem__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="357a2ca0c49840139473445ea1a3ee27"><span data-offset-key="357a2ca0c49840139473445ea1a3ee27:0"> defined in the class (see </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0560" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b5e5114a5c8445fa8ef20530787830f9"><span data-offset-key="b5e5114a5c8445fa8ef20530787830f9:0"><strong>PEP 560</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="8eb988c2aa7e454a9857ef48973a472e"><span data-offset-key="8eb988c2aa7e454a9857ef48973a472e:0"> for more details).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="427ca6e76fa04001b2b2f1e707b06c22"><span data-offset-key="427ca6e76fa04001b2b2f1e707b06c22:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="427ca6e76fa04001b2b2f1e707b06c22:1">`GenericAlias`</span><span data-offset-key="427ca6e76fa04001b2b2f1e707b06c22:2"> object acts as a proxy for </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-generic-type" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="db87032ed10f40c7aa050433ce28df55"><span data-offset-key="db87032ed10f40c7aa050433ce28df55:0">generic types</span></span></a><span data-key="1f7fec4c573e4754a988b6f9944f05c0"><span data-offset-key="1f7fec4c573e4754a988b6f9944f05c0:0">, implementing </span><span data-offset-key="1f7fec4c573e4754a988b6f9944f05c0:1">*parameterized generics*</span><span data-offset-key="1f7fec4c573e4754a988b6f9944f05c0:2"> - a specific instance of a generic which provides the types for container elements.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="025f28dde94d4bc9a50cf961818bd8e7"><span data-offset-key="025f28dde94d4bc9a50cf961818bd8e7:0">The user-exposed type for the </span><span data-offset-key="025f28dde94d4bc9a50cf961818bd8e7:1">`GenericAlias`</span><span data-offset-key="025f28dde94d4bc9a50cf961818bd8e7:2"> object can be accessed from </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/types.html#types.GenericAlias" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a063c5c5886843d7a4c10c17823cdac1"><span data-offset-key="a063c5c5886843d7a4c10c17823cdac1:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">types.GenericAlias</code></span></span></a><span data-key="bb68c5d5fae34311a42470a1eafc9306"><span data-offset-key="bb68c5d5fae34311a42470a1eafc9306:0"> and used for </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#isinstance" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="26518dc2c2a5453b819a5e193e008e82"><span data-offset-key="26518dc2c2a5453b819a5e193e008e82:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">isinstance()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="15c88c9322a04641af4aeafa56686436"><span data-offset-key="15c88c9322a04641af4aeafa56686436:0"> checks. It can also be used to create </span><span data-offset-key="15c88c9322a04641af4aeafa56686436:1">`GenericAlias`</span><span data-offset-key="15c88c9322a04641af4aeafa56686436:2"> objects directly.</span><span data-offset-key="15c88c9322a04641af4aeafa56686436:3">`T[X, Y, ...]`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fc6c0b4ecd714b849f6db11954de5756"><span data-offset-key="fc6c0b4ecd714b849f6db11954de5756:0">Creates a </span><span data-offset-key="fc6c0b4ecd714b849f6db11954de5756:1">`GenericAlias`</span><span data-offset-key="fc6c0b4ecd714b849f6db11954de5756:2"> representing a type </span><span data-offset-key="fc6c0b4ecd714b849f6db11954de5756:3">`T`</span><span data-offset-key="fc6c0b4ecd714b849f6db11954de5756:4"> containing elements of types </span><span data-offset-key="fc6c0b4ecd714b849f6db11954de5756:5">*X*</span><span data-offset-key="fc6c0b4ecd714b849f6db11954de5756:6">, </span><span data-offset-key="fc6c0b4ecd714b849f6db11954de5756:7">*Y*</span><span data-offset-key="fc6c0b4ecd714b849f6db11954de5756:8">, and more depending on the </span><span data-offset-key="fc6c0b4ecd714b849f6db11954de5756:9">`T`</span><span data-offset-key="fc6c0b4ecd714b849f6db11954de5756:10"> used. For example, a function expecting a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#list" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e6c495b36a514b7f873cd63df072e9f4"><span data-offset-key="e6c495b36a514b7f873cd63df072e9f4:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">list</code></span></span></a><span data-key="7f37833a657a4ded8b6f3d1aaeaf8cba"><span data-offset-key="7f37833a657a4ded8b6f3d1aaeaf8cba:0"> containing </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#float" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="242a20bc92e5403cb2d404d8f70558b2"><span data-offset-key="242a20bc92e5403cb2d404d8f70558b2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">float</code></span></span></a><span data-key="50360aae7fb04c5386efed81baef92a0"><span data-offset-key="50360aae7fb04c5386efed81baef92a0:0"> elements:</span></span></span>

    def average(values: list[float]) -> float:    return sum(values) / len(values)

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b5390228ded44425a142a0d0fb3846f2"><span data-offset-key="b5390228ded44425a142a0d0fb3846f2:0">Another example for </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-mapping" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c4806fc3b4cb4da48635c936f09b68cf"><span data-offset-key="c4806fc3b4cb4da48635c936f09b68cf:0">mapping</span></span></a><span data-key="fe5ca7d1d15e410da421df706fbeb416"><span data-offset-key="fe5ca7d1d15e410da421df706fbeb416:0"> objects, using a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#dict" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="857d899d028a4af382f7eeeb60efb4e2"><span data-offset-key="857d899d028a4af382f7eeeb60efb4e2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">dict</code></span></span></a><span data-key="3edb480b58f8475e84dd86857f6bf535"><span data-offset-key="3edb480b58f8475e84dd86857f6bf535:0">, which is a generic type expecting two type parameters representing the key type and the value type. In this example, the function expects a </span><span data-offset-key="3edb480b58f8475e84dd86857f6bf535:1">`dict`</span><span data-offset-key="3edb480b58f8475e84dd86857f6bf535:2"> with keys of type </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c01b13b4b5cd477586381ace96c0d8aa"><span data-offset-key="c01b13b4b5cd477586381ace96c0d8aa:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str</code></span></span></a><span data-key="02ff5ea9a3314c7e9b7480c6b05909dd"><span data-offset-key="02ff5ea9a3314c7e9b7480c6b05909dd:0"> and values of type </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b602aa12a1c945f59208550c08ee5369"><span data-offset-key="b602aa12a1c945f59208550c08ee5369:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">int</code></span></span></a><span data-key="165d48e2c42e4fe2b8fa6dbee6493db0"><span data-offset-key="165d48e2c42e4fe2b8fa6dbee6493db0:0">:</span></span></span>

    def send_post_request(url: str, body: dict[str, int]) -> None:    ...

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f7a3a67e00ce450888330c9e3564a1f3"><span data-offset-key="f7a3a67e00ce450888330c9e3564a1f3:0">The builtin functions </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#isinstance" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="475fe217c58e437b8d6d15ebdb383aed"><span data-offset-key="475fe217c58e437b8d6d15ebdb383aed:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">isinstance()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="c0166d5bceb8451b87c28224e7f83c94"><span data-offset-key="c0166d5bceb8451b87c28224e7f83c94:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#issubclass" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e77f98b3e56944919cc3bdb36cb92f22"><span data-offset-key="e77f98b3e56944919cc3bdb36cb92f22:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">issubclass()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="53ad8b398a6f4b2db5d713da7ed05264"><span data-offset-key="53ad8b398a6f4b2db5d713da7ed05264:0"> do not accept </span><span data-offset-key="53ad8b398a6f4b2db5d713da7ed05264:1">`GenericAlias`</span><span data-offset-key="53ad8b398a6f4b2db5d713da7ed05264:2"> types for their second argument:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> isinstance([1, 2], list[str])Traceback (most recent call last):  File "<stdin>", line 1, in <module>TypeError: isinstance() argument 2 cannot be a parameterized generic

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="abed56efd8f3405685892e9c709a91f9"><span data-offset-key="abed56efd8f3405685892e9c709a91f9:0">The Python runtime does not enforce </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-annotation" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bf23662432cc417f97dcbd7ef9ff4a6b"><span data-offset-key="bf23662432cc417f97dcbd7ef9ff4a6b:0">type annotations</span></span></a><span data-key="9b5e14e788ff4f649848b44ebf2e3417"><span data-offset-key="9b5e14e788ff4f649848b44ebf2e3417:0">. This extends to generic types and their type parameters. When creating an object from a </span><span data-offset-key="9b5e14e788ff4f649848b44ebf2e3417:1">`GenericAlias`</span><span data-offset-key="9b5e14e788ff4f649848b44ebf2e3417:2">, container elements are not checked against their type. For example, the following code is discouraged, but will run without errors:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> t = list[str]>>> t([1, 2, 3])[1, 2, 3]

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a847347f51a44459a31521b63a6a3a92"><span data-offset-key="a847347f51a44459a31521b63a6a3a92:0">Furthermore, parameterized generics erase type parameters during object creation:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> t = list[str]>>> type(t)<class 'types.GenericAlias'>​>>> l = t()>>> type(l)<class 'list'>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="34d5e02fe80547598be818f90e844405"><span data-offset-key="34d5e02fe80547598be818f90e844405:0">Calling </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#repr" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6b1c33f0042a47d3a0befd4ce821f325"><span data-offset-key="6b1c33f0042a47d3a0befd4ce821f325:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">repr()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="70eb35499b704dc6ade132003c742c5e"><span data-offset-key="70eb35499b704dc6ade132003c742c5e:0"> or </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bef94b78887546fca8e301dd54fe080e"><span data-offset-key="bef94b78887546fca8e301dd54fe080e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="054cf7f61297402989899d7e2393f653"><span data-offset-key="054cf7f61297402989899d7e2393f653:0"> on a generic shows the parameterized type:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> repr(list[int])'list[int]'​>>> str(list[int])'list[int]'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0cf84bd2c287452d95012d1de05ea4b5"><span data-offset-key="0cf84bd2c287452d95012d1de05ea4b5:0">The </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__getitem__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="eafb3d91c1d54b06a7b81022695c6123"><span data-offset-key="eafb3d91c1d54b06a7b81022695c6123:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__getitem__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="e2e75469aeed465eaadb763e3de42c4e"><span data-offset-key="e2e75469aeed465eaadb763e3de42c4e:0"> method of generics will raise an exception to disallow mistakes like </span><span data-offset-key="e2e75469aeed465eaadb763e3de42c4e:1">`dict[str][str]`</span><span data-offset-key="e2e75469aeed465eaadb763e3de42c4e:2">:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> dict[str][str]Traceback (most recent call last):  File "<stdin>", line 1, in <module>TypeError: There are no type variables left in dict[str]

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a4d5afeaa065474899358d0b4d4eb25b"><span data-offset-key="a4d5afeaa065474899358d0b4d4eb25b:0">However, such expressions are valid when </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/typing.html#generics" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9fc3461ad174498da893b83b5476fa7c"><span data-offset-key="9fc3461ad174498da893b83b5476fa7c:0">type variables</span></span></a><span data-key="99b6a53a6d1e46af9abdcd3914d73a6a"><span data-offset-key="99b6a53a6d1e46af9abdcd3914d73a6a:0"> are used. The index must have as many elements as there are type variable items in the </span><span data-offset-key="99b6a53a6d1e46af9abdcd3914d73a6a:1">`GenericAlias`</span><span data-offset-key="99b6a53a6d1e46af9abdcd3914d73a6a:2"> object’s </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#genericalias.__args__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="24a0417576b245f7a24f67db840dab1c"><span data-offset-key="24a0417576b245f7a24f67db840dab1c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__args__</code></span></span></a><span data-key="9df898a663684ca38b1805662bb2562d"><span data-offset-key="9df898a663684ca38b1805662bb2562d:0">.&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> from typing import TypeVar>>> Y = TypeVar('Y')>>> dict[str, Y][int]dict[str, int]
